# Architectural Trellis: Displacement Geometry

## Version 4.16 (Tiered Architecture)

Structural skeleton of a state-dependent vacuum geometry framework, organized around an axiomatic tier structure separating metaphysical commitments, physical constraints, empirical demands, theoretical landscape, specific construction, derived constraints, functions, and contracts.

- v4.0: GUT Box phase transition. The confirmed model passes all eight S-G20 constraints: gauge group, three families, Dark Dimension localization, tadpole, SUSY, proton decay, neutrino mass structure, rank-3 Yukawa. Three structural findings propagated: SF-G1 (BPS-Chirality Tension on factorizable tori in the Dark Dimension), SF-G2 (Divisor Transversality Escape via F-theory horizontal divisors on fibered bases), SF-G3 (Avenue B Parametric Kill of magnetized brane Landau gapping). Constraint annotations updated for K8, K10, K11, K12, K14 with specific model data. Pati-Salam gauge group invariant across all three surviving bases. - v4.4: Superconductivity audit and QFI scaling crisis. Six-thread investigation of framework applicability to room-temperature superconductivity, low-temperature unconventional superconductivity, and anomalous thermal transport in Kagome metals. All room-temperature superconductivity pathways killed. Kagome ATHE torsion mechanism (F24) killed by ambient-VEV deficit (49 OoM) combined with inability to achieve VEV suppression (CDW QFI is $O(N)$, 69 OoM below K7). Paper 0 extraction reveals load-bearing gap: the $f^2 N^2$ scaling in K1/Appendix 14 is derived from phase-estimation QFI using GHZ states, then identified with $\text{Var}(T_{\mu\nu})$ from the heat kernel coupling without proving equivalence. These are different generators measuring different quantities. For equilibrium gapped states, $\text{Var}(T_{\mu\nu})$ is $O(N)$ by the fluctuation-dissipation theorem. This gap threatens all framework applications requiring VEV suppression, including nuclear pasta (F05, F21, C21a/b/c), LUNA screening (F13, F13.2, C13a-e), geometric wavefunction collapse (F19), and stellar cooling. Ambient-VEV torsion for nuclear pasta yields $\Phi_T \sim 10^{-30}$ rad vs. claimed 0.05 rad (28 OoM deficit). VEV suppression to $v_{\text{eff}} \sim 69\,\text{TeV}$ required, demanding $\mathcal{f}_Q \sim 10^{35}\,\text{GeV}^4$, while nuclear-density matter at $O(N)$ provides $\sim 1\,\text{GeV}^4$ (35 OoM deficit). Dimensional inconsistency in $\mathcal{f}_Q$ identified: Paper 0 defines $\mathcal{f}_Q = 4\,\text{Var}(T_{\mu\nu})$ in $[\text{Mass}]^8$ but the coupling requires $[\mathcal{f}_Q] = [\text{Mass}]^4$. Resolution requires the proper-time integration to absorb four powers of mass; this step is absent from Paper 0. Three candidate resolution paths identified (modular flow escape, generator rederivation, dimensional reconciliation). New critical open problem: OP-0 (QFI Scaling and Generator Identification). Planckian crossover $T^* \sim 38\,\text{K}$ cataloged as structural observation (degenerate with McMillan, fitted prefactor). Chiral hypermomentum selection rule survives as qualitative prediction independent of VEV suppression. 151 K PQP Hg1223 record cataloged. Nine new dead mechanisms. Three new structural observations. One critical open problem. Two new structural lessons. Seven new corpus entries.

- v4.5: OP-0 resolution via modular Hamiltonian formulation and gauge KK species enhancement. The existential scaling gap is resolved through a three-component mechanism: (i) the non-perturbative coupling in Paper 0 Appendix 12 computes $\text{Var}(K_{\text{mod}})$, not $\text{Var}(T_{\mu\nu})$, with the two quantities provably divergent for ODLRO states in finite subregions (Bisognano-Wichmann theorem fails at finite density with SSB); (ii) the capacity of entanglement $C_E = \text{Var}(K_{\text{mod}})$ includes Donnelly-Freidel edge mode contributions scaling as $(L/\epsilon)^2$ (area law, confirmed numerically for both BdG quasiparticle and Goldstone sectors on 2D lattices); (iii) the Pati-Salam gauge KK tower from the $dP_3$ Laplacian provides $\sim 10^2$ to $10^4$ brane-localized vector boson species, each contributing $c = 1/10$ to the central charge sum, lowering $f_{Q,\text{crit}}$ from $10^{32}$ to $10^{28}$ to $10^{30}$. The compound budget (density-wave spectral integral $\sim 10^{13}$ to $10^{16}$, edge mode area scaling $\sim 10^{13}$, total $\sim 10^{27}$ to $10^{29}$) meets or exceeds the lowered threshold when $\sim 100$ gauge KK modes are present below the Species Scale. OP-0 status changes from EXISTENTIAL to RESOLVED (conditional on gauge KK mode count from FTheoryTools computation). Path A permanently dead (heat kernel $a_4$ is UV-local, insensitive to ODLRO). Equilibrium condensed-matter applications without external driving remain dead (FDT binds $\text{Var}(T_{\mu\nu})$ to $O(N)$). Nuclear pasta survival depends on the modular Hamiltonian formulation being adopted as the physical coupling. PS spectrum nearly cancels SM trace anomaly ($|\Sigma_{\text{total}}| = 0.008$ for SM+PS matter alone), making the gauge KK tower the decisive species contribution. The VEV suppression mechanism operates as a pole: $P_{\text{torsion}} \sim 1/(1 - f_Q/f_{Q,\text{crit}})$, with no effect far from the critical value and divergent effect near it. Two new structural findings (SF-Q1, SF-Q2). Three new structural lessons. Eight new dead mechanisms. Eight new corpus entries.

- v4.6: Coupling uniqueness refinement via Gemini adversarial audit. The $\gamma(\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B)\mathcal{f}_Q$ coupling is confirmed as the unique operator capable of driving macroscopic VEV suppression, with the uniqueness now characterized as thermodynamic (scaling discrimination between $O(N)$ and $O(N^2)$ regimes) rather than Lagrangian (representation-theoretic). Three competing SO(1,4)-scalar, parity-even, dimension-6 operators identified at one loop from the $a_4$ Seeley-DeWitt coefficient ($\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B T^\mu{}_\mu$, $\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B C_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}C^{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$, $\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B \text{Tr}(F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu})$); all three scale extensively as $O(N)$ and remain gravitationally suppressed, incapable of breaching the species-scale activation threshold. The Lagrangian uniqueness claim is killed (Class Block) and moved to the exclusion reservoir. K7 activation threshold annotated with explicit $O(N)$ vs. $O(N^2)$ scaling discrimination mechanism. K4 audit confirmation: the $\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B \text{Tr}(F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu})$ operator is mandatory (conformal trace anomaly, K11 exhaust channel) and gravitationally suppressed ($y^4/(16\pi^2) \sim 10^{-67}$). The formal definition of $\mathcal{f}_Q$ is permanently bound to Formulation B (modular Hamiltonian, Araki relative entropy under Tomita-Takesaki modular flow). Formulation A (heat kernel coincidence limit) serves as the perturbative entry point, recovering Formulation B in the Bisognano-Wichmann limit. Sub-element Shore. One new exclusion reservoir entry. One new corpus entry.

- v4.7: Dimensional resolution of the gamma coupling. The variance coupling coefficient $\gamma(\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B)\mathcal{f}_Q$ is derived from first principles as $\gamma = c_{\text{KK}}/(128\pi^2\Lambda_s^2)$, replacing the inherited $\gamma \sim 1/(16\pi^2 M_{\text{Pl}}^2)$ assumption that carried forward through v4.4 through v4.6. The derivation proceeds via four steps: (1) single-species $a_4$ Seeley-DeWitt coefficient at $1/M_{\text{Pl}}^2$ strength, (2) additive spectral-trace sum over $N_{\text{species}} = (M_{\text{Pl}}/\Lambda_s)^2$ Kaluza-Klein graviton modes, (3) classical Einstein equation reduction of Ricci-squared to stress-energy variance, (4) Dvali-Gomez species identity collapsing $M_{\text{Pl}}^2$ to $\Lambda_s^2$ in the final coefficient. The key structural point: the KK heat kernel sum is additive over eigenvalue contributions (spectral trace), coherent over amplitudes only for propagators and scattering processes. Sturm-Liouville orthogonality arguments that invoke cancellation apply to the wrong mathematical category for this observable. The pole condition becomes $F_{Q,\text{crit}} = 16\pi^2 m_\rho^2 \Lambda_s^2/c_{\text{KK}} \sim 10^{12}$ to $10^{13}\,\text{GeV}^4$, superseding the prior $10^{32}\,\text{GeV}^4$ estimate. The compound matter budget of $10^{27}$ to $10^{29}\,\text{GeV}^4$ exceeds the corrected threshold by 14 to 17 orders of magnitude. OP-0 resolves unconditionally. The v4.5 gauge KK species lowering mechanism moves to the exclusion reservoir as structurally incorrect (right survival outcome reached via wrong dimensional analysis). Gauge KK mode count from FTheoryTools computation remains relevant for precision GUT spectrum work and retains its role in K8, K10, K11, but no longer gates OP-0. K7 rewritten with explicit derivation. New open problem OP-CK tracks computation of the $c_{\text{KK}}$ prefactor for the full MacDowell-Mansouri Karch-Randall spin-2 system with Faddeev-Popov ghost subtractions. Three new linter rules (LINT-11, LINT-12, LINT-13). Adjudication Document added to corpus documenting the heat kernel spectral trace argument and the resolution of two contradictory prior Gemini reports. Paper 0 v9 to v10 update module generated. One new structural finding (SF-D0, species-enhanced one-loop coefficients in brane heat kernels). Two new structural lessons (SL-12, SL-13). One exclusion reservoir entry (ER-Q-01). Five new corpus entries. Terminology migration: scaffold to trellis across the living document system.

- v4.8: Addazi-Meluccio integration shore (SF-DG-009). Three Gemini Deep Research reports (CC Derivation Run 1, CC Derivation Run 2, Radiative Stability of AM Potential at MeV Radion) cataloged. Four foundational pre-geometric gravity papers integrated into corpus: Addazi-Meluccio (arXiv:2602.16840), Meluccio (arXiv:2505.02925), Addazi-Capozziello-Marciano-Meluccio (arXiv:2409.02200, CQG 2025), Addazi-Capozziello-Marciano-Meluccio (arXiv:2505.01272, PRD 2025). Two distinct findings. First, the framework's original $\gamma(z_0)$ species-enhanced stabilization mechanism for the Karch-Randall brane radial position is killed (CC Run 1 Q2, independently confirmed by Run 2 Q2 through a different algebraic path). The $(L/z_0)^4$ measure factor combined with $\gamma(z_0) \propto z_0^2$ yields $V_{\mathrm{eff}}^{\mathrm{phys}} \propto z_0^{-2}$ after $\phi$-extremization; the $z_0$-gradient is strictly negative for physical states and the brane runs to the IR horizon. The $\gamma$-correction lifts the Karch-Randall degeneracy into runaway, not stability. Second, the MM intrinsic $\Lambda \sim M_P^4$ catastrophe is resolved through adoption of the Addazi-Meluccio topological quantization mechanism. The MM SSB action generates a Gauss-Bonnet term whose coupling acts as a gravitational $\theta$-angle; periodicity forces $\Lambda$ into the discrete tower $\Lambda^{(k)} = 3cM_P^2/[32(-\theta^{(0)} + 2\pi k)]$ with $c = 128\pi^2$. The observed hierarchy $M_P^2/\Lambda \sim 10^{120}$ corresponds to $k \sim S_{\mathrm{dS}}$. Inter-sector tunneling is suppressed by $e^{-S_{\mathrm{dS}}}$. Adoption of the mechanism requires Tier 4 reformulation of the SSB potential from sombrero $V = \lambda(\phi^A\phi_A - v_0^2)^2$ to the periodic AM form $V = Y_{\mathrm{SSB}} |J|[1 - \cos(c Y_{\mathrm{MM}}(|\phi| - v))]^p$, with $v \sim 10^{139}$ GeV trans-Planckian under standard EFT scaling and $M_P^2 = 32 Y_{\mathrm{MM}} v m^2$ generated on the brane. Radiative stability at MeV radion mass confirmed by Gemini Radiative Stability Report: the trans-Planckian VEV provides 16 orders of magnitude of kinematic dominance (barrier height $\sim 10^{32}$ GeV$^4$ vs. aperiodic CW slope $\sim 10^{-3}$ GeV$^3$), and the non-renormalization theorem for periodic operators gives exact one-loop protection of $Y_{\mathrm{SSB}}$. Mass window $\mu_\rho \in [1\,\mathrm{meV}, 100\,\mathrm{GeV}]$ safe. New Tier 3 axiom T3.6 (pre-geometric topological quantization of $\Lambda$) added. New constraint K18 (trans-Planckian VEV suppresses aperiodic tilts via geometric suppression) added. New function F-CC (cosmological constant quantization and initial sector selection) added. F20 substantially revised to incorporate $\Lambda^{(k)}$ sector selection during SSB; F12 initial condition reformulated as intra-sector thawing from $\Lambda^{(k)}_{\mathrm{initial}}$. Tier 4 §4.4 fully rewritten to the periodic AM potential. OP-CC (MM intrinsic $\Lambda$ counterterm requirement) discharged. S-CC-001 reformulated (decoupled from $\Lambda$ derivation, now restricted to brane radial stabilization). Three new open problems opened: S-CC-002 (instanton-generated $z_0$ stabilization), S-CC-004 (holographic Casimir backreaction), S-CC-005 (bulk CS level / boundary topological sector identification). Integration structurally non-disruptive to existing phenomenology: the two-regime behavior (vacuum-stable, ODLRO-erased) that F13.2 and F19 require becomes a derived consequence of the AM periodic potential plus the existing $\gamma F_Q$ coupling, rather than two separate axioms. - v4.9: Paper -1 §VI correction shore (SF-DG-009.1). Three independent AI-generated technical reports cataloged: Gemini DR on §VI rewrite route (kills §VI D, proposes principal symbol pivot), DeepSeek cross-exam (independently verifies bracket computation, reproduces leading term with matching signs), ChatGPT Track A construction (formalizes the No-Go Lemma for local algebraic redefinitions). Paper -1 §VI D vanishing claim retracted: the 30×30 primary-primary block $\{Z^i_{AB}, Z^j_{CD}\}$ is generically nonzero in the broken phase, driven by $v$ and spatial curvature through the BF-type pre-symplectic structure $\Phi^j_{CD} = 2\alpha\,\epsilon_{CDEFG}\,\epsilon^{0jkl} F^{EF}_{kl}\,\phi^G$. The full 44×44 Dirac matrix is therefore a first-order pseudo-differential operator, not an ultra-local pointwise finite matrix. No-Go Lemma (ChatGPT construction): no invertible local algebraic constraint redefinition $\widetilde{Z} = m(x)\,Z$ can absorb the 30×30 derivative block; local conjugation preserves the principal symbol order, and cancellation would require $m$ to annihilate the principal coefficient $\mathcal{C}^k \neq 0$. Structural origin of the obstruction (DeepSeek identification): the derivative index pattern $\epsilon^{0ikl}\partial_k$ is a spatial curl operator whose inverse on $\mathbb{R}^3$ is the non-local Biot-Savart kernel. Consequently, any formally successful canonical transformation relocates the non-locality into the definition of $K$ rather than eliminating it. Paper -1 rewrite pivots to the principal-symbol route: the 44×44 is analyzed as a pseudo-differential operator with Douglis-Nirenberg mixed-order structure, and non-degeneracy is established through invertibility of the principal symbol $\sigma(\Delta)(\xi) \neq 0$ for $\xi \neq 0$ rather than through pointwise determinant. The clean factorization $\det \sigma(\tilde{\Delta}) \propto (\det e)^k (v+\rho)^m \lambda^n \times (\xi\text{-dependent piece})$ is conjectured and remains to be verified by explicit CAS computation (S-MM-002). Ghost-freedom (Paper -1 §VIII) preserved through symbol-level positivity argument: classification of constraints as first-class or second-class is independent of ultra-local vs. differential character of the Dirac matrix, so the topological protection of the Hamiltonian constraint inside the SO(1,4) Gauss algebra survives unchanged. §IX fully reframed: out, "ultra-local pointwise finite matrix"; in, "first-order pseudo-differential operator with non-local Dirac brackets on reduced phase space via Green's function inversion." Narrative speculation about holographic naturalness and topological UV phase transitions stripped from the rewrite; these are not supported by cited literature and are downgraded to unsourced editorial framing. NS program impact: no change to the large-data kill (Bounding Box scope reduction remains killed); small-data regime derivation chain unchanged; new low-priority sorry S-NS-018 added to verify that non-local Dirac brackets integrate out for macroscopic boundary fluid composite observables. Eight new corpus entries (three AI technical reports plus associated source attachments). Three new ER entries (ER-MM-001, ER-MM-002, ER-MM-003). Two new sorry tags (S-MM-002, S-MM-003). One discharged sorry (S-MM-001, killed). Two new linter rules (LINT-18, LINT-19). Paper -1 v3 patch v2 (in preparation) supersedes patch v1.

- v4.10: Higgs sector kinetic-term resolution shore (SF-DG-009.2). Investigation triggered by the rank-counting consequences of the v4.9 §VI principal-symbol pivot: when the 30×30 primary-primary block is rank-deficient at leading order (curl kernel plus broken-sector $\epsilon$-contraction kernel), the strict leading-symbol reading forces DOF $\leq 1$, threatening the framework's conditional 2+1 prediction. Five computational shore cycles run in parallel-and-sequential mode against ChatGPT, with three independent route attempts evaluated. Cycle 1 (S-MIX-001, DBI-completion rescue): DEAD. The bare DBI sector provides a healthy brane-bending kinetic term $Z_\pi = T_3 (L/z_0)^4 > 0$, but no $\pi\chi$ tree-level mixing arises from the explicit action; $\epsilon$-contractions and induced-metric matching produce only $\chi^2$, $\pi\chi^2$, $\pi^2\chi^2$, never $\pi\chi$. Result: $m_{\text{mix}}^2 = 0$, $\sin(\theta) = 0$, decoupled brane scalar. Cycle 2 (S-MIX-002, Candidate enumeration): five candidate sources for $Z_\chi$ identified (Goldstone-eating from gauge sector, AM volume form $|J|$, Stelle-West nonlinear realization, Wise/Cartan geometry, add-by-hand). Candidates A (Goldstone-eating via $F^{a4}$) and B ($|J|$ derivative structure) killed by explicit $\epsilon$-index gymnastics: every $(\partial\chi)$ insertion in $F^{a4}$ is annihilated by $\epsilon_{abcd4}$ after broken-vacuum projection (a single index-4 already saturated by $\phi^E = v\delta^E_4$), and the four-derivative $|J|$ structure forces all derivative slots into Lorentz-broken indices, eliminating any $(\partial\chi)^2$ combination. Cycle 3 (S-MIX-003, Path B-B Einstein-Cartan torsion elimination): DEAD. Explicit Levi-Civita contraction in the broken phase yields $\beta'\cdot a_1 = -(4/3)\alpha m^2/(v+\rho)$ for the $K^2$ coupling to $e^2$, failing the criterion $\beta'\cdot a_1 > 2/3$ by both sign and field dependence. Computation cross-checked two ways (direct wedge contraction vs. $T_{\text{vec}}^2$ normalization), result robust. The torsion-elimination route gives a Palatini-style ghost kinetic term, not the displayed healthy sign. Cycle 4 (S-MIX-004, Weyl rescaling to Einstein frame): HEALTHY. Standard Jordan-to-Einstein conformal rescaling $g_{\mu\nu} = F^{-1}(\rho)\,\hat{g}_{\mu\nu}$ on the bare MM non-minimal coupling $F(\rho) R(g)$ produces the Einstein-frame action $\hat{S} = \int\sqrt{-\hat{g}}\,[\hat{R} - (3/2)(F'/F)^2\,\hat{g}^{\mu\nu}\partial_\mu\rho\,\partial_\nu\rho + \dots]$, with healthy sign in mostly-plus signature. For $F = 4\alpha m^2(v+\rho)$ (linear, as the bare MM expansion gives), the kinetic coefficient is $-(3/2)/(v+\rho)^2 < 0$ (healthy), and the canonical scalar is logarithmic in the Higgs norm: $\psi = \sqrt{3}\,\ln((v+\rho)/v)$. Cycle 5 (literature reconnaissance): Langenscheidt 2019 thesis (arXiv:1907.10440), "Interactions in MacDowell-Mansouri Gravitation," identifies the structural origin of the kinetic-term puzzle: scalar kinetic terms in MMSW gravity require AUXILIARY FIELDS to maintain SO(1,4) covariance. The naive $(D\phi)^\dagger(D\phi)$ construction produces an antisymmetric $\mu\nu$ structure that vanishes as a Klein-Gordon kinetic term (thesis §4.2). The principled resolution is a first-order auxiliary action $S_{\text{aux}} = (1/3!\rho)\int_M \epsilon_{ABCDE}\,\phi^A\,D\phi^B \wedge D\tau^C \wedge D\tau^D \wedge D\tau^E$ with the radial mode $\phi^5$ propagating and the four Lorentz components $\phi^a$ auxiliary, eliminated via algebraic equations of motion to give a Klein-Gordon equation $(\Box + 4/\rho^2)\phi^5 = 0$. Three convergent results across Cycles 4 and 5 plus standard Jordan-Brans-Dicke scalar-tensor theory: (i) bare MM is Jordan-frame scalar-tensor with linear $F$; (ii) Weyl rescaling produces healthy Einstein-frame kinetic term with derived coefficient; (iii) Langenscheidt auxiliary-field formulation produces the same kinetic term in the original frame, forced by SO(1,4) covariance. Frame-mixing diagnosis: Paper -1 §II E displays $(v+\rho)^2 R - (\partial\rho)^2 + \beta(v+\rho)^2 T^2$, which is incompatible as a single-frame Lagrangian: the $(v+\rho)^2 R$ coefficient is Jordan with quadratic non-minimal coupling, the $-(\partial\rho)^2$ kinetic term is what emerges in Einstein frame, and the bare MM expansion gives $F \propto (v+\rho)$ (linear), not $(v+\rho)^2$. The displayed action is a phenomenological Brans-Dicke parametrization with $\omega_{BD} \approx 1/4$, not a direct expansion. Five status changes: S-MIX-001 closed as DEAD (DBI tree-level rescue dead), S-MIX-002 closed (Candidate E++ adopted: Langenscheidt auxiliary structure), S-MIX-003 closed as DEAD (torsion elimination dead), S-MIX-004 closed (Weyl route confirmed), Path B confirmed alive via Langenscheidt mechanism. Tier 4 §4.3 (Brane Action) updated: Higgs kinetic structure made explicit. Paper -1 §II B incomplete (auxiliary action missing), §II E frame-mixed; Paper -1 v3 patch v3 in preparation specifies edits. Three new exclusion reservoir entries (ER-MIX-001, ER-MIX-002, ER-MIX-003). Two new linter rules (LINT-20, LINT-21). One new structural finding (SF-MIX-001). Four new sorry tags (S-MIX-005 through S-MIX-008). Eleven new corpus entries (five ChatGPT computational reports, Langenscheidt thesis, Path B partial derivation, Path B resolution synthesis, prompt drafts, Stelle-West re-read context). Framework's two graviton plus one radion content preserved. BD-ghost theorem (Paper -1 §VIII) and No-Go Lemma (Paper -1 §VI C) both unaffected (independent of Higgs kinetic structure). $v(F_Q)$ phenomenology window preserved (radion propagates, $F_Q$ coupling intact via $\chi$ identified with the canonical Einstein-frame scalar or with $\phi^5$ in the auxiliary formulation). The matter-sector exclusion record v1 (May 2026) supersedes the v4.7 OP-0 status: the coupling derivation stands, the activation claim dies. OP-0 splits into two components with opposite fates. OP-0-ACTIVATION (the claim that any matter substrate reaches the threshold) closes DEAD: the compound matter budget of $10^{27}$ to $10^{29}$ GeV⁴ rested on super-extensive Var(T), which the exclusion record kills on five independent arguments (FDT volume-law scaling, decoherence of GHZ-class states, dimensional pinning of the conversion, and two failed vehicle searches). CC-1 demoted from foregrounded core to conditional structure: the pole exists in the Lagrangian and no known equilibrium substrate activates it. Matter-sector activation chain (F13, F13.2, F19, F21, F05 and the C13/C21 contract chains) moved to the exclusion reservoir with the existing matter-sector exclusion record as governing document; reactivation conditions inherit from that record's three-gate test. The refresh-duality structural finding (SF-DG-012) establishes that the CC-1 pole admits an exact dual description as registration latency: VEV depletion is queue utilization, radion softening is bandwidth saturation, and $v_{\text{eff}} \to 0$ is queue overflow, identifying pole saturation with local symmetry restoration to the pre-geometric SO(1,4) phase. The duality produces one new conditional contract: C-RD-1, the radion mass equality $m_\rho = \sqrt{c_{\text{KK}}}\, \Lambda_s^2 / (4\pi M_{\text{Pl}}) = 0.44$ to $1.4$ MeV for $c_{\text{KK}} \in [1, 10]$, converting the v4.8 adiabaticity floor ($m_\rho \geq$ MeV) into a two-sided prediction. Falsifier: any independent determination pinning $m_\rho$ outside $[0.3, 3]$ MeV kills the dual reading while leaving CC-1 intact. The queue-capacity formula $\Lambda_s^4 / N_{\text{eff}} = \Lambda_s^6 / M_{\text{Pl}}^2 = 2.1 \times 10^{12}$ GeV⁴ reproduces $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$ at $c_{\text{KK}} \sim 5$, a soft prediction registered against OP-CK. One erratum corrected (E-1, the §4.6 / Appendix C species-scale formula). One new structural finding (SF-DG-012). Two new structural lessons (SL-SUSC-1, SL-RD-1). One new conditional contract (C-RD-1). One new linter rule (LINT-SUSC-1). The framework's surviving skeleton is unaffected: SO(1,4) MacDowell-Mansouri on Karch-Randall braneworld, Paper -1 ghost-freedom chain (S-MM-CR conditionality unchanged), the gamma derivation and SF-D0, AM periodic potential with quantized $\Lambda^{(k)}$ (T3.6), Dark Dimension structure (T3.5), F-theory GUT Box on $dP_3$, the v4.13 static-$\Lambda$ cosmological commitment with B-NU-1 neutrino-mass exposure, Newton recovery, Path A / Path B contingency architecture. Corpus entries DG-CFT-061 through DG-CFT-063 (CE-DG-011-a through CE-DG-011-c). The empirical face consolidates toward one observable: a gravitational noise spectrum (stochastic G), first-order in fluctuations, requiring no protected substrate and no super-extensive variance; comparison class Diosi-Penrose, CSL, Oppenheim. The matter sector reduces to two live items pursued in the rescue trellis (S-TORSION-LAGRANGIAN, S-QRF), both with likely-negative priors that close the sector honestly on a kill.

- v4.16: Cumulant reorganization shore (SF-DG-013), with the speculation-quarantine companion (SF-DG-012-ontology) recorded but not promoted. The matter-state functional that couples to geometry is reidentified: it is the modular free energy $W(\epsilon) = \log\langle e^{-\epsilon K}\rangle$, the cumulant generating functional of the modular Hamiltonian $K$, whose cumulants fill the three coupling roles with fixed (non-tunable) unit weights. The first cumulant $\langle K\rangle$ (modular energy) is the SOURCE, manifestly stress-energy coupled because the modular Hamiltonian of a region is an integral of $T_{\mu\nu}$ (Bisognano-Wichmann for wedges); this dissolves the generator gap as an order error. The second cumulant $\langle\delta K^2\rangle$ (modular variance) is the STIFFNESS and equals the quantum Fisher information (canonical energy = QFI, Lashkari-Van Raamsdonk); $F_Q$ lives here, at second order, controlling the pole, not at first order as the source. The third cumulant (non-Gaussianity) is the leading stiffness correction, predicted and uncomputed. F_Q is not wrong, it is mis-ranked: hired as the source, it is in fact the stiffness, the same error family as ER-PXR-002 (metric job-conflation) and the QFI/Var(T) conflation that opened OP-0, now identified a third time one order up. Three independent anchors (entanglement first law, canonical-energy = QFI, horizon entropy $S_{dS} = \langle K\rangle_{\text{horizon}}$) each force their weight to unity, which makes the reorganization verified-tier; the assembly into $W(\epsilon)$ from DG's own coupling remains to be derived (S-CUMULANT-DERIVE, the highest-priority open calculation, upstream of the generator gate). Convexity selection rule promoted: the modular variance is non-negative, so $W(\epsilon)$ is convex, so the matter $F_Q$ channel can only SOFTEN geometry (toward the pole), never STIFFEN it; matter softens, only the vacuum stiffens. Class blocks follow: chameleon/density-screened stiffening, matter-driven UV-softening, density-induced repulsion or antigravity, and geometric stiffness tracking the nuclear EOS are all forbidden from the matter channel. New linter rule LINT-CONVEX-1 [HARD MODE]: any matter-sector coupling whose computed effect raises geometric stiffness violates the convexity of $W$; halt and recheck order/sign. Catastrophe count promoted: the registration sector is a codimension-two cusp catastrophe, proven stable against the entire KK tower (heavy modes integrate out Gaussian, renormalizing the $\phi^2$ coefficient only, never generating an independent $\phi^3$ or new $\phi^1$); the trans-sector fold (one cognitive axis, one geometric axis on a single pleated surface) is CLOSED through the tower route, with the only surviving route a codimension-three umbilic requiring a second light scalar degenerate with the radion (S-SECOND-LIGHT-SCALAR, decidable by a spectrum calculation in the existing F-theory model). The cusp point sits exactly at the CC-1 pole / symmetry-restoration value, coinciding with the refresh-duality threshold of SF-DG-012. The laminar clock-quarantine is restated as verified (carried from SF-DG-012 Part A): the torsion-timescale sub-objection (DEAD on a 22-order clock gap) is QUARANTINED, since two processes separated by many orders in clock rate are laminar-quarantined rather than in conflict (fast layer runs at its clock, slow layer configures and reads exceptions; large separation is cleaner quarantine), per the AVF Grid-OS isomorphism. S-GEN reclassified from an independent frontier sorry to the OUTPUT of S-CUMULANT-DERIVE: the wall that closed the matter sector and gated the biology arc is reinterpreted as a rank-confusion in the modular expansion. One new structural lesson (SL-RANK-1, order-and-rank confusion as the framework's recurring failure mode). The LENR sector is reopened only as a transient EXHAUST channel (not a rate mechanism, which stays dead): a single-event coherent emission whose bill is instantaneous coherence rather than standing power, gated entirely on S-EXHAUST-COHERENCE and surviving on a $\sim 31\times$ match between $N_{\text{coh}} = (\Lambda_s/E)^2$ and $N_{\text{eff}}$ at the nuclear-transition seesaw scale $E \sim \Lambda_s^2/M_{\text{Pl}}$. The SF-DG-012 ontology arc (Speculation Ledger SL-EXP-01 through SL-EXP-10: F_Q-pixel carve, Born-sphere ontology, gravitization of QM, qualia-as-coherent-F_Q, laminar cognition, DNA error correction) is recorded as characterized speculation with explicit generator and magnitude bills; nothing from it is load-bearing or citable, and its net finding is negative and sharp (no generated route pays both the generator and magnitude bills). Corpus entries DG-CFT-064 through DG-CFT-069 (CE-DG-012-a/b, CE-DG-013-a through CE-DG-013-d). Next action: run S-CUMULANT-DERIVE (closes or reopens S-GEN, the upstream gate for everything), then S-EXHAUST-COHERENCE (decides LENR-via-DG, the priority target), then S-NOISE (the empirical-face calculation, now downstream of S-CUMULANT-DERIVE).
