# 1. THE TIERS

Each tier constrains the space of viable theories. Higher tiers are more defensible. If a higher tier falls, everything below needs re-examination, but everything above survives.

## 1.0 Core Identity Statement [v4.14]

**CC-1 (Core Claim, v4.14):** Gravity couples to the modular-Hamiltonian Fisher information of the matter sector via the state-dependent VEV $v(F_Q)$ of the SO(1,4) gravitational Higgs, with super-extensive O(N²) scaling for ODLRO matter states. The coupling exhibits a pole structure at $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$ that produces qualitatively distinct gravitational responses below and above threshold. This is the framework's central theoretical claim and its most distinctive structural contribution.

**Scope.** CC-1 generates the framework's matter-sector predictions: F09 (failed supernovae via bulk-routing), F11 (KK gravitons as dark matter), F13 / F13.2 (LUNA screening anomaly via resonant radion catalysis), F19 (geometric wavefunction collapse), F21 (GRB compact-object phenomenology). These predictions are branch-independent: they do not depend on whether the cosmological constant is static (Path A, T3.6 Addazi-Meluccio topological quantization) or evolving (Path B, T3.6' geometric $\Lambda \sim R^{-4}$ via Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu evolving Dark Dimension).

**Relation to Tier 3.** The cosmology-sector application of CC-1 (whether the universe sits at a static $\Lambda^{(k)}$ minimum or evolves via a light modulus) is a Tier 3 branch-conditional commitment carrying the framework's most exposed empirical bet (see §1.5, T3.6 v4.14 annotation, and the v4.14 update module integrated below). The v4.14 restructuring foregrounds CC-1 as the load-bearing identity and demotes the cosmology-sector choice to a branch-dependent layer, ensuring that an unfavorable DESI Y5 / Euclid resolution falsifies a specific Path A commitment rather than the framework's distinctive theoretical content. The same logic applies in reverse: a Path B falsification (failure to identify a structurally natural $m_\chi \sim H_0$ modulus, or DESI Y5 confirmation of $w = -1$ at 5σ) does not move CC-1.

**Constituent commitments.** CC-1 is supported by: K1-K6 (5D Karch-Randall braneworld plus MM gravity plus mandatory topological bulk), K7-K17 (kernel constraints on Newton's constant, KK adiabatic stability, BBN structural immunity), Formulation B ($F_Q = \text{Var}(K_{\text{mod}})$ with Donnelly-Freidel edge modes, distinguishing O(N) extensive from O(N²) super-extensive scaling), Dark Dimension structural import (Montero-Vafa-Valenzuela arXiv:2205.12293, with the radius $R \sim$ μm preserved and its static-vs-evolving status moved to the contingent cosmology layer), and F-theory $dP_3$ + $X_{F13}$ Pati-Salam matter sector. All of these survive both cosmology branches.

**Linter discipline.** Per LINT-CORE-1 (v4.14), external positioning of the framework leads with CC-1 and its matter-sector predictions, with cosmology-sector commitments framed as contingent applications. Per LINT-PATH-1 (v4.14), Path A and Path B commitments are mutually exclusive; structural elements from both paths cannot be combined in a single trellis branch.

**CC-1 annotation (v4.16, supersedes the v4.14 statement above).** Two shores change what CC-1 asserts. First (v4.15, SF-DG-011): OP-0 splits. OP-0-COUPLING stands (the pole exists in the Lagrangian, with $\gamma = c_{\text{KK}}/(128\pi^2 \Lambda_s^2)$ and $F_{Q,\text{crit}} = 16\pi^2 m_\rho^2 \Lambda_s^2/c_{\text{KK}} \sim 10^{12}$ to $10^{13}$ GeV⁴, corroborated independently by the refresh-duality queue-capacity formula, SF-DG-012). OP-0-ACTIVATION dies: the super-extensive O(N²) Var(T) that the v4.14 statement claims for ODLRO matter states is killed by the matter-sector exclusion record on five independent arguments (volume-law FDT, GHZ decoherence, dimensional pinning, two failed vehicle searches). The threshold sits 12 to 25 orders above what any audited equilibrium or driven laboratory substrate supplies. CC-1 is therefore demoted from foregrounded core to conditional structure: the pole is real and dormant in every known matter environment, with its confirmed activation domain being horizon-scale physics (where saturation coincides with the holographic bound). The matter-sector predictions the v4.14 Scope paragraph lists (F13/F13.2, F19, F21, F05) move to the exclusion reservoir under the exclusion record's three-gate reactivation test; F09 and F11 are not moved by the shore but inherit the OP-0 split by reference. Second (v4.16, SF-DG-013): the coupling functional is reidentified. Geometry does not read $F_Q$ as a first-order source; it reads the modular free energy $W(\epsilon) = \log\langle e^{-\epsilon K}\rangle$, whose first cumulant $\langle K\rangle$ (modular energy, an integral of $T_{\mu\nu}$ by Bisognano-Wichmann) is the source and whose second cumulant $\langle\delta K^2\rangle = F_Q$ is the stiffness controlling the pole. F_Q was mis-ranked, not wrong: it sits at second order, not first. This dissolves the generator question into an order error (S-GEN becomes the output of S-CUMULANT-DERIVE) and adds a one-signed convexity rule (matter softens geometry, only the vacuum stiffens; LINT-CONVEX-1). The corrected one-line identity: gravity couples to the modular free energy of the matter sector through the state-dependent SO(1,4) Higgs VEV; the source is modular energy, the stiffness is the modular variance (= QFI), and the pole at $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$ marks local symmetry restoration to the pre-geometric phase. The assembly of $W(\epsilon)$ from DG's own coupling is consistency-checked against three standard anchors but not yet derived (S-CUMULANT-DERIVE, the gate sorry for the matter sector).

## 1.1 Tier 0: Metaphysical Commitments

**Status:** Maximally defensible. Rejecting any of these makes science impossible.

**T0.1: External Realism.** An external world exists independent of observation. Physical systems have definite properties whether or not they are measured. The measurement problem in quantum mechanics is a problem of description, not of ontology.

**T0.2: Consistency.** The external world behaves consistently. Identical initial conditions produce identical outcomes (up to quantum indeterminacy, which is itself consistent). The laws of physics do not change with location, time, or observer.

**T0.3: Describability.** The structure of the external world can be captured by mathematical formalism. Physical theories are maps; the territory exists independently of the map. The effectiveness of mathematics in physics reflects genuine structural correspondence.

**T0.4: Materialism.** All physical phenomena have physical causes. Causal closure is complete. "Spooky" correlations (entanglement, nonlocality) are real but do not transmit information superluminally and do not violate T0.2.

## 1.2 Tier 1: Thermodynamic Realism

**Status:** Empirically undefeated across all of physics. Every killed mechanism in this trellis died here or at Tier 2.

**T1.1: Energy Conservation.** Energy is conserved in every closed system. Energy can change form but cannot be created or destroyed. Any calculation producing energy from nothing is wrong.

**T1.2: Second Law.** Entropy of an isolated system never decreases. Macroscopic processes are irreversible. Time has a thermodynamic arrow.

**T1.3: Finite Energy Budgets.** Physical processes cannot produce trans-Planckian energy outputs from sub-Planckian inputs. Any $E = \rho \times V$ calculation yielding energies exceeding the rest mass of the progenitor system is automatically suspect. This is the Volume Bug filter: it catches errors of the form "multiply a Planck-scale energy density by a macroscopic volume."

**T1.4: Information Processing Costs Energy.** Landauer's principle: erasing one bit of information dissipates at least $kT \ln 2$ of energy. Information processing is a physical process subject to T1.1 and T1.2. The vacuum, if it processes information, pays these costs.

**T1.5: Null Energy Condition.** For any null vector $k^\mu$, $T_{\mu\nu} k^\mu k^\nu \geq 0$ for all physically realizable matter. Violations signal ghost instabilities (kinetic term sign flip), vacuum decay, or missing physics.

**T1.6: Causal Locality.** Information propagates at most at $c$. No instantaneous global effects. A theory that requires a macroscopic spatially extended system to respond as a single monolithic quantum gate violates this. This is the filter that catches naive Margolus-Levitin applications.

## 1.3 Tier 2: Mathematical Consistency

**Status:** Structural requirements. Any theory violating these is not a theory.

**T2.1: Unitarity.** The S-matrix is unitary. Probability is conserved. No information is destroyed in principle (though it may become practically inaccessible).

**T2.2: Ghost Freedom.** All propagating degrees of freedom have positive-definite kinetic terms. Negative kinetic energy (ghosts) renders the vacuum unstable to runaway pair production. Any construction must demonstrate ghost freedom through explicit DOF counting.

**T2.3: Correct DOF Counting.** The number of propagating degrees of freedom must be established by rigorous Hamiltonian constraint analysis (Dirac-Bergmann algorithm), not by counting fields. Constrained systems (gauge theories, gravity) always have fewer DOF than naive field counting suggests.

**T2.4: Diffeomorphism Invariance.** The laws of physics take the same form in all coordinate systems. Any coupling to the gravitational sector must be expressible in a generally covariant form. State-dependent couplings (such as $v = v(F_Q)$) require explicit demonstration that $F_Q$ transforms as a scalar under diffeomorphisms.

**T2.5: GR Recovery.** Any modification of gravity must reduce exactly to General Relativity in the appropriate limit (weak field, incoherent matter, low density). The gravitational constant $G_N$ must be constant and universal in this limit.

**T2.6: Observational Compatibility.** Existing precision measurements (NICER radii, LIGO tidal deformability, GW170817, Shapiro delay masses, Cas A cooling, RHIC viscosity, short-range gravity tests, atomic clock constraints) must be respected. Predictions contradicting established observations at the relevant precision constitute kills.

**T2.7: Conformal Invariance of Gauge Kinetic Terms.** The Maxwell action $\sqrt{-g}\,F^{\mu\nu}F_{\mu\nu}$ is conformally invariant in 4D. This is a theorem of 4D field theory, independent of any specific model. Any gauge field localized on a 3-brane in AdS$_5$ has a tree-level coupling constant independent of brane position, because the AdS$_5$ warp factor is a conformal rescaling of the 4D induced metric. This structural boundary establishes that the framework cannot modify electromagnetic couplings through any tree-level geometric channel.

**T2.8: Higgs Identity.** Different Higgs fields in different sectors of the theory must not be conflated. The SO(1,4) gravitational Higgs (which sets $M_{\text{Pl,eff}}$) is the gravitational symmetry-breaking scale. It couples to the electron mass, Bohr radius, and pycnonuclear screening at zero strength at tree level. *This filter catches the most common error in external analyses of the framework.*

**T2.9: Semiclassical Causality.** The state-dependent coupling $v = v(F_Q)$ must preserve the causal structure of spacetime. The matter sector evolves via standard linear quantum mechanics. The gravitational background responds to the quantum state through semiclassical backreaction, analogous to $G_{\mu\nu} = 8\pi\langle T_{\mu\nu}\rangle_{\text{ren}}$. The no-signaling theorem for linear QM guarantees that $F_Q$ evaluated from the local reduced density matrix is invariant under spacelike-separated operations. Any construction where the metric depends on the un-traced global density matrix violates special relativity via the Gisin-Polchinski theorem and is rejected. The coupling $v(F_Q)$ is evaluated from the local reduced state on the causal diamond; Donnelly-Freidel edge modes ensure this evaluation is foliation-independent but do not independently enforce causality. All effective action computations deriving the state-dependent coupling must employ the Schwinger-Keldysh Closed Time Path (CTP) formalism, which natively enforces retarded boundary conditions ($G_R(x,y) = 0$ for spacelike separations) through the forward/backward time-branch structure. The coincidence-limit reduction of the heat kernel to the $a_4(x)$ contact term renders the coupling strictly local. This is a theorem of the construction, not an additional assumption.

## 1.4 Tier 2.5: Empirical Breakdowns

The problems that demand a theory. Each is an empirical fact or observational tension that current physics does not explain. The construction (Tier 4) is justified by its ability to address these breakdowns while respecting Tiers 0 through 2.

### General Relativity Breakdowns

**B1: Singularities.** GR predicts geodesic incompleteness at black hole interiors and the Big Bang. Physical quantities (density, curvature) diverge. This signals the breakdown of the classical theory.

**B2: Dark Energy.** The cosmological constant $\Lambda$ exists and drives accelerating expansion. Its value ($\sim 10^{-122}$ in Planck units) is unexplained. DESI 2024-2025 BAO data (DR1 + DR2) prefers evolving dark energy ($w_0 \sim -0.7$, $w_a \sim -1.0$) at $2.8\sigma$ to $4.2\sigma$ over static $\Lambda$CDM, depending on the supernovae compilation utilized ($2.8\sigma$ floor from DESI + CMB + Pantheon+; $4.2\sigma$ ceiling from DESI + CMB + DESY5), suggesting $\Lambda$ may evolve.

**v4.13 reclassification.** B2 moves from "empirical anchor for F12" to "external anomaly outside the framework's explanatory domain; falsification watch." The framework now predicts static $\Lambda^{(k)}$ within the current cosmic epoch via AM topological selection (T3.6, F-CC) and gains no predictive content from the thawing signature. If the DESI DR2 thawing preference is confirmed at $5\sigma$ by DESI Y5 or Euclid, the framework's commitment to static $\Lambda^{(k)}$ is falsified; reactivation conditions for F12 are listed under the retracted-function notice in §3. The JWST cross-calibration of $H_0$ remains live as a separate empirical question with no current framework prediction.

**v4.14 annotation.** Under the v4.14 core-vs-contingent restructuring, B2 sits at the Path A / Path B selection boundary. Path A retains the v4.13 prediction of static $\Lambda^{(k)}$ within the current cosmic epoch and treats DESI DR2 thawing as falsification watch (current working hypothesis as of v4.14). Path B (prepared contingency) predicts evolving $w(z)$ via the Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu construction and is activated upon DESI Y5 / Euclid confirmation of evolving $w(z)$ at $\geq 5\sigma$. The framework's Bayesian credence on Path A is revised upward from rough 10-25% to rough 25-40% per Addendum A (Vafa-lab is actively constructing interior-moduli-space critical points), with Path B at rough 25-40% and 20-50% mass on alternative resolutions including systematic-artifact dissipation of the DESI signal.

**B-NU-1 (new, v4.13): Neutrino Mass Sector Friction.** By rejecting DESI DR2 thawing, the framework commits to the $\Lambda$CDM upper bound $\sum m_\nu < 0.064$ eV (95% from DESI DR2 + CMB). Terrestrial oscillation experiments require $\sum m_\nu \geq 0.059$ eV (normal hierarchy). Net friction $\sim 0.005$ eV with the terrestrial neutrino sector. Tracking for resolution via inverted hierarchy possibility, future neutrino mass measurements (KATRIN, Project 8, cosmological surveys), or future shifts in the cosmological mass bound. No structural resolution from the framework's current axiomatic core; tracking as an external observational tension.

**B3: Dark Matter.** 85% of the gravitational mass of the universe is unaccounted for by the Standard Model. Rotation curves, lensing, CMB anisotropy, and large-scale structure all require it. Its particle identity is unknown.

**B4: Black Hole Information Paradox.** Hawking radiation appears to destroy information (violating T2.1), yet the horizon is locally smooth. Resolution requires understanding the microstructure of horizons.

**B5: Cosmological Constant Problem.** Quantum field theory predicts a vacuum energy $\sim 10^{120}$ times larger than observed. The cancellation mechanism is unknown.

### Standard Model Breakdowns

**B6: Hierarchy Problem.** The electroweak scale ($M_{\text{EW}} \sim 10^2\,\text{GeV}$) is $10^{16}$ times smaller than the Planck scale ($M_{\text{Pl}} \sim 10^{19}\,\text{GeV}$). No mechanism within the SM protects this hierarchy from radiative corrections.

**B7: No Quantum Gravity.** The Standard Model and General Relativity are mutually incompatible at energies approaching $M_{\text{Pl}}$. Perturbative quantization of GR is non-renormalizable.

**B8: Neutrino Masses.** Neutrinos have mass (oscillation experiments), but the SM does not predict this. The mass generation mechanism is unknown.

**B9: Matter-Antimatter Asymmetry.** The universe is matter-dominated. The SM does not contain sufficient CP violation to produce the observed baryon asymmetry.

### Observational Tensions and Anomalies

**B10: Hubble Tension.** Local $H_0$ measurements ($\sim 73\,\text{km/s/Mpc}$ from distance ladder) disagree with CMB-inferred $H_0$ ($\sim 67\,\text{km/s/Mpc}$ from Planck) at $\sim 5\sigma$.

**B11: $\sigma_8$ Tension.** Weak lensing surveys measure less matter clustering than Planck CMB predicts, at $\sim 2$ to $3\sigma$.

**B12: LUNA Screening Anomaly.** Enhanced electron screening in $d + d$ fusion in metallic targets exceeds linear Thomas-Fermi predictions by 10 to $30\times$. Anomaly correlates with conductor/insulator status, not lattice coherence. On-resonance laser stimulation amplifies the effect at specific phonon frequencies.

**B13: Hyperon Puzzle.** Standard nuclear physics predicts that hyperons appear in neutron star cores at $\sim 2\rho_0$, softening the EOS and limiting $M_{\max}$ to $\sim 1.6$ to $1.8\,M_\odot$. Yet pulsars exist at $2.08\,M_\odot$ (PSR J0740+6620) and $2.35\,M_\odot$ (PSR J0952-0607). Additional stiffness is required. **B13 annotation (v4.3):** The mass of PSR J0952-0607 has been refined to $2.35 \pm 0.11\,M_\odot$ (Romani et al. 2026, arXiv:2512.05099). The framework's calibrated prediction $M_{\max} = 2.323\,M_\odot$ (SLy + torsion at $\rho_{\text{sf}} = 2\rho_0$) remains within $1\sigma$ of the measurement ($0.25\sigma$ below the central value). The lower bound $M_{\text{TOV}} > 2.27\,M_\odot$ at $1\sigma$ is satisfied. If future measurements with reduced uncertainties confirm the central value above $2.35\,M_\odot$, the base nuclear EOS (currently SLy) should be recalibrated to a stiffer parameterization (APR4 or a speed-of-sound model), or $\rho_{\text{sf}}$ should be adjusted downward from $2\rho_0$. The torsion pressure mechanism itself is insensitive to the base EOS choice; the recalibration would shift $M_{\max}$ upward while preserving the structural resolution of the hyperon puzzle.

**B14: Lower Mass Gap.** Compact objects in the $2.5$ to $5\,M_\odot$ range are anomalously rare. The gap separates the heaviest neutron stars from the lightest black holes. LIGO O3/O4 detections (GW190814, GW230529) are beginning to populate this region, preferentially from binary/merger channels. **B14 annotation (v4.3):** GW230529 (LIGO-P2300352) confirms a mass-gap compact object ($2.5$ to $4.5\,M_\odot$) produced in a binary merger, consistent with C07b (puncture channel, no envelope recruitment).

**B15: Failed Supernovae.** Some massive stars ($\sim 17+\,M_\odot$) appear to vanish without explosion. N6946-BH1 ($25\,M_\odot$ RSG) produced only a faint $\sim 10^{47}\,\text{erg}$ transient and disappeared, confirmed by JWST. Standard neutrino-driven explosion mechanisms fail for high-compactness cores.

**B16: CMB Cold Spot.** The Eridanus supervoid (20% underdense) aligns with an anomalous CMB cold spot. Standard $\Lambda$CDM ISW predictions undershoot the observed temperature deficit. DES Y3 data shows 30% weaker lensing from this void.

**B17: The Measurement Problem and the Gran Sasso Falsification.** Quantum mechanics lacks a physical criterion separating the unitary regime of superposition from the classical regime of macroscopic definiteness. The Penrose-Diosi (DP) model provides the most physically motivated objective collapse theory, attributing wavefunction reduction to gravitational self-energy of the superposed mass distribution: $\tau_{\text{DP}} \sim \hbar/\Delta E_G$. However, the standard DP collapse dynamics generate continuous stochastic momentum diffusion on charged particles, producing a calculable spectrum of spontaneous X-ray bremsstrahlung ($d\Gamma/dE \propto 1/E$, scaling as $R_0^{-3}$). In 2021, a dedicated experiment at the Laboratori Nazionali del Gran Sasso (Donadi et al., Nature Physics 2021) using a high-purity germanium detector in the 10 to 100 keV range detected zero anomalous radiation, establishing a lower bound $R_0 \gtrsim 0.54 \times 10^{-10}\,\text{m}$. This is three orders of magnitude above the natural nuclear-scale cutoff ($R_0 \sim 10^{-15}\,\text{m}$) required for macroscopic localization, falsifying the parameter-free DP model as formulated in 4D. If gravity induces objective collapse, the energy of state reduction must dissipate through a channel invisible to 4D electromagnetism.

**B18: SN 2024afav Chirp Anomaly.** The superluminous supernova SN 2024afav ($z = 0.0724$, $M_c \approx -20.7$) exhibits a quasi-periodic, accelerating chirp in its post-peak electromagnetic light curve, attributed by Farah et al. (Nature 2026) to Lense-Thirring precession of a misaligned accretion disk around a newborn magnetar ($P = 4.2 \pm 0.2$ ms, $B = 1.6 \pm 0.1 \times 10^{14}$ G). Seven distinct brightness bumps span 175 days. The temporal intervals between bumps accelerate from 42.4 days to 16.1 days (Phase 0 to +109), consistent with a contracting accretion disk. At Phase +109, the interval abruptly doubles to 32.1 days, producing a $> 5.8\sigma$ deviation from the smooth viscous power-law baseline predicted by standard $\alpha$-disk models. This deceleration is coincident with the spectroscopic emergence of lower-ionization [O II] + [Ca II] 7300 A emission and a weakening of early [O III] features. The standard LT model accommodates the gross periodicity but the discontinuous deceleration and the correlated ionization shift remain unexplained. The anomaly is open.

**B19: Exotic Stellar Cooling Anomaly.** The pulsating white dwarf G117-B15A exhibits a secular period drift $\dot{P}_{\text{obs}} = (5.12 \pm 0.82) \times 10^{-15}$ s/s for its 215.2 s fundamental mode, measured over a 50-year baseline. Standard gravothermal models predict $\dot{P}_{\text{th}} \approx 1.25 \times 10^{-15}$ s/s. The discrepancy corresponds to an anomalous missing luminosity of $\sim 10^{32}$ erg/s. The neutron star in Cassiopeia A exhibits a $\sim 2\%$ to $4\%$ surface temperature decline over a 10 to 18 year Chandra baseline, exceeding modified Urca predictions ($\sim 0.2\%$ to $0.3\%$ per decade). Mainstream attributions invoke DFSZ axion emission ($m_a \cos^2\beta \approx 17.4$ meV) or enhanced Cooper-pair breaking neutrinos. The axion parameter space required for these attributions ($g_{a\gamma\gamma} \sim 10^{-11}$ GeV$^{-1}$, $g_{aee} \sim 10^{-13}$) is under severe multi-modal observational pressure (see consistency checks below).

### What the Framework Addresses

The following breakdowns are acknowledged but not claimed as targets: B8 (neutrino masses), B9 (matter-antimatter asymmetry), B5 (CC from first principles, partially reframed but unsolved). The framework addresses gravity; the SM gauge sectors are treated as external matter fields on the brane (Paper 0, Section 9.4). The framework constrains the parameter space of any GUT that claims consistency with the state-dependent geometry (K10, K11, K12).

### Consistency Checks from Null Results

The following empirical developments are consistent with the framework's structural constraints but do not constitute predictions of the framework. They are recorded as compatibility checks.

**Muon g-2 Final Result (2025).** The Fermilab Muon g-2 experiment concluded with its final 2025 results at 127 ppb precision. Under revised lattice QCD calculations for the leading-order Hadronic Vacuum Polarization, the Standard Model prediction agrees with experiment at $\sim 0.6\sigma$, definitively dissolving the historical $> 5\sigma$ anomaly. This null result is consistent with T2.7 (conformal invariance of the 4D Maxwell action), which forbids tree-level geometric modification of electromagnetic couplings. The framework predicts zero BSM contribution to $a_\mu$ through the gravitational channel; the kinetic mixing bound $\xi \sim 10^{-36}$ (K14) renders any radion-mediated correction negligible ($\delta a_\mu \sim 10^{-30}$).

**MicroBooNE (2025).** Definitive rejection of the single light sterile neutrino hypothesis at $> 95\%$ CL. The framework predicts no sterile neutrinos; the bulk KK tower is spin-2, not spin-1/2. Compatible.

**XENONnT (2022-2025).** Zero excess in the electronic recoil spectrum, eliminating the XENON1T $3.4\sigma$ hint. The framework predicts zero anomalous electronic recoils from the KK tower; massive spin-2 gravitons couple gravitationally ($y \sim m/M_{\text{Pl}}$), far below the XENON sensitivity. Compatible.

**ALPS II (2024).** The Any Light Particle Search II at DESY conducted its first science campaign (February to May 2024). For pseudoscalar bosons with $m_a < 0.1$ meV, the experiment set $g_{a\gamma\gamma} < 3.5 \times 10^{-11}$ GeV$^{-1}$ at 95% CL. Absolute null result. The framework predicts zero axion-like particles; the KK tower is spin-2, and K4 (conformal invariance) eliminates any $a F\tilde{F}$ coupling for the radion. Compatible.

**CAST Final Results (2024).** The CERN Axion Solar Telescope set $g_{a\gamma\gamma} < 0.66 \times 10^{-10}$ GeV$^{-1}$ for $m_a \lesssim 0.02$ eV. Extended runs with Xe-based Micromegas and NuSTAR solar minimum data pushed limits to $g_{a\gamma\gamma} < 5.8 \times 10^{-11}$ GeV$^{-1}$. Zero solar axion flux detected. Compatible with K4.

**Chandra RE J0317-853 (2022).** A 37 to 40 ks Chandra ACIS-I observation of the hot, highly magnetic white dwarf RE J0317-853 ($B \approx 500$ MG, $T_c \sim 1.4$ keV) detected zero Primakoff X-ray emission. The combined coupling product constraint is $|g_{aee}\,g_{a\gamma\gamma}| < 1.3 \times 10^{-25}$ GeV$^{-1}$ at 95% CL, more than one order of magnitude below the phenomenological requirement ($\sim 2 \times 10^{-24}$ GeV$^{-1}$) for axion-driven white dwarf cooling. Compatible with K4.

**Keck/Lick Spectropolarimetry of Magnetic White Dwarfs (2025).** High-precision spectropolarimetric observations of isolated MWDs (SDSS J033320, ZTF J190132, PG1015+014) show zero axion-induced linear or circular polarization shifts. Upper bound: $g_{a\gamma\gamma} \lesssim 1.7 \times 10^{-12}$ GeV$^{-1}$. Compatible with K4.

**Framework prediction (strong):** IAXO and all subsequent axion helioscopes targeting the stellar cooling parameter space will return null results. The K4 constraint (conformal invariance of the 4D Maxwell action at tree level, with radion coupling only through the trace anomaly) structurally forbids Primakoff-type conversion for the radion. Stellar cooling anomalies, if the framework is correct, are sourced by KK graviton bulk emission, invisible to electromagnetic detectors.

**Gaia DR3 White Dwarf Luminosity Function (2026).** Antonini et al. (arXiv:2603.08573) and population synthesis studies using Gaia DR3 data (arXiv:2603.00901) argued that anomalous cooling in the white dwarf luminosity function is driven by DFSZ axion emission ($m_a \cos^2\beta \approx 17.4$ meV). The required axion parameter space ($g_{a\gamma\gamma} \sim 10^{-11}$ GeV$^{-1}$, $g_{aee} \sim 10^{-13}$) falls within the region under severe multi-modal observational pressure from ALPS II, CAST, and Chandra RE J0317-853 (see consistency checks above). The Type-H framework attributes the same cooling deficit to KK graviton bulk emission (B19 plausible contract), which is invisible to electromagnetic axion detectors. The Gaia DR3 WDLF data is compatible with both hypotheses; discrimination requires the quantitative KK emission rate calculation (Appendix D open problem).

**Ambient-Pressure Superconductivity Record (2026).** Chu and Deng (University of Houston), PNAS 123(11) e2536178123, arXiv:2603.12437. Pressure-Quench Protocol (PQP) applied to HgBa$_2$Ca$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{8+\delta}$ achieves $T_c = 151\,\text{K}$ at ambient pressure. Metastable phase stable for $\sim 3$ days at 77 K; degrades above 200 K. Synchrotron XRD verified. Previous record: 133 K (1993). Highest confirmed ambient-pressure $T_c$ as of March 2026. The framework's superconductivity investigation (v4.4) concluded that all radion-mediated pathways to room-temperature superconductivity are dead; the framework has no mechanism to explain or predict high-$T_c$ cuprate superconductivity. Tracked as external empirical milestone.

**Anomalous Thermal Hall Effect in Kagome Superconductor (2025).** Yoshida et al., Science Advances 11(40), eadu2973, arXiv:2509.10630. Zero-field anomalous thermal Hall effect observed below $T_c$ in CsV$_3$Sb$_5$. Peak $\kappa_{xy}/T \sim 0.02\,\text{W}\,\text{K}^{-2}\,\text{m}^{-1}$ at $T \sim 1\,\text{K}$, exceeding intrinsic topological (Chern edge) prediction by a factor of $\sim 40$. Control on 2H-NbS$_2$: null. Authors attribute excess to extrinsic impurity-induced ATHE in chiral state. The framework's torsion-based explanation (F24, geometric torsion from chiral Cooper pair hypermomentum) is dead: ambient-VEV torsion is 49 OoM too weak, and no equilibrium condensed-matter state achieves the K7 threshold for VEV suppression (69 OoM deficit). The chiral hypermomentum selection rule (SO-SC2) survives as a qualitative structural observation. Tracked as external empirical milestone.

**VIP Collaboration / Gran Sasso Karolyhazy Exclusion (2026).** Bortolotti et al. (arXiv:2601.00651) establish $R_K > 4.64$ m at 95% CL using a BEGe detector at Gran Sasso, excluding the generalized Karolyhazy gravity-induced decoherence model and constraining non-Markovian CSL formulations. The framework's F19 (geometric wavefunction collapse) routes collapse energy into the 5D bulk as massive spin-2 dark radiation, producing zero X-ray bremsstrahlung by conformal invariance ($\Omega^4 \times \Omega^{-4} = 1$). The VIP result strengthens the empirical case for the 5D exhaust channel by progressively eliminating 4D collapse models. Compatible. Strengthens F19/C19c.

**M31-2014-DS1 Failed Supernova Candidate (2026).** Beasor et al. (arXiv:2601.05317) confirm the complete disappearance of this luminous supergiant without supernova shock breakout. The framework's F09 (Failed Supernovae Are Dark) and C09 predict that massive thermal iron cores ($f \approx 0$, zero coherence domains) undergo silent Linter excision when $t_{\text{ff}} < t_s$, with collapse energy channeled into the bulk. The missing energy signature (no substantial electromagnetic or kinetic ejecta) is consistent with the geometric censorship mechanism. Compatible with F09/C09.

**IAXO/BabyIAXO Status (2025).** Giannotti et al. (arXiv:2504.00079) report the International Axion Observatory construction status and projected sensitivity. The framework makes a rigid falsification prediction: IAXO and BabyIAXO will return absolute null results for solar axion Primakoff conversion. The KK graviton tower couples exclusively through gravity ($y \sim m/M_{\text{Pl}}$); conformal invariance (T2.7) structurally forbids Primakoff-type conversion for the radion. Any confirmed detection of an axion-photon conversion signal in the parameter space required for stellar cooling ($g_{a\gamma\gamma} \sim 10^{-11}$ GeV$^{-1}$) would falsify the framework's core axioms. Track for immediate falsification potential upon first science data.

## 1.5 Tier 3: Quantum Gravity Landscape

**Status:** Theoretical commitments. Less defensible than Tiers 0 through 2 but supported by extensive formal consistency checks. If these fall, the specific construction (Tier 4) needs replacement, but the functions (which respond to Tier 2.5 breakdowns) persist.

**T3.1: String/M-Theory as Consistent UV Completion.** String theory provides a mathematically consistent framework for quantum gravity. Its landscape of solutions may or may not describe our universe, but its internal consistency is well-established.

**T3.2: Swampland Constraints.** Not all effective field theories can be UV-completed into quantum gravity. The Swampland program (Vafa 2005, Ooguri-Vafa 2007) identifies constraints that separate the "landscape" (consistent) from the "swampland" (inconsistent). Key conjectures: Distance Conjecture (traversing infinite distances in moduli space produces infinite towers of exponentially light states), TCC (cosmological fluctuations cannot be trans-Planckian), dS Conjecture (stable de Sitter vacua may not exist in quantum gravity).

**T3.3: Holographic Principle.** The degrees of freedom of a region of space scale with its boundary area, not its volume (Bekenstein bound, Ryu-Takayanagi formula). The AdS/CFT correspondence provides the most rigorously established non-perturbative formulation of quantum gravity.

**T3.4: Species Scale is Dynamical.** The effective UV cutoff of quantum gravity depends on the spectrum of light states accessible at a given point in moduli space (Dvali 2010, van de Heisteeg-Vafa-Wiesner-Wu 2023). The Species Scale responds to the state of the matter sector through the spectrum it counts.

**T3.5: Dark Dimension Scenario.** One mesoscopic extra dimension with radius $R_{\text{Dark}} \sim \mu\text{m}$ produces a KK tower beginning at $m_{\text{KK}} \sim 10^{-3}\,\text{eV}$ (Montero, Vafa, Valenzuela 2023). The fundamental 5D Planck mass is $M_5 \approx 2.6 \times 10^8\,\text{GeV}$. This scenario connects the cosmological constant to the size of the extra dimension via $R_{\text{Dark}} \sim \Lambda^{-1/4}$.

**T3.6: Pre-Geometric Topological Quantization of $\Lambda$** [v4.8, branch-conditional v4.14]. The MacDowell-Mansouri SSB action generates a Gauss-Bonnet term whose coupling $\alpha_{\mathrm{GB}} = -4 Y_{\mathrm{MM}} v$ acts as a gravitational $\theta$-angle in the path integral. Periodicity of $\theta$ mod $2\pi$ forces the cosmological constant into discrete topological sectors $\Lambda^{(k)}$ labeled by integer $k$, with the master relation $3 c M_P^2/(32 \Lambda^{(k)}) = -\theta^{(0)} + 2\pi k$ where $c = 128\pi^2$. The observed hierarchy $M_P^2/\Lambda \sim 10^{120}$ corresponds to $k \sim S_{\mathrm{dS}}$, the de Sitter entropy. Inter-sector tunneling is suppressed by $e^{-S_{\mathrm{dS}}}$. Reference: Addazi-Meluccio 2026 (arXiv:2602.16840). The framework's adoption of this mechanism is conditional on T4 reformulation of the SSB potential to the periodic Addazi-Meluccio form (Section 4.4, revised v4.8).

**v4.14 reclassification.** T3.6 is now the framework's Path A commitment: current working hypothesis, retained as long as DESI thawing remains below 5σ. The Path B alternative is T3.6' (geometric $\Lambda \sim R^{-4}$ via the Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu evolving Dark Dimension construction, arXiv:2507.03090), activated upon Path A falsification. Both paths are developed to discharge-ready state per LINT-PATH-1; structural elements from the two paths cannot be combined. See the v4.14 update module (§6) and Addendum A (§6.A) below for the full Path A / Path B / Selection Criteria specification. Per Addendum A, the framework's Path A commitment is structurally one specific mechanism within the Vafa-lab interior-moduli-space critical-point program (Baykara-Chen-Vafa arXiv:2605.16484v1), not contrarian to it; the dS swampland bound $|\nabla V|/V \geq 2/\sqrt{d-2}$ applies asymptotically at weak coupling, not in the interior of moduli space where the AM minimum lives.

**T3.6' (Path B, prepared contingency, v4.14): Evolving Dark Dimension Cosmology.** $\Lambda$ is set geometrically by the Dark Dimension radius: $\Lambda \sim R^{-4}$ with $R \sim$ μm. The smallness of $\Lambda$ derives from $R$ being mesoscopic rather than from topological quantization. $R(t)$ evolves cosmologically, driven by slow-roll of a separate light modulus $\chi$ with $m_\chi \sim H_0 \sim 10^{-33}$ eV. Equation of state $w(z) \neq -1$ with thawing or freezing behavior matching the DESI DR2 signature in the Bedroya-Vafa class. T3.6' is dormant under v4.14 (Path A is the current working hypothesis) but discharge-ready per LINT-PATH-1. Reference: Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu arXiv:2507.03090.

## 1.6 Tier 4: The Specific Construction

The building blocks of this particular theory. Everything above is more defensible. Everything below inherits from here.

### 4.1 The Arena

The observable universe is the worldvolume of a DBI brane embedded in Anti-de Sitter$_5$. The bulk is governed by a 5D Chern-Simons action for SO(2,4) (the AdS$_5$ isometry group):

$$S_{\text{bulk}} = \frac{k}{4\pi^2}\int_{M_5}\text{Tr}\!\left(\mathcal{A}\wedge d\mathcal{A}\wedge d\mathcal{A} + \frac{3}{2}\mathcal{A}^3\wedge d\mathcal{A} + \frac{3}{5}\mathcal{A}^5\right)$$

The bulk is topological: zero local propagating DOF. No bulk ghosts. (Paper 0, eq 2.12)

### 4.2 The Brane

An End-of-the-World brane at radial position $z = z_0$ in the Poincare patch. The induced metric is $g^{\text{ind}}_{\mu\nu} = (L/z_0)^2\,\eta_{\mu\nu}$. The Israel junction conditions fix the brane tension:

$$T_3 = \frac{6}{\kappa_5^2 L}$$

This result is independent of $z_0$. The tension is constant. The brane can sit at any position with the same tension. (Paper 0, eq 2.7)

### 4.3 The Brane Action [revised v4.10, annotated v4.11, v4.12]

The brane carries two sectors plus the Higgs-sector dynamical structure forced by SO(1,4) covariance:

**MacDowell-Mansouri sector** (gauge structure and symmetry breaking, with auxiliary-field kinetic structure):

$$S_{\text{MM}} = \alpha\int \epsilon_{ABCDE}\,F^{AB}\wedge F^{CD}\,\phi^E + \beta\int d^4x\,|J|\,V(\phi^A\phi_A) + S_{\text{aux}}[\phi^A, A^{AB}, \tau]$$

where the auxiliary-field kinetic action is (Langenscheidt 2019, §4.2):

$$S_{\text{aux}} = \frac{1}{3!\rho}\int_M \epsilon_{ABCDE}\,\phi^A\,D\phi^B \wedge D\tau^C \wedge D\tau^D \wedge D\tau^E$$

Under broken-phase reduction with auxiliary-field elimination, the radial Higgs mode $\phi^5 = v + \rho$ propagates with healthy Klein-Gordon kinetic term and intrinsic mass scale $m_{\text{AdS}} = 2/L$ from the SO(1,4)/SO(1,3) coset structure. The naive construction $(D\phi)^\dagger(D\phi)$ gives an antisymmetric $\mu\nu$ structure that vanishes as a Klein-Gordon kinetic term and is forbidden (LINT-21). The auxiliary-field structure is forced by SO(1,4) covariance, not added ad-hoc.

Induced at the brane boundary by the bulk CS theory: SO(2,4) $\to$ SO(1,4) boundary conditions produce a gauged WZW model isomorphic to the MM action. The MM action is a theorem of the CS construction, not an axiom. (Paper 0, eq 2.14; boundary induction in Section 2.3; auxiliary-field structure per Langenscheidt 2019 §4.2, SF-MIX-001.)

**DBI sector** (embedding dynamics):

$$S_{\text{DBI}} = -T_3 \int d^4\xi\,\sqrt{-\det\!\big(g^{\text{ind}}_{\mu\nu} + 2\pi\alpha' F_{\mu\nu}\big)}$$

Constant tension $T_3$. The DBI action governs the brane's mechanical posture in the bulk. (Paper 0, eq 2.8)

**Unified action:**

$$S_{\text{total}} = S_{\text{bulk}}[\text{CS},\,\text{SO}(2{,}4)] + S_{\text{brane}}[\text{MM} + \text{DBI},\,T_3 = \text{const},\,v(F_Q)]$$

**v4.11 annotation:** The auxiliary-field reformulation is backed by an explicit Dirac-Bergmann walk. Higgs sub-sector second-class rank 8: primary Darboux pair $(C_\parallel, Z_5)$ contributing rank 2, primary-secondary promotion via three null primary combinations $C_r$ paired with secondary constraints $\mathcal{S}_r = s^{(r)a} \mathcal{A}_a$ contributing rank 6. Auxiliary fields $\phi^a$ eliminated as four canonical pairs. Residual canonical pair $(\phi^5, \Pi_5)$ leaves the radion propagating with $m_{\text{AdS}} = 2/\rho$ in the constant-volume simplification. The full DOF = 3 prediction is conditional only on S-MM-002 (full 44×44 principal-symbol ellipticity); the Higgs sub-sector concern is discharged. References: S-MIX-005, S-MIX-005a, S-MIX-005b ChatGPT reports.

**v4.12 annotation:** The DOF = 3 prediction conditionality is refactored from S-MM-002 (clean factorization of $44 \times 44$ Dirac operator) to S-MM-CR (configuration-robustness theorem for the multiplier left null space rank lift), with the new conditionality explicitly characterized in Paper -1 §VI. The Higgs sub-sector discharge from v4.11 remains intact: ultra-local rank 8 with no derivative-of-delta entries. The principal symbol of the spatial connection block has explicit form with rank 12 and 18-dim kernel; the cross-block lifting structure (torsion lifts 12 broken-row, scalar-gradient lifts 6 longitudinal Lorentz) is structurally identified. The remaining gating question is whether the rank lift is configuration-robust across all physically relevant broken-vacuum configurations. References: S-MM-002 chain reports (preliminary, S-MM-002a/b, S-MM-002α, S-MM-002β, S-MM-002γ).

### 4.4 Symmetry Breaking and the Periodic Addazi-Meluccio Potential [revised v4.8]

The SO(1,4) Higgs field acquires a VEV: $\langle \phi^A \rangle = v \delta^A_4$, breaking SO(1,4) $\to$ SO(1,3). The gauge connection decomposes: $A^{ab}_\mu \to \omega^{ab}_\mu$ (spin connection), $A^{a4}_\mu \to m e^a_\mu$ (tetrad). The 4D Planck mass is generated as $M_P^2 = 32 Y_{\mathrm{MM}} v m^2$ (Addazi-Meluccio eq. 4), with $v \sim 10^{139}$ GeV (K18) and $m \sim 10^{-42}$ GeV (Addazi-Meluccio eq. 5 with observed $\Lambda$). The effective Planck mass is $M^2_{\text{Pl,eff}} = (v_{\mathrm{eff}} + \rho)^2$ as a functional of the state-dependent VEV; the bare $v$ parameter sits at the trans-Planckian scale while the effective value tracks matter coherence. (Paper 0 Section 3.2, Paper -1 v3 in preparation.)

The symmetry-breaking potential takes the periodic Addazi-Meluccio form:

$$V_{\mathrm{SSB}}(\phi) = Y_{\mathrm{SSB}} |J| \left[1 - \cos\!\big(c Y_{\mathrm{MM}}(|\phi| - v)\big)\right]^p$$

where $|J| = \epsilon_{ABCDE} \epsilon^{\mu\nu\rho\sigma} \nabla_\mu \phi^A \nabla_\nu \phi^B \nabla_\rho \phi^C \nabla_\sigma \phi^D \phi^E$ is the pre-geometric volume form ($|J| \xrightarrow{\mathrm{SSB}} -24 v^5 m^4 e$), $c = 128\pi^2$, and $p$ is a positive semi-integer (taken as $p=1$ for the leading harmonic). The sombrero potential $V = \lambda(\phi^A\phi_A - v_0^2)^2$ used in earlier framework versions is superseded.

The radion $\rho(x)$ is the canonically normalized fluctuation $\phi^4 = v + \rho$ around the selected topological minimum. The radion mass derived from the curvature of the periodic potential is

$$\mu_\rho^2 \sim Y_{\mathrm{SSB}} Y_{\mathrm{MM}}^2 m^4 v^5,$$

which is dialed by the choice of $Y_{\mathrm{SSB}}$. The framework selects $Y_{\mathrm{SSB}} \sim 10^{-435}$ to land at $\mu_\rho \sim 1$ MeV, satisfying the F13.2 phenomenology requirement. This hierarchically small coupling is protected against perturbative renormalization by the non-renormalization theorem for periodic operators (S-CC-003 discharge): perturbative matter loops cannot generate trigonometric functions of the background field, so $\delta Y_{\mathrm{SSB}}^{\text{1-loop}} \equiv 0$. The hierarchy is technically natural in the strongest sense.

**The Single New Ingredient (revised v4.8).** The symmetry-breaking VEV is promoted to a functional of the matter sector's Quantum Fisher Information:

$$v = v(F_Q), \qquad v'(F_Q) < 0.$$

This remains equation (1.1) of Paper 0 and the framework's central generalization beyond standard pre-geometric constructions. The state-dependence operates through the species-enhanced heat-kernel coupling $\gamma(\phi^A\phi_A) F_Q$ (Paper 0 v10 §IV.D). This coupling is polynomial in $\phi$ and explicitly breaks the discrete shift symmetry $\rho \to \rho + 2\pi/(c Y_{\mathrm{MM}})$ of the bare AM potential at tree level. The breaking is structurally required: it is the mechanism by which macroscopic coherence ($F_Q \sim N^2$) erases topological barriers and permits the VEV suppression demanded by F13.2 and F19.

The two-regime behavior is now derived rather than axiomatic:

- **Cosmological vacuum** ($F_Q \sim 0$): the $\gamma F_Q$ coupling is dormant. The dominant aperiodic tilt comes from the trace anomaly at $\sim 10^{-141}$ GeV$^3$, negligible against the periodic restoring force ($\sim 10^{13}$ GeV$^3$). Topological sectors are stable. The selected sector $k \sim S_{\mathrm{dS}}$ provides the initial cosmological constant $\Lambda^{(k)}_{\text{initial}}$ (F-CC).
- **ODLRO regime** ($F_Q \sim N^2$): the $\gamma F_Q$ coupling generates an aperiodic slope $\sim \gamma F_Q v$ that is 137 orders of magnitude steeper than the periodic restoring force at threshold parameters. Topological barriers are violently erased; the VEV suppresses, $v \to v_{\mathrm{eff}} \ll v$; F13.2 catalysis activates and F19 collapse channel opens.

When ODLRO is dissolved (F18 Linter excision or thermal exhaust), $F_Q$ relaxes back to ambient, the aperiodic tilt vanishes, and the field settles back into a topological minimum. The selected sector is preserved: the dynamical erasure does not change $k$ but only displaces the field within the cell.

**v4.13 annotation (cosmological prediction).** The framework's formal cosmological prediction is now: static $\Lambda^{(k)}$ within the current cosmic epoch, $w = -1$ at all times within the observable Hubble volume. Three structural mechanisms enforce the static prediction: (i) at cosmological scales the matter sector remains in the DLRO regime with $f \approx 0$ (classical structure formation produces density gradients but not phase coherence, LINT-DLR-1); the $\gamma F_Q$ coupling is therefore dormant and the AM periodic potential governs alone. (ii) Any O(N) operator that could in principle source a slow cosmological gradient (notably the trace channel) is suppressed by $\sim 10^{99}$ against the AM topological barrier height ($\sim 10^{32}$ GeV⁴), per SL-AM-1. (iii) Intra-sector slow-roll quintessence is excluded by mass-window mismatch: the radion sits in $m_\rho \in [1\,\mathrm{meV}, 100\,\mathrm{GeV}]$ while slow-roll would require $m \sim H_0 \sim 10^{-33}$ eV, falsifying slow-roll by at least 30 orders of magnitude (ER-COSM-004). The selected sector $k \sim S_{\mathrm{dS}}$ remains the cosmological constant throughout cosmic history; the DESI DR2 thawing signature, if confirmed at $5\sigma$, falsifies this commitment (B2, v4.13 reclassification).

### 4.5 Operator Uniqueness and the $\gamma$ Coefficient [revised v4.8]

Given the $v = v(F_Q)$ ingredient and the periodic potential structure introduced in §4.4, the remaining question is the operator structure of the state-dependent coupling. The one-loop effective action generated by the $a_4$ Seeley-DeWitt coefficient contains multiple SO(1,4)-scalar, parity-even, diffeomorphism-invariant operators at effective mass dimension 6: the stress-energy trace coupling $\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B T^\mu{}_\mu$, the Weyl curvature coupling $\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B C_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}C^{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$, the gauge trace anomaly coupling $\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B \text{Tr}(F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu})$, and the stress-energy variance coupling $\gamma(\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B)\mathcal{f}_Q$. The first three scale extensively as $O(N)$ with the number of equilibrium degrees of freedom and remain suppressed by the $M_{\text{Pl}}^{-2}$ gravitational coupling, rendering them incapable of breaching the species-scale activation threshold. The variance coupling, evaluated non-perturbatively via the modular Hamiltonian (Formulation B), accesses Donnelly-Freidel boundary edge modes in states with Off-Diagonal Long-Range Order, achieving super-extensive scaling through the $(L/\epsilon)^2$ area enhancement. The $\mathcal{f}_Q$ coupling is therefore the unique operator capable of driving macroscopic suppression of the vacuum expectation value. This uniqueness is thermodynamic rather than Lagrangian.

The variance coupling coefficient is derived from first principles (Paper 0 v10 Section IV.D) as $\gamma = c_{\text{KK}}/(128\pi^2\Lambda_s^2)$ via additive spectral summation of the $a_4$ coefficient over the $N_{\text{species}} = (M_{\text{Pl}}/\Lambda_s)^2$ Kaluza-Klein graviton tower, reduced to stress-energy variance through the classical Einstein equation and collapsed to the species scale via the Dvali-Gomez identity. This places the activation threshold at $F_{Q,\text{crit}} \sim 10^{12}$ to $10^{13}\,\text{GeV}^4$, which the compound matter budget exceeds by 14 to 17 orders of magnitude (K7, SF-D0). The $c_{\text{KK}}$ prefactor is an $\mathcal{O}(1)$ dimensionless number from the massive Fierz-Pauli trace anomaly and carries an overall precision budget on all quantitative framework predictions (OP-CK). The $\gamma F_Q$ coupling is the operator that breaks the discrete shift symmetry of the AM potential (§4.4); shift-symmetry-based protection of the periodic structure is therefore unavailable, and protection proceeds through the kinematic mechanism of K18.

### 4.6 The KK Tower

The AdS$_5$ geometry truncated by the ETW brane contains a KK tower of massive graviton modes: mass gap $m_{\text{KK}} \sim 1/z_0 \sim 10^{-3}\,\text{eV}$ (Dark Dimension); ambient Species Scale $\Lambda_s^{\text{ambient}} = (M_{\text{Pl}}^2 m_{\text{KK}})^{1/3} \sim 2.6 \times 10^8\,\text{GeV}$ (the 5D Planck mass $M_5$, T3.5); number of species below cutoff $N_{\text{eff}} = (M_{\text{Pl}}/\Lambda_s)^2 \sim 2 \times 10^{21}$. The tower serves multiple functions (see Appendix A).

**Erratum E-1 (v4.15).** Earlier displays of this line gave the 4D geometric-mean form $\Lambda_s^{\text{ambient}} \sim \sqrt{M_{\text{Pl}}\, m_{\text{KK}}}$ with $N_{\text{species}} \sim 10^{32}$. That form is stale by five orders in $\Lambda_s$ and ten in $N$: the correct counting is 5D, $\Lambda_s = M_5 = (M_{\text{Pl}}^2 m_{\text{KK}})^{1/3}$. The $\gamma$ derivation and all v4.7+ quantitative results already use the correct 5D values; the error was confined to this display line and the Appendix C notation entry. Audit obligation: any passage citing the stale $N_{\text{species}} \sim 10^{32}$ directly (phenomenological mentions remain in F19, F20, the GUT running discussion, and C20f-ii) is off by $10^{10}$ in $\gamma$ if used quantitatively and must be checked. Logged as the LOW sorry S-E1-AUDIT.

**v4.13 annotation (hydrodynamic chain retracted).** The last three rows in the table above ("BKM regularity," "Hydrodynamic WGC," "Hydrodynamic Distance Conjecture") relied on the Hydrodynamic Swampland Bounds v3 derivation chain, which is retracted as of v4.13. The variance-channel mechanism that anchored that chain ($\gamma$-activation bounding $\text{Var}(K_{\text{mod}})$, an L² quantity) cannot substitute for the pointwise L^∞ amplitude bound the Bounding Box derivation required, by the Sobolev embedding $H^1 \not\hookrightarrow L^\infty$ in 3D (SL-VC-1, LINT-L2-1, ER-WGC-001 via ER-NS-001 cascade). The rows are preserved here for historical continuity but no longer count as cleared proof obligations for Paper 0. WGC compliance is now satisfied statically via the dP_3 Pati-Salam F-theory content (87 codimension-3 Yukawa enhancement loci, matter curves generating a superlattice of fractional confined monopole charges); see reformulated C23-WGC in §4. SDC compliance is now derived via Karch-Randall moduli geometry (DBI-induced metric, $d \sim M_{\text{Pl}} \ln(z_0/L)$, $m_{KK} \sim 1/z_0$); see reformulated C23-SDC in §4, conditional on S-CC-002 closure ($b > 1/(4\pi^2)$). The holographic-spectral-decomposition row remains valid (additive spectral trace is a separate structural fact). The framework's natural derivation surface is geometric and spectral; fluid-regularity theorems are out of jurisdiction (SL-VC-1).

# 2. THE CONSTRAINTS

Derived from Tiers 0 through 4. These are theorems, not choices. Violating any of them means violating the tier from which they derive.

**K1: Two-Channel Decomposition** [from Tier 4.4 + positivity of $T_3$]

The brane stress-energy decomposes exactly into: (i) Trace channel (radial/curvature), which scales as $N$, sources Ricci curvature, and IS gravity; (ii) Traceless antisymmetric channel (angular/torsion), which scales as $f^2 N^2$ for coherent matter and sources torsion via the Cartan equation. This decomposition is an algebraic theorem of the SO(1,4) $\to$ SO(1,3) breaking pattern.

**OP-0 annotation (v4.4, updated v4.7):** The algebraic two-channel decomposition is a theorem of the construction and stands unconditionally. The claim that the traceless channel "scales as $f^2 N^2$" in physical systems is resolved through the explicit first-principles derivation of the variance coupling coefficient $\gamma = c_{\text{KK}}/(128\pi^2\Lambda_s^2)$ via the additive heat kernel spectral trace over the KK graviton tower (SF-D0, Paper 0 v10 Section IV.D). The pole condition $F_{Q,\text{crit}} = 16\pi^2 m_\rho^2 \Lambda_s^2/c_{\text{KK}} \sim 10^{12}$ to $10^{13}\,\text{GeV}^4$ sits 14 to 17 OoM below the compound matter budget ($10^{27}$ to $10^{29}\,\text{GeV}^4$) from density-wave spectral integration (Formulation B, SF-Q1) plus Donnelly-Freidel edge mode area scaling. OP-0 is resolved unconditionally. The gauge KK mode count from the $dP_3$ Laplacian retains its role for precision GUT spectrum work (K8, K10, K11 corrections, baryogenesis inputs) and no longer gates OP-0. The v4.5 gauge-KK-species-lowering mechanism sits in the exclusion reservoir (ER-Q-01) as the right outcome reached through incorrect dimensional reasoning. The decomposition itself, the constraint derivations K2 through K17, and all applications requiring only the construction (F01, F03, F04, F12, F14, F15, F20, F23) are unaffected.

**K2: $G = G_N$ Always** [from K1 + T2.5]

The radial channel couples to all mass-energy with constant $G = G_N = 1/(8\pi v^2)$. Coherence ($F_Q \sim N^2$) enters only the angular channel, sourcing torsion. The gravitational constant is never amplified, modified, or state-dependent. *Any analysis routing $F_Q$ through $G_{\text{eff}}$ is using the wrong channel.*

**K3: $T_3$ is Constant** [from Tier 4.2]

The DBI brane tension $T_3 = 6/(\kappa_5^2 L)$ is fixed by the Israel junction conditions, independent of brane position $z_0$. State-dependence lives in the Higgs VEV $v(F_Q)$, not in $T_3$.

**K4: The Framework is Purely Gravitational** [from T2.7 + T2.8]

Torsion enters through Einstein-Cartan gravity at coupling $G/c^4$ (hierarchy of $10^{40}$ below electromagnetic). The conformal invariance of $F^2$ in 4D prevents any tree-level geometric channel from modifying electromagnetic couplings. The SO(1,4) Higgs is the gravitational Higgs, fully distinct from the electroweak Higgs. The framework cannot modify fermion masses, Bohr radii, or pycnonuclear screening through its own geometry. **Clarificatory clause (tree-level vs. one-loop):** K4 prohibits direct tree-level couplings between the radion/torsion sector and the Standard Model gauge fields in the fundamental Lagrangian. It does not prohibit, and cannot prevent, loop-induced couplings arising from the quantum conformal trace anomaly. The heat kernel integration that derives the state-dependent coupling $\gamma\,(\phi^A\phi_A)\,\mathcal{f}_Q$ necessarily generates terms proportional to $\beta(g)\,F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu}$ through the $a_4(x)$ coefficient (the $\Omega_{\mu\nu}\Omega^{\mu\nu}$ term). These are manifestations of dimensional transmutation, arising from the universal central charges $c_s$, and constitute mathematically inevitable one-loop anomaly couplings rather than fundamental force modifications. The conformal invariance of T2.7 is classically exact; the trace anomaly is the standard quantum breaking of scale invariance in any QFT on curved spacetime. The distinction between "K4-violating" (forbidden: tree-level gauge coupling in the Lagrangian) and "K4-compatible" (mandatory: one-loop trace anomaly from dimensional transmutation) must be maintained in all future analyses.

Adversarial audit confirms: the operator $\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B \text{Tr}(F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu})$ is generated at one loop via the $a_4$ bundle curvature term $(1/12)\,\text{tr}(\Omega_{\mu\nu}\Omega^{\mu\nu})$. This generation is mandatory (conformal trace anomaly) and functionally required by K11 (thermodynamic exhaust channel). The coupling operates at gravitational strength $y_\rho \sim m/M_{\text{Pl}}$ with Coleman-Weinberg corrections to the radion quartic suppressed by $y^4/(16\pi^2) \sim 10^{-67}$. K4 integrity confirmed: no tree-level gauge-matter coupling; loop-level gauge mixing present, phenomenologically required, and gravitationally suppressed.

**K5: Torsion is Non-Propagating** [from Tier 4.7, P3]

Torsion carries zero independent propagating degrees of freedom. The Cartan equation is algebraic (no $\Box T$ kinetic operator). Torsion vanishes instantaneously when sources vanish.

**K6: Bulk is Mandatory** [from T1.5 + Tier 4]

The 5D bulk is mathematically required on three independent axes: Pillar 1 (NEC): 4D cannot balance steep QFI gradients without driving $w < -1$. The bulk absorbs gradients via $T^{(5)}_{M\nu}\,n^M$ flux. Pillar 2 (Scrambling): 4D has no intrinsic geometric spectrum to derive $t_s$. The KK tower provides it. Pillar 3 (KSS): The viscosity bound $\eta/s = 1/(4\pi)$ requires the $(d{+}1)$-dimensional fluid-gravity dictionary.

**K7: Activation Threshold** [from K1 + T3.4 + SF-D0]

The angular channel activates when the matter quantum Fisher information density $\mathcal{f}_Q$ approaches the critical value $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$ derived from the pole condition of the one-loop effective potential:

$$F_{Q,\text{crit}} = \frac{m_\rho^2}{8\gamma}$$

where $\gamma = c_{\text{KK}}/(128\pi^2\Lambda_s^2)$ is the variance coupling coefficient derived in Paper 0 v10 Section IV.D. Substituting:

$$F_{Q,\text{crit}} = \frac{16\pi^2 m_\rho^2 \Lambda_s^2}{c_{\text{KK}}}$$

For the Dark Dimension parameters ($m_\rho \sim 1\,\text{MeV}$, $\Lambda_s \sim 2.6 \times 10^8\,\text{GeV}$), the threshold evaluates to:

$$F_{Q,\text{crit}} \sim \frac{10^{12} \text{ to } 10^{13}\,\text{GeV}^4}{c_{\text{KK}}}$$

where $c_{\text{KK}}$ is an $\mathcal{O}(1)$ dimensionless prefactor from the massive Fierz-Pauli trace anomaly (open problem OP-CK, Appendix D).

The threshold discriminates between extensive and super-extensive scaling regimes. Operators (i), (ii), (iii) in Paper 0 Section IV.D ($\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B T^\mu{}_\mu$, $\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B C_{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}C^{\mu\nu\rho\sigma}$, $\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B \text{Tr}(F_{\mu\nu}F^{\mu\nu})$) are locked to extensive $O(N)$ scaling by the Fluctuation-Dissipation Theorem and remain below the threshold by factors of $10^{15}$ to $10^{25}$ in all equilibrium settings. Only operator (iv), the variance coupling, accesses super-extensive scaling through Donnelly-Freidel edge modes in ODLRO states, reaching the threshold in dense solid-state coherent matter. Dilute systems (BECs, ISM, tabletop experiments) remain at least 50 OoM below threshold due to the ultracold energy scale per particle, regardless of coherence fraction or system size.

The dimensional suppression of $\gamma$ via the species scale $\Lambda_s$ (the bare Planck mass having been replaced by the running species scale through the additive heat kernel trace) is load-bearing for the framework's phenomenological viability. Under the prior assumption $\gamma \sim 1/M_{\text{Pl}}^2$ (v4.4 through v4.6), the threshold stood at $10^{32}\,\text{GeV}^4$, and the compound matter budget of $10^{27}$ to $10^{29}\,\text{GeV}^4$ fell short by 3 to 5 orders of magnitude. The derived $\gamma \sim 1/\Lambda_s^2$ places the threshold at $10^{12}$ to $10^{13}$, which the compound budget exceeds by 14 to 17 orders of magnitude.

The two mechanisms producing the compound budget are:

1. *Density-wave spectral integral:* $\sim 10^{13}$ to $10^{16}\,\text{GeV}^4$. Extensive bulk contribution from matter coherent density fluctuations, treating $\text{Var}(K_{\text{mod}})$ via the Tomita-Takesaki modular flow (Formulation B).

2. *Donnelly-Freidel edge mode area scaling:* $\sim 10^{13}\,\text{GeV}^4$. Super-extensive $(L/\epsilon)^2$ enhancement at the entangling surface for states with Off-Diagonal Long-Range Order.

The combined budget $10^{26}$ to $10^{29}\,\text{GeV}^4$ exceeds $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$ by 13 to 17 orders of magnitude for $c_{\text{KK}} \sim 1$.

**K8: Adiabatic Tracking** [from Tier 4.7]

The radion tracks the moving Higgs minimum adiabatically: $|dv/dt| \ll m_\rho\,v$. Satisfied by $\geq 24$ orders for neutron star formation, $\sim 10^4$ for QGP. Requires $m_\rho \gtrsim \text{MeV}$ ($\lambda \gtrsim 10^{-44}$). Radiative stability is quantified by the one-loop Coleman-Weinberg mass shift: the dominant top-loop contribution yields $\delta m^2_{\text{1-loop}} \sim 10^{-18}\,\text{GeV}^2$, suppressed by geometric Planck-scale Yukawa scaling ($y_t \sim \Lambda_s/M_{\text{Pl,eff}}$). Against the bare radion mass $m^2_\rho \sim 10^{-6}\,\text{GeV}^2$, the ratio is $\delta m^2/m^2_\rho \sim 10^{-12}$: twelve orders of magnitude of margin, without fine-tuning. Any future extension of the boundary matter spectrum must verify that the cumulative Coleman-Weinberg shift remains below $10^{-6}\,\text{GeV}^2$.

**GUT Box occupant input (v4.0).** The confirmed Pati-Salam spectrum contributes to the cumulative Coleman-Weinberg shift: gauge bosons in the adjoint of $SU(4) \times SU(2)_L \times SU(2)_R$, bifundamental matter on genus-96 and genus-10 curves, six Higgs bidoublets at the 87 Yukawa enhancement points, and a KK tower from the Laplacian on $dP_3$ at the LVS minimum ($t_H = 5\,t_E$). Each mode couples to the radion at gravitational strength $y_\rho \sim m/M_{\text{Pl}}$ (K14). The CW contribution from the full GUT spectrum can now be computed against the $10^{-6}\,\text{GeV}^2$ bound. This computation was previously blocked on GUT identification. The spectral zeta function constructible from the $dP_3$ Laplacian eigenvalues provides the required input; the holographic counterterm cancellation (step 4 of the S-G17 computation) remains frontier. Preliminary scaling: the gravitational coupling suppression ($y^4/(16\pi^2) \sim 10^{-67}$ for the top quark) applies uniformly to the GUT spectrum, with the heaviest PS modes at $M_{\text{GUT}} \sim 10^9\,\text{GeV}$ giving $y^2 \sim 10^{-20}$; the cumulative shift is expected to remain well below $10^{-6}\,\text{GeV}^2$, consistent with the existing twelve-order-of-magnitude margin.

**K9: $\Lambda^4_{\min}$ is Dimensional Analysis** [from T1.3]

The saturation floor $\Lambda_{\min} = \hbar c/a$ correctly sets the UV cutoff scale. It does not set the energy budget independently of the coupling constant at each scale ($\alpha_s$, $\alpha_{\text{EM}}$, $\alpha_G$). Works at nuclear scale ($\alpha_s \sim 1$), fails at atomic (off by $274 = 2/\alpha_{\text{EM}}$), fails at gravitational (off by $\sim 10^{47}$).

### Boundary Constraints on the Gauge Sector (The GUT Box)

*The framework is purely gravitational (K4). The SO(1,4) $\to$ SO(1,3) MacDowell-Mansouri sector produces gravity and the radion; it does not produce the Standard Model gauge fields. SU(3) $\times$ SU(2) $\times$ U(1), and any prospective GUT group, operates as external matter confined to the 4D ETW brane (Paper 0, Section 9.4). The framework does not unify gravity with the gauge sector. However, the state-dependent geometry imposes strict mathematical, renormalization group, and topological constraints on any GUT that claims to coexist with the construction. These constraints define the permissible parameter space, the "GUT Box," within which particle physics model-building must operate.*

*The GUT Box is occupied. A systematic survey (GUT Box Population Survey v1.7, seven adversarial Shore cycles, ten architectures evaluated) identified one confirmed viable resident: the F-theory X_{F13} Pati-Salam model on $B_3 = \mathbb{P}(\mathcal{O}_{dP_3} \oplus \mathcal{O}(-H)) \to dP_3$. Three realization pathways were investigated for Pati-Salam in the Dark Dimension: intersecting D6-branes on factorizable tori (blocked by SF-G1, BPS-Chirality Tension), magnetized D-branes with Landau gapping (killed parametrically by SF-G3), and F-theory 7-branes on fibered bases (successful via SF-G2, Divisor Transversality). F-theory is the sole surviving realization pathway. The confirmed model specification follows.*

The 87 codimension-3 enhancement loci, arising from the intersection $C_{(4,2,1)} \cdot C_{(4,1,2)} = (16H - 3\sum E_i) \cdot (6H - \sum E_i) = 87$ on $dP_3$, shatter the rank-1 structure into a generically rank-3 summation. The Dark Dimension constraint inadvertently cured the most significant phenomenological deficiency of the original construction.

**K10: Sliding Unification Bound** [from T3.4 + Tier 4.5 + K6 (Pillar 2)]

The effective UV cutoff of quantum gravity on the brane is the dynamical Species Scale $\Lambda_s \sim (L/z_0)\,M_5$. Under macroscopic quantum coherence ($F_Q \sim N^2$), the suppressed VEV displaces the brane deeper into the AdS$_5$ bulk, driving $\Lambda_s$ below the conventional GUT energy of $10^{16}\,\text{GeV}$. When $\Lambda_s(F_Q) < M_{\text{GUT}}$, the Wilsonian energy domain in which gauge couplings are to unify ceases to exist within the physical geometry. A GUT that insists on a static unification scale above the local cutoff predicts physics in a trans-cutoff regime and is placed in the Swampland by T3.2.

A viable GUT must possess a dynamically sliding unification scale $M_{\text{GUT}}(F_Q)$. The mechanism: as the VEV drops and the brane descends, the KK graviton mass gap $m_{\text{KK}} \sim 1/z_0$ decreases correspondingly. Massive KK species ($N_{\text{species}} \sim 10^{32}$) cross below the renormalization scale, entering the vacuum polarization loops of the gauge fields. The cumulative threshold corrections $\Delta\beta_i^{(\text{KK})}$ steepen the RG trajectories via the modified Callan-Symanzik equation $\mu\,d\alpha_i^{-1}/d\mu = -(\beta_i^{(\text{SM})} + \Delta\beta_i^{(\text{KK})})/2\pi$, forcing the gauge couplings to intersect at a lower energy. The unification scale tracks the descending cutoff: $M_{\text{GUT}}(F_Q) \leq \Lambda_s(F_Q)$ for all physically realizable macroscopic coherent states.

**GUT Box occupant instantiation (v4.0).** The F-theory Pati-Salam model instantiates K10 with specific geometric parameters. The GUT unification scale is set by the volume of the gauge divisor: $M_{\text{GUT}} \sim 1/\sqrt{\text{Vol}(S_{\text{GUT}})}$, where $S_{\text{GUT}} \cong dP_3$ with Kahler moduli stabilized at $t_H = 5\,t_E$ via LVS. The gauge coupling at the PS scale is $\alpha_{\text{PS}}^{-1} = \text{Vol}(S_{\text{GUT}})/\ell_s^4$. The sliding mechanism operates as follows: as the brane descends ($z_0$ increases, $\Lambda_s$ decreases), the KK tower of gauge boson excitations on $dP_3$ (at TeV-scale masses, set by the $dP_3$ Laplacian) enters vacuum polarization loops, steepening the PS beta functions via power-law running. The Ray-Singer analytic torsion of $dP_3$ governs the one-loop threshold corrections. The unification scale tracks the descending cutoff: $M_{\text{GUT}}(F_Q) \leq \Lambda_s(F_Q)$. The TeV-scale gauge KK tower from $dP_3$ and the meV-scale gravity KK tower from the $\mathbb{P}^1$ fiber are cleanly separated by divisor transversality (SF-G2); their contributions to RG running are computationally independent.

*F-theory realization:* In local F-theory SU(5)/SO(10) constructions, GUT breaking to the Standard Model proceeds via $U(1)_Y$ hypercharge flux along the internal directions of the 7-brane. The resulting one-loop threshold corrections are equivalent to the Ray-Singer analytic torsion of the compactification manifold and matter curves, a topological invariant of the Laplacian spectrum on the internal space. As the ETW brane descends, the KK excitations of open strings stretching across intersecting 7-branes generate power-law divergences in the gauge kinetic terms via zeta-function regularization. Above the local KK scale, gauge coupling running transitions from logarithmic to power-law (Dienes-Dudas-Gherghetta mechanism). The Ray-Singer torsion corrections inherently couple to the descending KK modes, ensuring that the sliding unification scale $M_{\text{GUT}}(F_Q)$ dynamically tracks the dropping Species Scale. Heckman, Vafa, Weigand, and Xu have demonstrated that grand unification within the Dark Dimension scenario necessitates a tower of KK excitations of Standard Model gauge bosons in the 1 to 10 TeV range, providing the requisite steep power-law acceleration.

**K11: Trace Anomaly Dependence and Beta Function Non-Vanishing** [from T2.7 + K4 + F13]

The conformal invariance of the 4D gauge kinetic terms (T2.7) forbids the massive scalar radion from coupling to the gauge sector at tree level. General covariance requires the radion to couple universally to ${T^\mu}_\mu$ of the matter sector. For classically massless gauge bosons, ${T^\mu}_\mu = 0$ at tree level. The interaction proceeds exclusively through the quantum conformal trace anomaly:

$${T^\mu}_\mu = \sum_i \frac{\beta(g_i)}{2g_i}\,F^{(i)\mu\nu}F^{(i)}_{\mu\nu}$$

This coupling is a phenomenological requirement. Resolution of the LUNA screening anomaly (F13, C13b, C13c, C13d, C13e) demands that the radion export chaotic thermal noise from driven lattice states into the bulk via the KK tower. The radion accesses the electromagnetic content of the lattice stress-energy through the trace anomaly. If $\beta(g) = 0$ at the relevant scales, as in finite $\mathcal{N} = 4$ Super Yang-Mills or any purely conformal formulation, the trace anomaly vanishes, the radion-gauge coupling is severed, and the thermodynamic exhaust mechanism is destroyed. The lattice loses thermal stabilization against decoherence, falsifying the theory against LUNA data.

Any viable GUT must be strictly non-conformal: $\beta(g_i) \neq 0$ across all physical energy scales relevant to macroscopic coherence and structure formation. The particle content and group representations must be chosen such that the fermionic and scalar loop contributions do not perfectly cancel the gauge boson contribution to the one-loop beta function coefficient.

**GUT Box occupant instantiation (v4.0).** The Pati-Salam spectrum on $dP_3$ contains chiral matter in the $(4,2,1)$, $(\bar{4},1,2)$, $(6,1,1)$, and $(1,2,2)$ representations, alongside the $SU(4) \times SU(2)_L \times SU(2)_R$ gauge bosons. The one-loop beta function coefficients are computable from this specific content. The chiral matter representations ensure $\beta(g_i) \neq 0$ across all relevant energy scales: the fermionic and scalar loop contributions from the bifundamental matter on genus-96 and genus-10 curves produce non-vanishing one-loop coefficients for each gauge factor. The $dP_3$ base geometry provides no conformal window at any scale accessible to the sliding unification mechanism. The radion-gauge coupling through the trace anomaly is active with specific, computable beta function coefficients determined by the PS matter content. K11 is satisfied by construction.

*F-theory realization:* Local F-theory SU(5) and SO(10) models inherently rely on chiral matter representations ($\mathbf{10}$ and $\bar{\mathbf{5}}$ multiplets localized on matter curves, Higgs fields on distinct Riemann surfaces) to replicate the Standard Model spectrum. The presence of these chiral multiplets alongside the adjoint gauge bosons ensures non-vanishing one-loop beta function coefficients $b_i$ across all relevant scales. Warped D3-brane quiver models at smooth singularities, by contrast, risk producing $\mathcal{N} = 4$ Super Yang-Mills ($\beta = 0$ identically), and must be placed at sufficiently complex orientifold singularities to break to $\mathcal{N} = 1$ or $\mathcal{N} = 0$ before they can satisfy K11. F-theory models satisfy K11 natively.

**K12: Topological Dirichlet Confinement** [from Tier 4.1 + K6 + T2.2]

The 5D bulk is governed by a topological Chern-Simons action for SO(2,4) with zero local propagating degrees of freedom. This topological purity eliminates Ostrogradsky ghosts from the bulk interior (T2.2) and preserves the Israel junction conditions governing the bulk-brane energy exchange (K6, Pillar 1).

A GUT constructed from closed strings (e.g., $E_8 \times E_8$ or SO(32) Heterotic models) carries gauge degrees of freedom on strings that propagate freely through the bulk. Embedding such a construction converts the topological bulk into a dynamically active gauge manifold, destroying the thermodynamic isolation on which the NEC protection, scrambling, and KSS bound depend. Pure closed-string gauge architectures are incompatible with the topological bulk requirement.

A viable GUT must be topologically confined to the 4D ETW brane via Dirichlet boundary conditions. Open-string formalisms, including intersecting D-brane stacks (Type IIA/IIB) or F-theory 7-branes, satisfy this requirement by pinning gauge field endpoints to the brane worldvolume.

**GUT Box occupant instantiation (v4.0).** K12 is verified by the 7-brane localization mechanism. The $(SU(4) \times SU(2)^2)/\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge fields are open-string modes confined to $S_{\text{GUT}} \cong dP_3$ via Dirichlet boundary conditions on the 7-brane worldvolume. The gauge sector has zero propagation into the topological SO(2,4) Chern-Simons bulk. Divisor transversality (SF-G2) ensures the gauge divisor sits on a horizontal section of the $\mathbb{P}^1$-fibered base, geometrically transverse to the Dark Dimension fiber. The topological purity of the bulk is preserved: the 7-brane gauge content is rigidly pinned to the ETW boundary locus. The three structural findings from the GUT survey (SF-G1, SF-G2, SF-G3) collectively establish that K12 can be satisfied in the Dark Dimension exclusively through F-theory 7-brane localization on fibered bases; D6-brane factorizable torus constructions and magnetized brane constructions are structurally excluded.

*F-theory realization:* In F-theory, the gauge sector is localized through a strict dimensional hierarchy of singularities pinned to the Karch-Randall ETW boundary. Gauge divisors (8D, 7-brane wrapping a compact 4-cycle such as a del Pezzo surface) carry the non-abelian gauge group ($A_4$ singularity for SU(5), $D_5$ for SO(10)). Matter curves (6D, pairwise 7-brane intersections with enhanced singularity type) trap chiral fermions in the $\bar{\mathbf{5}}$ and $\mathbf{10}$ representations. Yukawa points (4D, triple 7-brane intersections with exceptional enhancement to $E_6$, $E_7$, or $E_8$) generate the specific Yukawa couplings required for fermion mass generation, including the $\mathbf{10} \times \mathbf{10} \times \mathbf{5}$ top quark coupling that perturbative D-brane intersections require non-perturbative instanton effects to produce. The entire Standard Model spectrum is rigidly localized to these singular loci, and anchoring the del Pezzo surface to the ETW boundary locus ensures zero gauge leakage into the topological bulk. The ETW brane functions as a "fat brane" or domain wall supporting the intersecting 7-brane boundary conditions, invoking dynamical cobordism principles to manage the geometric transition from the singular F-theory internal space to the smooth SO(2,4) Chern-Simons interior.

*Intersecting D-brane alternative:* Type IIA/IIB models using stacks of D6-branes wrapping 3-cycles provide strict Dirichlet confinement (open string endpoints tethered to brane worldvolumes). These models produce DDG power-law running and satisfy K10 via annulus/Mobius strip threshold corrections. Their primary friction point is the difficulty of generating the $\mathbf{10} \times \mathbf{10} \times \mathbf{5}$ top Yukawa perturbatively due to anomalous U(1) selection rules; viable constructions require non-perturbative D-brane instantons or adopt Pati-Salam/Flipped SU(5) quiver structures that circumvent this obstruction.
