### Radiative Stability and Cosmological Constraints

**K13: Holographic Casimir Regularization** [from K6 + T3.4 + T1.1]

The cumulative one-loop correction from the $\sim 10^{32}$ KK graviton modes to the radion quartic coupling must be computed via holographic renormalization, not naive additive summation. Under standard additive EFT, the KK tower generates $\delta\lambda \sim 10^{-35}$, which violates the required $\lambda \geq 10^{-44}$. Hamilton-Jacobi boundary counterterms constructed from intrinsic and extrinsic curvatures of the brane absorb power-law divergences into renormalization of $T_3$. The finite Casimir remainder, computed via zeta-function regularization, scales as $\delta\lambda_{\text{finite}} \sim m^4_{\text{KK}}/M^2_{\text{Pl,eff}} \sim 10^{-60}$ under maximal QFI loading. Any analysis using a rigid momentum cutoff without holographic counterterms produces the wrong answer.

**K14: Gravitational Coupling Suppression** [from K4 + T2.8]

The radion couples to all Standard Model fields with gravitational strength: $y_\rho \sim m/M_{\text{Pl}}$. For the top quark, $y_{\rho tt} \sim 7 \times 10^{-17}$. One-loop corrections to $\lambda$ from boundary matter fields are $\delta\lambda \sim y^4/(16\pi^2) \sim 10^{-67}$, negligible against $10^{-44}$. The gravitational gauge sector contributes zero at one loop (first-order BF structure, 44 second-class constraints freeze propagating gauge DOF). The hierarchy $\lambda \sim 10^{-44}$ is radiatively stable in the Dirac sense: corrections are smaller than the parameter. The 't Hooft shift symmetry argument is both unnecessary and formally self-contradictory (the trace anomaly coupling required by K11 breaks it). The protection mechanism is gravitational coupling suppression (K14).

**GUT Box occupant verification (v4.0).** The radion couples to each PS mode at $y_\rho \sim m/M_{\text{Pl}}$. The 7-brane worldvolume modes on $dP_3$ generate one-loop corrections to $\lambda$ at $\delta\lambda \sim y^4/(16\pi^2)$, gravitationally suppressed. Bulk-gauge mixing proceeds at one loop through the trace anomaly, with mixing amplitude suppressed by $M_{\text{Pl}}$; no tree-level gauge leakage into the bulk occurs (verified by divisor transversality and K12 Dirichlet confinement).

**K15: Pre-Geometric Phase Constraint** [from Tier 4.7 + F20]

The radion $\rho(x)$ exists only in the broken SO(1,3) phase. In the unbroken SO(1,4) phase, the Higgs momentum satisfies $\Pi_A \approx 0$ (primary constraint), and no scalar mode propagates. Analyses that assume the radion propagates during inflation or during the pre-geometric epoch are applying the broken-phase field content to the unbroken-phase dynamics. The adiabatic tracking condition $|dv/dt| \ll m_\rho\,v$ applies only post-SSB.

**K16: Species Scale Running Clarification** [from K2 + Hydrodynamic Swampland Bounds v3]

The fundamental Planck mass $M_{\text{Pl}}$ and Newton constant $G_N = 1/(8\pi M_{\text{Pl}}^2)$ are fixed throughout. The quantity that runs is the effective Species Scale $\Lambda_s = M_{\text{Pl}}/\sqrt{N_{\text{eff}}}$, where $N_{\text{eff}}$ counts the Kaluza-Klein species accessible at a given point in the fluid's thermodynamic phase space. The VEV shift $v_{\text{eff}}^2 = v_0^2 - (\gamma/\lambda)\mathcal{f}_Q$ is standard EFT threshold bookkeeping: as more KK modes become thermally accessible ($N_{\text{eff}}$ increases), the EFT validity cutoff drops ($\Lambda_s$ decreases), and the effective symmetry-breaking scale $v_{\text{eff}}$ parameterizing the broken-phase EFT below $\Lambda_s$ is correspondingly reduced. The holographic spectral decomposition establishes that the boundary stress-tensor variance counts bulk KK modes: $\mathcal{f}_Q \sim N_{\text{eff}} \cdot c\,T^8$, where $c$ is the per-species central charge. The identification is exact in the large-$N$ limit. Newton's constant $G_N = 1/(8\pi v_0^2)$ is untouched throughout. Any analysis describing "local $G_{\text{eff}}$ amplification" via VEV suppression from coherence loading is routing $\mathcal{f}_Q$ through the wrong channel and applying the killed mechanism (see Dead list, "$G_{\text{eff}}$ amplification", K2).

**K17: BBN Structural Immunity** [from K7 + K4 + T2.7 + C13e (domain restriction)]

The framework preserves standard Big Bang Nucleosynthesis. During the BBN epoch ($T \sim 30$ to $100$ keV, $t \sim 1$ to $20$ minutes), the primordial plasma is a maximally incoherent, radiation-dominated thermal fluid ($f \approx 0$, $\mathcal{f}_Q \sim N$). Three structural barriers prevent radion activation: (i) The plasma is unbound; it possesses no crystalline lattice, no periodic deformation potential, and no interstitial sublattice to support coherent phonon modes. The radion "Non-Linear Squeezer" mechanism requires a rigid acoustic environment. (ii) The coherence fraction is zero ($f \approx 0$), pinning the VEV at ambient Planck-scale values and keeping the Species Scale at its cosmological maximum. (iii) K4 and T2.7 prohibit the radion from modifying tree-level electroweak cross-sections. The fine-structure constant, the electron mass, and the Beryllium-7 electron capture rate are geometrically immutable. The Cosmological Lithium-7 deficit is outside the framework's explanatory domain. Any future proposed resolution of the Lithium Problem through radion catalysis must first demonstrate how macroscopic quantum coherence forms in an unbound thermal plasma lacking external coherent drivers, which the framework's own axioms structurally forbid.

**K18: Trans-Planckian VEV Suppresses Aperiodic Tilts** [v4.8, from T3.6 + Tier 4 §4.4 reformulation]

Adoption of the Addazi-Meluccio periodic SSB potential (§4.4) forces the bare VEV to be vastly trans-Planckian: $v \sim M_P \cdot S_{\mathrm{dS}} / (Y_{\mathrm{MM}} M_P) \sim 10^{139}$ GeV under standard EFT scaling $Y_{\mathrm{MM}} \sim M_P^{-1}$. The 4D Planck mass is generated through $M_P^2 = 32 Y_{\mathrm{MM}} v m^2$ (Addazi-Meluccio eq. 4) rather than identified with the bare VEV. This trans-Planckian hierarchy provides geometric suppression of all aperiodic radiative corrections to the periodic potential: the field-space distance between adjacent topological vacua remains $\Delta\rho \sim 1/(c Y_{\mathrm{MM}}) \sim 10^{19}$ GeV (Planck-scale), and the topological barrier height $V_{\mathrm{barrier}} \sim \mu_\rho^2 \Delta\rho^2 \sim 10^{32}$ GeV$^4$ at MeV radion mass overwhelmingly dominates aperiodic Coleman-Weinberg slopes ($\sim 10^{-3}$ GeV$^3$ at the cell boundary) by 16 orders of magnitude. The protection mechanism is kinematic (overwhelming barrier height) rather than symmetric: the discrete shift symmetry is broken by the framework's $\gamma(\phi^2) F_Q$ coupling and is not protective. Reference: Gemini CC Radiative Stability Report (April 2026), Addazi-Meluccio 2026. Constrains: F20, F-CC, Tier 4 SSB potential structure. Constrained by: T3.6.

### Structural Findings [GUT Box Survey v4.0; expanded through v4.12]

Three structural findings emerged from the GUT Box Population Survey (v1.7, seven Shore cycles). Each constrains the allowed string constructions within the GUT Box and specifies the viable escape routes.

**SF-G1: BPS-Chirality Tension on Factorizable Tori in the Dark Dimension.** On factorizable $T^6/(\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2')$ orientifolds with standard $N = 1$ BPS conditions, the requirements of Dark Dimension brane localization (all observable brane stacks trivially wrapped on the large torus), three chiral generations (nonzero per-torus intersection numbers), and supersymmetry (brane angle sum equal to zero with positive-definite complex structure moduli) admit no simultaneous solution. The Pigeonhole argument establishes that three stacks with only two allowed orientations on the large torus force at least one pair into parallel alignment, zeroing their intersection number. Demonstrated on all 33 Sabir et al. (2024) intersecting D6-brane models via exhaustive permutation analysis. Scope: blocks D6-brane factorizable torus constructions for any gauge group in the Dark Dimension. Non-factorizable Calabi-Yau compactifications, magnetized brane constructions, and F-theory 7-brane models remain open. Source: Torus Permutation Check report.

**SF-G2: Divisor Transversality Escape from BPS-Chirality Tension.** F-theory gauge localization via horizontal divisors on $\mathbb{P}^1$-fibered base threefolds provides a structural escape from SF-G1. The gauge divisor $S_{\text{GUT}}$ is engineered as a horizontal section of the $\mathbb{P}^1$ fibration, transverse to the macroscopic Dark Dimension fiber. The mechanism operates because: holomorphic divisors in F-theory enforce $N = 1$ SUSY via holomorphicity of the divisor, a condition that does not couple fiber and base directions; the gauge KK tower is determined by the Laplacian on $S_{\text{GUT}}$, independent of the fiber volume; matter curves are geometrically contained within $S_{\text{GUT}}$; gauge couplings depend only on $\text{Vol}(S_{\text{GUT}})$, decoupled from $\text{Vol}(\mathbb{P}^1\text{ fiber})$ at tree level with K14-suppressed one-loop corrections. Sen limit check confirms the BPS-Chirality Tension does not reappear in the Type IIB weak-coupling limit. Scope: applies to any F-theory construction where the GUT divisor can be placed on a horizontal section of a fibered base. The finding is independent of fiber type or gauge group. This is the mechanism by which the GUT Box is occupied. Source: F-Theory X_{F13} Base Geometry Adaptation report.

**SF-G3: Avenue B Parametric Kill (Magnetized Brane Landau Gapping).** The magnetized D-brane Landau gapping mechanism is parametrically unable to achieve Dark Dimension gauge localization on $T^6/(\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2')$ orientifolds. Closed-form bound: $m_{\text{LL}}^{\max} = M_s\sqrt{Q_{\max}/(2\pi N_c A M_s^2)} \sim 710\,\text{MeV}$ for Dark Dimension parameters, below the required 1 TeV threshold. The obstruction is an irreconcilable conflict between kinematics (mass gap scales linearly with flux $N$) and topology (induced RR charge scales linearly with $N$, bounded by the fixed orientifold budget $Q_{\max} \sim 32$). Required flux $N \sim 3.2 \times 10^7$ induces charge $Q \sim 6.4 \times 10^7$ against a budget of 32; the deficit factor is $\sim 2 \times 10^6$. Scope: parametric, applies to any magnetized D-brane model on any factorizable torus orientifold in the Dark Dimension. This eliminates an entire class of potential GUT realizations. Source: Avenue B Flux/Tadpole Budget report.

**SF-D0: Species-Enhanced One-Loop Coefficients in Brane Heat Kernels.** When a bulk Kaluza-Klein tower of $N_{\text{species}}$ fields runs in a one-loop effective action on a brane worldvolume, the local operator coefficients generated by the $a_4$ Seeley-DeWitt expansion inherit a polynomial $N_{\text{species}}$ enhancement. This is a UV enhancement of the Wilsonian coefficient through additive spectral summation, distinct from thermodynamic ($O(N)$ FDT-constrained) enhancement of the matter observable. The enhancement applies specifically to dimension-6 (and higher) operators whose coefficients are generated locally by the $a_4$ (or higher-order) heat kernel terms. The enhancement applies to local Wilsonian coefficients in the effective action, to diagonal spectral traces of the form $\text{Tr}\,e^{-s\Delta}$, and to operator coefficients at coincidence limits $x \to y$. The enhancement does not apply to operator evaluations subject to FDT (these remain $O(N)$), to coherent scattering amplitudes with external KK states (which carry sum rules that can produce cancellations), or to propagators between separated points (governed by Sturm-Liouville orthogonality of the KK wavefunctions). This structural finding generalizes beyond the specific $(\phi^2)\mathcal{f}_Q$ operator: any framework with bulk KK towers generating brane-localized effective operators should check whether the species enhancement applies to the specific operator coefficient under consideration. The operational test: identify whether the object being summed is a spectral trace (enhanced) or a coherent amplitude (cancellation-prone). This distinction underlies LINT-12. Applied to $\gamma$, SF-D0 yields $\gamma = c_{\text{KK}}/(128\pi^2\Lambda_s^2)$, replacing the prior $\gamma \sim 1/(16\pi^2 M_{\text{Pl}}^2)$ estimate and resolving OP-0 unconditionally. Scope: applies to any braneworld construction with a bulk KK tower and brane-localized heat kernel effective action. Source: Georgi-Grant-Hailu (2001), von Gersdorff-Irges-Quiros (2002), Fabinger-Horava (2000), Adjudication Document (April 2026), Paper 0 v10 Section IV.D.

**SF-D1: Even-Degree Parity Kill.** The geometric tadpole budget for X_{F13} over any $dP_n$ base evaluates to $N_{\text{geom}} = (6132 - 228n)/24 = 255.5 - 9.5n$. For even blow-up index $n = 2k$, this expression reduces to $255.5 - 19k$, a strict half-integer. The flux penalty $\frac{1}{2}\int G_4 \wedge G_4$ for integer flux satisfying the three-family Diophantine lock ($a = 3$, $\sum b_i = 15$) evaluates to an even integer ($2|F|^2$, with $|F|^2 = 9 - \sum b_i^2 \in \mathbb{Z}$). The difference between a half-integer budget and an even-integer penalty is inescapably half-integer: $N_{D3} \notin \mathbb{Z}$. This absolute algebraic parity contradiction eliminates $dP_2$, $dP_4$, $dP_6$, and $dP_8$ unconditionally under the X_{F13} architecture with $L = \mathcal{O}(-H)$ twist. Half-integer flux shifts that could in principle restore parity shatter the $a = 3$ Diophantine lock required for three chiral families. Scope: applies to X_{F13} on all even-degree del Pezzo surfaces under the standard twist; parity behavior under other fibers remains indeterminate. Source: Del Pezzo Exclusion Sweep report.

**SF-D2: Gauge Group Fiber-Locking.** The Pati-Salam gauge symmetry $(SU(4) \times SU(2)_L \times SU(2)_R)/\mathbb{Z}_2$ is determined entirely by the X_{F13} toric fiber and is invariant under variation of the base surface within the surviving family $\{dP_3, dP_5, dP_7\}$. The base geometry affects the chiral spectrum details (flux distribution, tadpole margin, Yukawa multiplicity, moduli stabilization landscape) but leaves the gauge group unchanged. The derivation chain for gauge group selection is: framework constraints (K10, K11, K12) $\to$ Dark Dimension boundary conditions (SF-G2 divisor transversality) $\to$ X_{F13} fiber selection $\to$ Pati-Salam. The base choice is a secondary vacuum selection problem within a three-element discrete landscape. Source: Del Pezzo Exclusion Sweep report, Fiber Exclusion Sweep report.

**SF-MIX-001: Auxiliary-field structure required for Higgs sector kinetic term in MMSW gravity.** Scalar kinetic terms in MacDowell-Mansouri-Stelle-West (MMSW) gravity cannot be written as direct $(D\phi)^\dagger(D\phi)$ constructions because the Hodge dual on the gauge-fiber side of the MMSW action produces an antisymmetric $\mu\nu$ structure that vanishes as a Klein-Gordon kinetic term (Langenscheidt 2019, §4.2). The principled resolution is a first-order auxiliary action with the scalar promoted to a 5-vector $\phi^A$; the radial mode $\phi^5$ propagates and the four Lorentz components $\phi^a$ are auxiliary, eliminated by algebraic equations of motion. This structure is forced by SO(1,4) covariance and is the standard treatment in the MMSW literature (Stelle-West 1980, Langenscheidt 2019). The framework's earlier implicit treatment of $-(\partial\rho)^2$ as a directly-displayable Jordan-frame kinetic term was a documentation gap inherited from Stelle-West's terse compensator handling. Generalization: any pre-geometric gauge-theoretic gravity construction with internal gauge symmetry larger than SO(1,3) and a scalar Higgs sector breaking to SO(1,3) faces the same obstruction; the resolution is universally an auxiliary-field formulation forced by the gauge-fiber Hodge dual structure. Scope: applies to any MMSW or related broken gauge-theoretic gravity construction with propagating scalar mode. Source: Langenscheidt 2019 (arXiv:1907.10440), ChatGPT S-MIX-002 Path B Survey (April 2026), ChatGPT S-MIX-004 Weyl Rescaling Verification (April 2026), Path B Resolution Synthesis (April 2026).

**SF-MIX-002 (v4.11): First-order matter Lagrangian primary blocks have rank 2 with secondary promotion of null primaries.** Primary-primary Dirac sub-blocks for first-order matter Lagrangians (where canonical momenta are linear in fields rather than velocities) generically have rank 2 in a 5-dimensional auxiliary sector, not full rank. The Darboux structure decomposes the primary constraints into one second-class pair plus null combinations orthogonal to the kinetic projection vector $f_a$. The null primary combinations are not gauge generators; they are promoted to second-class via brackets with the secondary constraints generated by their own preservation under the Hamiltonian. The promotion mechanism depends on the algebraic structure of the auxiliary EOM, specifically the identity coefficient on the auxiliary fields. Operational test: given a first-order Lagrangian for fields $(\phi^A) = (\phi^5, \phi^a)$ with one component propagating and the rest auxiliary, count primary constraints via $\Pi_A - \partial L / \partial \dot{\phi}^A = 0$, compute the primary-primary Dirac block, and identify null directions orthogonal to the kinetic projection. The expected rank is $2k$ where $k$ is the number of velocity-coupling kinematic projections. Promotion of null primaries proceeds through secondary constraints with brackets $M_{rs} = -G_{rs} \delta^3$ on the orthogonal subspace. Scope: applies to MMSW gravity with auxiliary scalars (Langenscheidt 2019), BF theory with matter, Stelle-West compensators, Dirac fermions in canonical analysis, and any first-order matter Lagrangian where auxiliary fields are eliminated via algebraic EOMs. Distinct from the standard Dirac-Bergmann pattern for second-order Lagrangians, where primary blocks are typically full rank. Source: ChatGPT S-MIX-005a Report (April 2026), ChatGPT S-MIX-005b Report (April 2026), Langenscheidt 2019 (arXiv:1907.10440).

**SF-MIX-003 (v4.11): Orthogonal projection of algebraic auxiliary EOM produces primary-secondary bracket rank determined by orthogonal subspace dimension.** When secondary constraints from preservation of null primaries take the form $\mathcal{S}_r = s^{(r)a} \mathcal{A}_a$ with $\mathcal{A}_a = \eta_{ab} \phi^b + B_a(\text{lower-order})$, the bracket matrix with the original null primaries is $M_{rs} = -s^{(r)a} s^{(s)b} \eta_{ab} \delta^3 + \Delta_{rs}$, the Gram matrix of basis vectors $s^{(r)}$ in the internal metric restricted to the orthogonal complement $H_f = \{u^a : u^a f_a = 0\}$. Generic rank equals $\dim H_f$. Lower-order covariantization terms shift the inhomogeneous part of $\mathcal{A}_a$ but do not affect the identity coefficient on $\phi^a$, hence do not threaten rank generically. Degeneracy conditions: $f_a = 0$ (kinetic projection vanishes), $f_a f^a = 0$ (null kinetic projection in Lorentzian internal metric), or accidental tuning of lower-order background. None of these are generic broken-vacuum configurations. Constant-volume simplifications ($D_\mu e^\mu_a = 0$) are convenience for the reduced scalar equation, not structural requirements for rank. Scope: applies wherever first-order matter Lagrangians produce algebraic auxiliary EOMs with identity coefficient on auxiliary fields. Operational test: identify the kinetic projection vector $f_a$, compute the orthogonal complement, verify the Gram matrix is invertible on a basis of the complement. Source: ChatGPT S-MIX-005b Report (April 2026), Langenscheidt 2019 (arXiv:1907.10440).

**SF-MM-002 (v4.12): Isolated 30×30 spatial connection symbol has rank 12 with 18-dimensional kernel.** In the broken phase $\langle \phi^A \rangle = v \delta^A_4$, the principal symbol of the multiplier preservation operator restricted to the 30 spatial connection primary constraints $Z^i_{AB}$ has the explicit form $\sigma_{ZZ}^{i,ab;l,cd}(\xi) = 8i\alpha (v+\rho) \epsilon_{abcd} \epsilon^{0ikl} \xi_k$ with $\sigma_{ZZ}^{i,a4;l,CD}(\xi) = 0$. Factorization: $\sigma_{ZZ} = 8i\alpha (v+\rho) *_{\text{int}} \otimes \text{curl}_\xi$. For $\xi \neq 0$, rank is 12 with 18-dimensional left kernel decomposing as 6 longitudinal Lorentz modes plus 12 broken-sector $a4$ modes. The 6 longitudinal directions are $R^{i,ab}_\Lambda = \xi^i \Lambda^{ab}$ for antisymmetric $\Lambda^{ab}$. The 12 broken-row directions are $R^{i,a4}_X = X^{ia}$ for arbitrary $X^{ia}$. Full ellipticity therefore requires cross-block contributions: torsion cross-block $\sigma_{TZ}^{a,jk;b4,l}(\xi) = (i/m)\delta^a_b(\delta^l_k \xi_j - \delta^l_j \xi_k)$ structurally lifts the 12 broken-row directions; the 6 longitudinal Lorentz directions require the scalar-gradient cross-block whose form depends on the explicit $\mathcal{F}_i$. Source: S-MM-002 Preliminary Report (April 2026), S-MM-002α/β reports.

**SF-MM-003 (v4.12): Subprincipal entries in MMSW multiplier matrix are lower differential order than the principal curl symbol.** The connection-dependent subprincipal contribution $U_M$ from the SO(1,4) covariant derivative $D_j$ in the Frechet variation of $Z^i_{AB}$ is ultra-local (order zero in spatial derivatives) while the principal curl symbol $\sigma_M$ is order one. Therefore $U_M$ does not upgrade the principal-symbol rank used in the ellipticity problem. It can affect frozen-background multiplier solving as an algebraic lower-order term, but the principal rank stays at the curl-driven value (12 in the 30-component spatial connection block). Tetrad-derivative entries in the Higgs-primary multiplier columns ($\delta f_a / \delta A_i^{b4}$) are similarly ultra-local. The DOF reduction beyond the principal rank therefore requires a configuration-robustness theorem (S-MM-CR) that the standard MM literature does not derive; the rank lift from 18 to the physical secondary count is generically background-sensitive. This is a generic feature of MMSW canonical analyses with auxiliary scalars, not specific to the Langenscheidt formulation. The standard MM literature on Hamiltonian constraint analysis presupposes the configuration-robustness condition without explicit derivation. Source: S-MM-002γ Report (April 2026).

### GUT Box Base Landscape [v4.1]

The confirmed F-theory Pati-Salam model is viable on three del Pezzo base surfaces. The $dP_3$ model (v4.0 specification) remains the optimal member of this family.

| Base ($S$) | $(-K)^2$ | $h^{1,1}$ | $\chi(Y_4)$ | $N_{\text{geom}}$ | Flux Vector | $N_{D3}$ | $N_Y$ | Flux Isotropy | Status |
|-----------|----------|-----------|-------------|-------------------|-------------|----------|-------|--------------|--------|
| $dP_3$ | 6 | 4 | 5448 | 227 | $3H - 5(E_1 + E_2 + E_3)$ | 95 | 87 | Perfect ($15/3 = 5$) | Optimal baseline |
| $dP_5$ | 4 | 6 | 4992 | 208 | $3H - 3\sum_{i=1}^5 E_i$ | 136 | 81 | Perfect ($15/5 = 3$) | Viable alternative |
| $dP_7$ | 2 | 8 | 4536 | 189 | $3H - 3E_1 - 2\sum_{i=2}^7 E_i$ | 141 | 75 | Broken ($15/7 \notin \mathbb{Z}$) | Marginal (asymmetric flux, stressed D-term) |

$dP_3$ retains its status as the geometric global optimum: maximum Yukawa multiplicity (87 loci), perfect flux isotropy, deepest tadpole margin, and cleanest LVS moduli stabilization. $dP_5$ is a serious alternative with identical D-flat relation ($t_H = 5t_E$) and isotropic flux. $dP_7$ survives formally but with structural disadvantages: forced flux asymmetry breaks the $S_n$ permutation symmetry of exceptional divisors, complicating instanton hierarchy and LVS stabilization.

The gauge group is identical across all three bases (SF-D2). The vacuum selection among $\{dP_3, dP_5, dP_7\}$ is a moduli landscape problem, secondary to the gauge group derivation.

### Toric Fiber Exclusion Status [v4.1]

The Klevers et al. classification (arXiv:1503.02068) catalogs 16 toric hypersurface fibrations. All 16 have been evaluated against the pre-filter stack (K10, K11, SM-embedding). Eight are killed; one is confirmed; seven are indeterminate pending computational resolution.

| Fiber | Gauge Algebra | SM-Embedding | K10/K11 | Geometric Evaluation | Verdict |
|-------|--------------|-------------|---------|---------------------|---------|
| X_{F1} | Trivial | FAIL | FAIL | N/A | KILLED (pre-filter) |
| X_{F2}, X_{F3}, X_{F4} | Discrete/Abelian | FAIL | FAIL | N/A | KILLED (pre-filter) |
| X_{F5}, X_{F6} | SU(5) variants | PASS | PASS | Missing fiber-specific $\chi(Y_4)$ and matter curves | INDETERMINATE |
| X_{F7} | Low-rank Abelian | FAIL | FAIL | N/A | KILLED (pre-filter) |
| X_{F8}, X_{F9}, X_{F10} | SU(5) variants | PASS | PASS | Missing fiber-specific data | INDETERMINATE |
| X_{F11} | $SU(3) \times SU(2) \times U(1)$ | PASS | PASS | Missing fiber-specific data | INDETERMINATE |
| X_{F12}, X_{F14}, X_{F15} | Low-rank/Discrete | FAIL | FAIL | N/A | KILLED (pre-filter) |
| X_{F13} | $(SU(4) \times SU(2)^2)/\mathbb{Z}_2$ | PASS | PASS | Fully mapped | **SURVIVES** |
| X_{F16} | $(SU(3)^3)/\mathbb{Z}_3$ | PASS | PASS | Missing fiber-specific data | INDETERMINATE |

**Critical path for resolution:** The seven indeterminate fibers require fiber-specific Euler characteristics and matter curve classes computed on $\mathbb{P}^1$-fibered del Pezzo bases. The toric data for all 16 fibers is cataloged in arXiv:1503.02068 (Tables 3 through 6, Appendix B). The computation is executable via FTheoryTools (Julia/OSCAR, arXiv:2506.13849), which implements the Batyrev-Borisov machinery and can resolve arbitrary toric hypersurface fibrations over specified bases. The computation consists of 21 fiber/base pairs (7 fibers $\times$ 3 bases). Estimated scope: weeks-scale with software, intractable by hand.

**Structural note (SF-D2):** If any indeterminate fiber survives, it produces a different gauge group (SU(5), direct SM, or Trinification). The gauge group selection would then fracture into a discrete landscape. If all seven are killed, the Pati-Salam gauge group is derived from boundary topology plus quantum gravity consistency. The resolution of this indeterminacy is the single highest-priority open computation in the GUT Box program.

# 3. THE FUNCTIONS

Functions are WHAT must hold, given the construction and constraints. Each responds to one or more Tier 2.5 breakdowns while respecting Tiers 0 through 2 constraints. Functions are listed WITHOUT their implementing contracts. Contracts follow in Part IV.

**F01: Gravity Emerges from Symmetry Breaking**
**Addresses:** B7 (no quantum gravity)
**Statement:** SO(1,4) $\to$ SO(1,3) SSB produces Einstein-Cartan gravity with a massive scalar radion and algebraically determined torsion. Three propagating DOF: two graviton polarizations + one scalar.
**Constrained by:** K1, K2, K5

**F02: Coherent Matter Couples to Geometry**
**Addresses:** B13 (hyperon puzzle), B15 (failed supernovae)
**Statement:** Phase-locked matter generates additional angular stress proportional to $f^2 N^2$ through the hypermomentum tensor. This stress sources torsion via the Cartan equation, suppresses the local effective Planck mass, and provides structural support beyond nuclear degeneracy pressure. $G$ remains $G_N$.
**Constrained by:** K1, K2, K7
**OP-0 conditionality (v4.4, updated v4.5):** The quantitative torsion amplitude depends on $\mathcal{f}_Q$ achieving super-extensive scaling via the modular Hamiltonian formulation (SF-Q1). Conditional on gauge KK mode count from FTheoryTools computation (see OP-0 resolution, v4.5).

**F03: The Geometry Stays Thermodynamically Stable**
**Addresses:** B1 (singularities, partial), B4 (information paradox, partial)
**Statement:** Under steep QFI gradients, the geometry maintains NEC compliance on the brane. The bulk provides the thermodynamic reservoir.
**Constrained by:** K6 (Pillar 1)

**F04: Scrambling Has a Timescale**
**Addresses:** B15 (failed supernovae), B14 (mass gap)
**Statement:** The vacuum processes dumped $O(N^2)$ correlations over a finite scrambling time $t_s$, derived from the KK tower mass spectrum. $t_s = (R_s/c)\ln(S_{\text{BH}})$ for macroscopic systems. The naive Margolus-Levitin application is a category error (T1.6).
**Constrained by:** K6 (Pillar 2)

**F05: Massive Neutron Stars Are Supported**
**Addresses:** B13 (hyperon puzzle)
**Statement:** Neutron stars above $2\,M_\odot$ receive structural support from torsion pressure in the superfluid core composing with nuclear fluid pressure, each carrying $\sim 50\%$ of the central load at $M_{\max}$. $G = G_N$ throughout.
**Constrained by:** K1, K2, K5, T2.6
**Calibration:** $\rho_{\text{sf}} = 2\rho_0$ (unique value satisfying $M_{\max}$, $R_{1.4}$, $\Lambda_{1.4}$ simultaneously; consistent with $^3P_2$ transition).

Conditional on gauge KK mode count from FTheoryTools computation (see OP-0 resolution, v4.5).
**v4.15 status (matter-sector exclusion record):** Moved to the exclusion reservoir as part of the nuclear-pasta activation chain. OP-0-ACTIVATION is dead: a neutron-star superfluid is an equilibrium substrate whose Var(T) is volume-law O(N) by FDT, 12 to 25 orders below the $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$ threshold the torsion pressure requires. The two-channel support claim ($\sim 50\%$ torsion at $M_{\max}$) is not available from the activated pole. Standard nuclear EOS support (C05a) is unaffected; the framework's neutron-star mass ceiling now rests on conventional physics plus the surviving cosmological commitments. Reactivation requires passing the exclusion record's three gates (a coupling other than species-summed $G_N$, a real-observable vehicle, substrate survival of the required coherence); the surviving live route for the matter sector is the rescue-trellis torsion-Lagrangian calculation (S-TORSION-LAGRANGIAN), not equilibrium superfluid activation.

**F06: Stellar Death is Rate-Dependent**
**Addresses:** B14 (mass gap), B15 (failed supernovae)
**Statement:** Geometric failure occurs when the free-fall rate exceeds the scrambling rate ($t_{\text{ff}} < t_s$). The mode of failure depends on which channel dominates: tear (thermal, radial) or puncture (coherent, angular).
**Constrained by:** K1, F04

**F07: The Mass Gap Exists**
**Addresses:** B14 (lower mass gap)
**Statement:** The $2.5$ to $5\,M_\odot$ mass gap arises from the tear/puncture dichotomy. Tears from isolated collapse recruit envelope mass, jumping to $\geq 5\,M_\odot$. Punctures from mergers carry no envelope, landing at $\sim 2.5$ to $3\,M_\odot$.
**Constrained by:** F06

**F13: LUNA Screening Is a Many-Body Response, Not a Geometric Modification**
**Addresses:** B12 (LUNA screening anomaly)
**Statement:** The conformal invariance of the 4D Maxwell action (T2.7) and the Higgs identity (T2.8) forbid all tree-level geometric routes to modified electromagnetic coupling. The fine-structure constant $\alpha$, the electron mass $m_e$, and the bare Coulomb potential $V(r) = Z_1 Z_2 e^2/r$ are geometrically immutable. The LUNA anomaly demands an explanation operating entirely within standard electromagnetism, modulated by many-body condensed matter physics.

Three pathways evaluated:

(1) WKB metric deformation (kinematic shift): DEAD. Conformally flat induced brane metric renders the Gamow tunneling integral exactly invariant. Perturbative regime: $\sim 4\,\mu\text{eV}$ ($10^8$ undershoot). Geometric truncation: erases barrier ($10^9$ overshoot). No stable intermediate.

(2) Loop-level KK vacuum polarization: Plausible but sub-leading. $\delta V \sim V\,(q/\Lambda_s)^2 \sim 0.3\,\text{eV}$ at Gamow momentum transfer $q \sim 10\,\text{keV}$. Three orders of magnitude below target.

(3) Nonlinear many-body electron response: Leading candidate. Coherent phonon driving in metallic targets triggers nonlinear collective electron response beyond linear Thomas-Fermi. Framework-independent.

The massive scalar radion $\rho(x)$ may serve as a thermodynamic catalyst: its coupling to ${T^\mu}_\mu$ of driven acoustic phonons could stabilize extreme phonon amplitudes against thermal decoherence by exporting chaotic noise to the bulk via the KK tower. Speculative; requires quantitative verification.

**Constrained by:** K4, K7, T2.7, T2.8

**OP-0 annotation (v4.4, updated v4.7):** The radion catalysis mechanism (F13.2) and all condensed-matter phenomenology derived from it (C13a through C13e) require VEV suppression, which operates through the pole condition $F_{Q,\text{crit}} = 16\pi^2 m_\rho^2 \Lambda_s^2/c_{\text{KK}}$. The compound budget exceeds this threshold by 14 to 17 OoM under the derived $\gamma \sim 1/\Lambda_s^2$ (Paper 0 v10 Section IV.D, SF-D0). OP-0 resolves unconditionally; the precision of the predicted screening enhancements carries an overall $\mathcal{O}(1)$ uncertainty from the $c_{\text{KK}}$ prefactor (OP-CK).

**v4.15 status (matter-sector exclusion record, supersedes the v4.7 reading above).** OP-0 splits. The pole condition and the derived $\gamma$ stand (OP-0-COUPLING). The compound-budget claim is retracted (OP-0-ACTIVATION dead): the "$10^{27}$ to $10^{29}$ GeV⁴" figure rested on super-extensive Var(T), which is volume-law O(N) by FDT for the driven metallic lattices F13.2 targets, since the active phonon mode is a classical collective coordinate carrying $F_Q$ in the decohered channel (LINT-DLR-1), not the coherent geometric channel. F13 and F13.2, with the contract chain C13a through C13e, move to the exclusion reservoir governed by the matter-sector exclusion record. The LUNA anomaly's standard-electromagnetism / many-body framing (pathway 3, framework-independent) survives as ordinary condensed-matter physics; only the radion-catalysis route is reservoired. Reactivation under the three-gate test; the rate channel is dead, with a transient EXHAUST channel for nuclear de-excitation left open and gated on S-EXHAUST-COHERENCE (v4.16, SF-DG-013).

#### F13.2: Condensed-Matter Phenomenology of Resonant Radion Catalysis

**Addresses:** B12 (LUNA screening anomaly), and extends to $Z = 28$ proton-capture regimes.

The phenomenological application of the radion trace coupling to condensed matter systems proceeds through three sequential mechanisms, each validated by dedicated quantitative stress tests.

**Resonant Mode Localization (C13c).** The initial feasibility analysis identified a severe global power bottleneck: suppressing the geometric VEV uniformly across a macroscopic lattice requires terawatt-class continuous power, which would vaporize the target long before the radion coupling activates. The resolution abandons global suppression entirely. Dual-laser stimulation tuned to the longitudinal optical phonon resonance of the interstitial sublattice (8 to 12 THz for PdD$_x$) establishes a phase-locked standing wave whose QFI density concentrates as $\sin^4(kx)$ at the geometric antinodes. The active volume fraction per unit cell is $\sim 7 \times 10^{-5}$, yielding a Localization Gain Factor $G_{\text{loc}} \sim 10^6$ to $10^7$. Within these microscopic antinodal volumes, the local QFI breaches the $10^{-6}$ VEV suppression threshold using standard kW-class laboratory laser setups. The massive radion's short Yukawa range (Compton wavelength $\sim 0.002\,\text{\AA}$ for $m_\rho \geq \text{MeV}$) confines its mechanical restoring force precisely to the $0.1\,\text{\AA}$ antinodal regions, transforming the mass penalty into a stabilization asset.

**Heavy Fermion Amplification (C13d).** The non-linear Thomas-Fermi scaling relation $U_e = U_{e,0}\,\sqrt{m^*/m_e}\,(n_e/n_{e,0})^{1/6}$ determines the screening potential achievable within the clamped lattice. For PdD$_x$ ($Z = 1$ fusion), localized compressions of $10^4$ to $10^6$ and effective masses of $\sim 12\,m_e$ yield screening shifts of 417 to 890 eV, reproducing the LUNA anomaly window. For $Z = 28$ ($p + \text{Ni} \to \text{Cu}$), the 3,000 eV minimum demands $m^* \geq 132\,m_e$, which exceeds the structural capacity of pure 3d transition metals. The framework resolves this via Cerium doping: CeNi$_5$ introduces localized 4f orbitals whose hybridization with the conduction band is governed by the Periodic Anderson Model. The radion clamp simultaneously enhances the hybridization matrix element $V_{kf}$ (via spatial compression) and amplifies the local density of states $\rho(E_F)$ by a factor of 100 (via ponderomotive electron bunching). This dual perturbation drives the system into a Hyper-Kondo regime, distinct from conventional high-pressure intermediate valence collapse, sustaining composite quasiparticle masses of 500 to 1000 $m_e$ and a total screening potential of $\sim 5{,}814\,\text{eV}$.

*Note on stellar context:* The compression factors $C = 10^4$ to $10^6$ apply strictly to weakly degenerate metallic lattices (LUNA context) where Fermi energy is $\sim$ eV. In degenerate stellar plasma at nuclear density ($E_F \sim 100$ MeV), Fermi pressure caps compression at $C \sim 10^3$ (see C21b). The LUNA predictions remain valid for their target context.

**Aneutronic Coherence Pumping (C13e).** The ${}^7\text{Li}(p,\alpha){}^4\text{He}$ reaction ($Q = 17.3\,\text{MeV}$) serves as an internal parametric amplifier. Within the radion-clamped phase space, the heavy alpha particles' stopping power is funneled exclusively into the driven coherent phonon mode rather than broadband thermal noise. The resulting zero-entropy energy is exported via stimulated emission into the 5D KK tower. The thermodynamic race between internal heating ($\tau_{\text{th}} \sim 1$ to $10\,\text{ps}$) and geometric cooling ($t_s \sim 0.2\,\text{ps}$) is won decisively by the exhaust, preserving both the lattice integrity and the Kondo singlet against the MeV-scale energy dump.

**Constrained by:** K4 (purely gravitational radion), K6 (bulk mandatory for NEC and scrambling), T2.7 (conformal invariance protects gauge sector), C13a, C13b (existing screening contracts)

**v4.15 status (matter-sector exclusion record).** F13.2 and its three mechanisms (C13c resonant mode localization, C13d heavy-fermion amplification, C13e aneutronic coherence pumping) are in the exclusion reservoir. The bottleneck is the susceptibility exclusion (SL-SUSC-1): the localized standing-wave mode must be simultaneously phase-rigid enough to hold the antinodal QFI and soft enough to source the geometric channel, which is one susceptibility pulled in two directions; equilibrium and driven warm substrates supply only volume-law variance. The local QFI breach of the suppression threshold does not survive the FDT/decoherence audit. C13a, C13b, C13sub struck alongside (see §4). What survives outside the framework: the LUNA window via standard nonlinear Thomas-Fermi screening. The transient nuclear-de-excitation exhaust (a different channel, conceding the rate to conventional physics) is the one live LENR route, gated on S-EXHAUST-COHERENCE (v4.16).

**F17: Horizons Are Zero-Resolution Surfaces**
**Addresses:** B1 (singularities), B4 (information paradox)
**Statement:** At $R_s$, radial suppression drives $\Lambda_s \to 0$. The geometry carries zero resolution. Gravitational time dilation = $\Lambda_s(r)/\Lambda_s(\infty)$. Clocks stop at the horizon because the vacuum has zero processing bandwidth.

The excision creates a codimension-2 termination surface whose area is a Casimir invariant of the corner symmetry algebra. The termination surface is mass-dependent (scales with $R_s$), replacing the dimensionless GR singularity with a finite-area geometric object. The 4D description (Donnelly-Freidel edge modes) and 5D description (ETW defect) are dual representations of the same boundary. **F18: The Linter Censors Insolvent Geometry**
**Addresses:** B1 (singularities), B4 (information paradox)

The 4D mechanism operates via Donnelly-Freidel edge modes (local Hilbert space factorization). The 5D dual is the Karch-Randall ETW defect.

The Linter's excision mechanism connects directly to black hole thermodynamics. The termination surface it creates carries exactly the edge mode DOF needed to account for Bekenstein-Hawking entropy: the "scar tissue" IS the edge mode surface. The 4D Donnelly-Freidel description (C18a) and the 5D ETW defect description (C18b) produce the same entropy from opposite directions: edge mode counting from below, RT surface anchoring from above. F17 provides the LOCATION of the termination surface, F18 provides the MECHANISM that creates it, and C18a/C18b provide the DESCRIPTION of what lives on it.
**Constrained by:** K6

**F19: Geometric Wavefunction Collapse**
**Addresses:** B17 (measurement problem, Gran Sasso falsification)
**Statement:** The Displacement Geometry framework rescues the Penrose-Diosi concept of gravitationally induced objective wavefunction collapse from the 2021 Gran Sasso experimental falsification. Three structural elements compose the resolution.

**(i) Dynamically Accelerated DP Timescale.** The framework preserves the exact mathematical form of the DP collapse equation $\tau_{\text{DP}} \sim \hbar/\Delta E_G$ but radically amplifies the gravitational self-energy through the state-dependent coupling. As a macroscopic system transitions from a thermal state ($F_Q \sim N$) to a coherent superposition ($F_Q \sim N^2$), the QFI spike suppresses the local geometric VEV $v(F_Q)$, driving a localized surge in $G_{\text{eff}} = 1/[8\pi\,v(F_Q)^2]$. The gravitational self-energy is calculated using this dynamically amplified coupling: $\Delta E_G^{(\text{eff})} = G_{\text{eff}} \int\!\!\int d^3x\,d^3x'\,[\delta\rho(x)\,\delta\rho(x')]/|x - x'|$. Because $G_{\text{eff}} \gg G_N$ inside the superposition volume, the collapse timescale plummets precisely when macroscopic coherence forms. Gravity executes the collapse as Penrose originally envisioned; the state's own entanglement entropy catalyzes the rate.

**(ii) The Heisenberg Cut as a Geometric Threshold.** The framework provides an absolute structural boundary between quantum and classical regimes. As QFI forces the brane to dimple deeper into the AdS$_5$ bulk, the local Species Scale $\Lambda_s$ drops. Bounded by the Margolus-Levitin theorem, the temporal pixel of the local geometry is $\delta t = \hbar/\Lambda_s$. When $\Lambda_s$ drops below the operational energy scale of the superposition ($E_{\text{sup}}$), the temporal pixel exceeds the dynamical timescale of the quantum system. The local vacuum geometry loses the information-processing bandwidth required to sustain the coherent entanglement. This topological insolvency triggers Linter excision (F18) via Donnelly-Freidel edge modes, forcing local Hilbert space factorization. The state vector is reduced to a classical mixed state. With coherence dissolved, $F_Q$ relaxes to $O(N)$, the VEV recovers, and the brane flattens.

**(iii) Gran Sasso Evasion via Dark Thermodynamic Exhaust.** The collapse energy does not remain within the 4D manifold. The standard DP model was falsified because, in a closed 4D system, stochastic momentum diffusion on charged particles produces unavoidable electromagnetic bremsstrahlung. In the Displacement Geometry framework, the observable universe is an open thermodynamic system: the ETW brane embedded in AdS$_5$. The Israel junction conditions permit energy-momentum flux across the boundary: $\nabla_\mu T^{\mu}{}_\nu\big|_{\text{brane}} = -T^{(5)}_{M\nu}\,n^M$. The steep stress-energy gradients generated by the collapsing QFI load are bled directly off the brane into the 5D bulk, where they excite the dense Kaluza-Klein graviton tower ($N_{\text{species}} \sim 10^{32}$ massive spin-2 modes, $m_{\text{KK}} \sim 10^{-3}\,\text{eV}$). The KK tower absorbs and scrambles the dumped coherence energy over the fast-scrambling time $t_s \sim (\hbar/\Lambda_s)\ln(N_{\text{species}})$. The collapse energy dissipates exclusively as soft, massive spin-2 dark radiation in the bulk.

The electromagnetic sector is structurally shielded by the exact conformal invariance of the 4D Maxwell action (T2.7). Under the geometric dimpling (brane displacement to larger $z_0$), the induced metric undergoes conformal rescaling by the warp factor $\Omega = L/z_0$. In the Maxwell action $\int d^4x\,\sqrt{-g}\,F^{\mu\nu}F_{\mu\nu}$, the determinant contributes $\Omega^4$ while the two inverse metrics contribute $\Omega^{-2}$ each: $\Omega^4 \times \Omega^{-2} \times \Omega^{-2} = 1$. The tree-level coupling of the photon field is mathematically blind to the geometric dimpling. Zero 4D X-ray bremsstrahlung is generated.

**Constrained by:** K4 (purely gravitational), K6 (bulk mandatory: Pillar 1 for NEC, Pillar 2 for scrambling), T2.7 (conformal invariance), F18 (Linter excision mechanism)

**OP-0 annotation (v4.4, updated v4.7):** The dynamically amplified $G_{\text{eff}}$ collapse mechanism (C19a) and the Species Scale threshold (C19b) both require $\mathcal{f}_Q$ to approach the pole condition in the superposition volume. Under the derived $\gamma \sim 1/\Lambda_s^2$ (Paper 0 v10 Section IV.D, SF-D0), $F_{Q,\text{crit}} \sim 10^{12}$ to $10^{13}\,\text{GeV}^4$ is reached by mesoscopic coherent systems via density-wave spectral integration plus edge mode contributions, and the collapse channel activates without reliance on an independent gauge KK species count. OP-0 resolves unconditionally; the exact collapse timescale for specific mesoscopic systems carries the $c_{\text{KK}}$ prefactor uncertainty (OP-CK).

**v4.15 status (matter-sector exclusion record, supersedes the v4.7 reading above).** F19 moves to the exclusion reservoir. OP-0-ACTIVATION dead: the claim that mesoscopic coherent superpositions reach $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$ via density-wave plus edge-mode contributions assumed super-extensive Var(T), which the exclusion record kills. A laboratory superposition does not sustain the GHZ-class coherence the threshold demands. The structural skeleton of the mechanism survives as descriptive physics (the DP equation, the Margolus-Levitin temporal pixel, the conformal shielding of the EM sector, the 5D exhaust channel), and the convexity rule (v4.16, LINT-CONVEX-1) confirms the matter channel can only soften geometry, consistent with a collapse-toward-the-pole reading rather than a stiffening one. But the quantitative collapse-rate prediction is reservoired pending a real-observable vehicle. The empirical face that survives this contraction is the gravitational-noise / stochastic-G channel (S-NOISE), first-order in fluctuations and requiring no threshold; comparison class Diosi-Penrose, CSL, Oppenheim.

**Channel routing note:** The dynamically amplified $G_{\text{eff}}$ described above operates during the transient collapse event, when the coherent state's QFI load sources extreme stress-energy gradients in the brane geometry. This is structurally distinct from the killed $G_{\text{eff}}$ mechanism (which proposed a static, local amplification of the Newtonian constant in the radial channel). The collapse $G_{\text{eff}}$ surge is a transient geometric effect terminated by the Linter within the temporal pixel $\delta t$; it does not persist as a modified gravitational constant. After excision, K2 ($G = G_N$ always) is immediately restored.

**F20: Geometry Condenses from a Topological Phase With Quantized $\Lambda$ Selection** [revised v4.8]
**Addresses:** Stochastic radion destabilization, monopole problem, initial conditions for F12 (dark energy evolution), cosmological constant initialization, MM intrinsic $\Lambda$ catastrophe (formerly OP-CC, now discharged).
**Statement:** The SO(1,4) $\to$ SO(1,3) symmetry breaking replaces standard slow-roll inflation with instantaneous geometric condensation, simultaneously selecting a topological sector $k$ from the Addazi-Meluccio tower of degenerate vacua. Prior to SSB, the theory is a topological BF gauge theory with zero local propagating degrees of freedom. The Dirac-Bergmann constraint analysis confirms that the Higgs momentum is algebraically constrained ($\Pi_A \approx 0$) and no scalar mode propagates in the unbroken phase. The radion $\rho(x)$ exists only in the broken phase.

The periodic SSB potential (Tier 4 §4.4, revised v4.8) admits a tower of degenerate minima at $v^{(k)} = v^{(0)} + 2\pi k/(c Y_{\mathrm{MM}})$, each corresponding to a distinct topological sector with cosmological constant $\Lambda^{(k)} = 3 c M_P^2 / [32(-\theta^{(0)} + 2\pi k)]$ (T3.6). The bare sombrero potential $V = \lambda(\phi^A\phi_A - v^2)^2$ with $\lambda \sim 10^{-44}$ and $v \sim M_{\text{Pl}}$ that was cataloged in earlier versions as incapable of supporting slow-roll inflation ($\eta \approx -4$, $n_s \approx -7$) is superseded; the first-order BF kinetic structure continues to eliminate any canonical kinetic term required for slow roll.

The vacuum manifold SO(1,4)/SO(1,3) $\cong S^3$ has $\pi_0 = \pi_1 = \pi_2 = 0$. No domain walls, cosmic strings, or magnetic monopoles are produced. Only $\pi_3$ textures (dynamically unstable Skyrmions) form and dissipate harmlessly. The monopole problem is dissolved by topology.

The selection of the physical sector $k_{\mathrm{phys}}$ proceeds dynamically through the SSB transition. Addazi-Meluccio show that the symmetry-breaking dynamics naturally selects $k \sim S_{\mathrm{dS}} \sim 10^{120}$, the sector matching the de Sitter entropy of the eventual horizon. Inter-sector tunneling is suppressed by the entropic factor $e^{-S_{\mathrm{dS}}}$, providing dynamical protection against radiative corrections to other sectors. The resulting $\Lambda^{(k)}_{\text{initial}}$ matches the observed cosmological constant up to F12 intra-sector evolution.

The latent heat thermalizes at $T_{\text{RH}} \sim 4 \times 10^7\,\text{GeV}$. The corresponding $H_{\text{RH}} \sim 160\,\text{keV}$ is safely below $\mu_\rho \gtrsim \text{MeV}$. Stochastic destabilization is dissolved: the radion does not exist pre-SSB, and the post-SSB Hubble parameter is too low to overcome the classical restoring force.

The post-SSB universe is a maximally incoherent thermal plasma with $f \approx 0$, $F_Q \sim N$, $v(F_Q) \approx v$. The handoff to the state-dependent regime is smooth.

**Constrained by:** K5, K6, K8, K15, K18, T3.6, Dirac constraint analysis ($\Pi_A \approx 0$ pre-SSB).

**Open (refined):** Three $\lambda$-independent nucleation mechanisms remain identified: gauge instanton tunneling ($S_{\text{inst}} = 4\pi^2/g^2$, bypassing CDL), thermal KK daisy resummation ($N_{\text{species}} \sim 10^{32}$ driving violently first-order transition), and dynamical cobordism (McNamara-Vafa). The structural argument that percolation is dissolved by the absence of a metric in the BF phase (C20g) eliminates the standard homogeneity problem. The critical remaining calculation is the derivation of the effective gauge coupling $g$ from the MM construction parameters. If $g \sim \mathcal{O}(1)$, the instanton action is $\mathcal{O}(10^1$ to $10^2)$ and $\Gamma_{\text{inst}} \gg H^4$. A secondary open problem is the radiative induction of an effective $\int \text{Tr}(F \wedge \star F)$ operator from boundary/KK effects in the pre-geometric BF phase, required for the instanton solutions to exist prior to metric condensation. New open problem (S-CC-005): identify whether the bulk SO(2,4) Chern-Simons level $k_{\mathrm{bulk}}$ matches the boundary topological sector $k_{\mathrm{phys}} \sim S_{\mathrm{dS}}$ via the descent equations. If yes, the topological selection is automatic from existing framework structure; if no, the AM mechanism is an additional ingredient that must be adopted explicitly.

**F21: Dual-Channel Gamow Enhancement**
**Addresses:** B15 (Failed Supernovae, extended to SN-less GRBs), metallicity paradox in GRB 111005A
**Statement:** Macroscopic quantum coherence ($F_Q \sim N^2$) in the pre-collapse stellar core enhances Gamow tunneling probabilities by $G^2_\mathrm{total} \sim 10^{20}$ to $10^{21}$ through two multiplicative, independent channels: (i) a non-perturbative geometric phase modification of the WKB exponent, sourced by the topological torsion flux of the coherent domain acting as a macroscopic Katanaev-Volovich dislocation defect (Bakke-Furtado formalism), yielding $G^2_\mathrm{topo} \sim 10^{11}$; (ii) ponderomotive compression of the degenerate electron gas by the radion standing wave locked to nuclear pasta density modulations, enhancing Thomas-Fermi screening by $C^{1/3}$ with $C \sim 10^3$ (capped by 100 MeV Fermi pressure), yielding $G^2_\mathrm{screen} \sim 10^9$. The combined enhancement reduces core luminosity, halts line-driven winds, and preserves progenitor angular momentum at super-solar metallicity.
**Derived from:** F13 (LUNA screening pathway), K1 (two-channel decomposition), K2 ($G = G_N$ always), K4 (framework purely gravitational), T2.7 (conformal invariance protects EM couplings)
**Key parameters:** $\Phi_T \approx 0.05$ rad, $L_\mathrm{domain} \approx 4.65$ nm, $N_\mathrm{domain} \approx 10^{19}$, $C \approx 10^3$, $U_\mathrm{eff} \approx 50$ keV
**OP-0 conditionality (v4.4, updated v4.5):** The torsion flux $\Phi_T \approx 0.05$ rad requires VEV suppression to $v_{\text{eff}} \sim 69\,\text{TeV}$ (suppression ratio $\sim 10^{14}$). The modular Hamiltonian formulation (SF-Q1) provides the super-extensive scaling mechanism: $\text{Var}(K_{\text{mod}})$ includes edge mode contributions absent from $\text{Var}(T_{\mu\nu})$. The compound enhancement budget ($\sim 10^{27}$ to $10^{29}\,\text{GeV}^4$) meets the species-lowered activation threshold ($f_{Q,\text{crit}} \sim 10^{28}$ to $10^{30}$) when gauge KK modes from $dP_3$ are present. Conditional on gauge KK mode count from FTheoryTools computation (see OP-0 resolution, v4.5).

**v4.15 status (matter-sector exclusion record).** F21 and the nuclear-pasta contract chain (C21a topological torsion flux, C21b ponderomotive screening) move to the exclusion reservoir. OP-0-ACTIVATION dead: the compound enhancement budget that supplies $\Phi_T \approx 0.05$ rad rested on super-extensive Var(T) in a degenerate stellar substrate, killed by the exclusion record. The Katanaev-Volovich topological-defect channel and the Bakke-Furtado WKB modification survive as formal structures but are not activated by any equilibrium pasta state. C21c (the solar constraint, $\Phi_T = 0$, standard Salpeter screening) is unaffected and remains a passed mandatory constraint. Reactivation under the three-gate test; the live matter-sector route is the rescue-trellis torsion-Lagrangian calculation (S-TORSION-LAGRANGIAN), which targets propagating torsion with its own scale $\Lambda_T$ rather than pole-activated VEV suppression.

**F22: Channel Orthogonality Decoherence Protection**
**Addresses:** Coherence survival at $T \sim 10$ MeV in collapsar cores and MAD disks
**Statement:** The macroscopic quantum coherent state ($F_Q \sim N^2$) receives protection against thermal decoherence and MRI turbulence through a parity selection rule. Torsion couples to the parity-odd axial vector current $J_5^\mu$. Thermal and hydrodynamic perturbations (density, pressure, velocity) are parity-even and couple to the trace of $T_{\mu\nu}$ (Ricci channel). The two channels are algebraically orthogonal representations of the SO(1,4) $\to$ SO(1,3) breaking. The coupling matrix element between channels is zero by parity at tree level, making the effective "gap" infinite regardless of temperature. The coherent domain structure persists for all densities above $\rho_\mathrm{crit}$; the domain dissolves when the density drops below $\rho_\mathrm{crit}$, removing the torsion source.
**Derived from:** K1 (two-channel decomposition), Paper 0 Section 4 (traceless channel construction)
**Caveat:** Tree-level exactness established. Higher-loop mixing angle $\epsilon$ between trace and traceless sectors requires bounding from above. Establishing an upper bound on $\epsilon$ is an open problem for Paper 0 (see Appendix D).
**OP-0 conditionality (v4.4, updated v4.5):** The torsion amplitude that the parity selection rule protects is conditional on $\mathcal{f}_Q$ achieving super-extensive scaling via the modular Hamiltonian formulation (SF-Q1). The selection rule itself (algebraic orthogonality of trace and traceless channels) is a theorem of the construction and survives independently. Conditional on gauge KK mode count from FTheoryTools computation (see OP-0 resolution, v4.5).

**F23: Swampland Conjectures as Hydrodynamic Theorems**
**Addresses:** T3.2 (Swampland constraints), providing non-perturbative proofs conditional on the construction
**Statement:** The Swampland Distance Conjecture and the Weak Gravity Conjecture are derivable as theorems of the hydrodynamic limit of continuous conformal fluids on the ETW brane, under three explicit assumptions: (A1) the Karch-Randall braneworld construction with constant DBI tension, (A2) the heat kernel coupling $\gamma\,(\phi^A\phi_A)\,\mathcal{f}_Q$ with $\gamma > 0$, and (A3) BKM regularity of the boundary fluid (a theorem of the SO(1,4) gauge structure via the Bounding Box).

*Distance Conjecture:* Extreme thermodynamic compression ($\mathcal{f}_Q \to N^2$) drives $\Lambda_s \to 0$. The KK mass gap $m_{\text{KK}} \sim 1/z_0$ decreases exponentially with geodesic distance in the radion moduli space: $m_{\text{KK}} \sim M_{\text{Pl}}\,e^{-\alpha\,d}$ with $\alpha = 1/4$ fixed by self-consistency with the WGC. The boundary-fluid Bures metric curvature plays the role of moduli-space distance.

*Weak Gravity Conjecture:* The extremality parameter $\zeta = m/(q\,\Lambda_s)$ satisfies $\zeta^{(\text{cross})} = q^{-1}\sqrt{T_{\text{local}}/M_{\text{Pl}}} \ll 1$ at the moment the lightest KK mode becomes thermally accessible. The KK exhaust opens before extremality is reached. The BKM regularity (Bounding Box) prevents the fluid from reaching Planck temperatures, ensuring $\zeta^{(\text{cross})} < 10^{-2}/q$ for all configurations within the constrained phase space.

*de Sitter bypass:* Follows from F12 (dark energy evolves). A static cosmological constant ($w = -1$ identically) requires $dv/dt = 0$ globally, which the construction structurally forbids. The observable cosmic expansion is the dynamical consequence of 5D KK exhaust maintaining the 4D NEC. Consistent with DESI DR2 thawing dark energy preference at $2.5$ to $4.2\sigma$.

**Constrained by:** K1, K2, K6, K8, K16
**Scope:** Conditional on A1, A2, A3. Within this scope, the conjectures are theorems of the hydrodynamic limit.

**F-CC: Cosmological Constant Quantization and Initial Sector Selection** [v4.8]
**Addresses:** B2 (dark energy initial value), B5 (cosmological constant problem, formerly OP-CC).
**Statement:** The cosmological constant $\Lambda$ is not a continuous parameter but is quantized into the discrete tower $\Lambda^{(k)} = 3 c M_P^2/[32(-\theta^{(0)} + 2\pi k)]$ via the Addazi-Meluccio topological mechanism (T3.6). The bulk SO(2,4) Chern-Simons construction descending to the boundary MM action mandates this quantization through the gravitational $\theta$-angle. The dynamical SSB process selects the sector $k_{\mathrm{phys}} \sim S_{\mathrm{dS}}$ matching the de Sitter entropy, providing the initial condition $\Lambda^{(k_{\mathrm{phys}})}_{\text{initial}}$ for F12 evolution. The selected vacuum is dynamically protected by three complementary mechanisms: entropic suppression of inter-sector tunneling ($\Gamma_{\mathrm{tunnel}} \sim e^{-S_{\mathrm{dS}}}$), geometric suppression of perturbative aperiodic corrections ($V_{\mathrm{barrier}}/\delta V_{\mathrm{aper}} \sim 10^{16}$ at MeV radion mass, per K18), and the non-renormalization theorem for periodic operators ($\delta Y_{\mathrm{SSB}}^{\text{1-loop}} \equiv 0$, per S-CC-003 discharge).
**Constrained by:** T3.6, K18, F20, F12.
**Constrains:** cosmological evolution trajectory, effective dark energy equation of state.
**Open (S-CC-005):** Identification of bulk SO(2,4) Chern-Simons level $k_{\mathrm{bulk}}$ with boundary AM topological sector $k_{\mathrm{phys}}$ via descent equations. If the identification holds, the topological selection is automatic from existing framework structure; otherwise the AM mechanism must be adopted as an additional ingredient.

# 4. THE CONTRACTS

Contracts are HOW functions are satisfied. Each is tagged to its parent function with explicit status. Contracts can compete (multiple candidates for same role), compose (jointly satisfy a function), or be regime-separated (active in different parameter regimes).

| Lagrangian uniqueness of $\gamma(\eta_{AB}\phi^A\phi^B)\mathcal{f}_Q$ | standard heat kernel theory (Class Block) | Tier 4 coupling uniqueness claim | The original formulation in Paper 0 claimed the coupling is the unique lowest-dimension SO(1,4)-invariant operator generated at one loop. No refinement of the symmetry analysis can restore Lagrangian uniqueness; the competing operators are mandatory outputs of the $a_4$ coefficient for any matter content. The thermodynamic dominance formulation replaces this claim entirely. No known reactivation path. | Gemini Adversarial Audit: Coupling Uniqueness (April 2026) |
| ER-Q-01: v4.5 gauge KK species lowering of $f_{Q,\text{crit}}$ | dimensional analysis (Block) | OP-0 resolution mechanism | The v4.5 resolution of OP-0 claimed that the Pati-Salam gauge KK tower from the $dP_3$ Laplacian provides $\sim 10^2$ to $10^4$ brane-localized vector boson species, each contributing $c = 1/10$ to the central charge sum, lowering $f_{Q,\text{crit}}$ from $10^{32}$ to $10^{28}$ to $10^{30}\,\text{GeV}^4$. The "two species counts" of v4.5 (one in $\gamma$, one in $f_{Q,\text{crit}}$) collapsed to one count double-counted. | ER-CC-001: Species-enhanced $\gamma(z_0)$ stabilization of Karch-Randall brane radial position | algebraic runaway (Class Block, v4.8) | S-CC-001 (brane stabilization via coupled saddle-point) | The bare DBI tension is $z_0$-independent under the Karch-Randall tuning; the $\gamma(z_0) = c_{\mathrm{KK}} z_0^2/(128\pi^2 L^2 M_5^2)$ inheritance was the only mechanism in the original construction that broke this degeneracy. Killed by Gemini CC Derivation Reports Run 1 and Run 2 (April 2026). The $z_0$-gradient is strictly negative for all physical states; the brane runs to the IR horizon, $m_{\mathrm{KK}} \to 0$, $\Lambda_s \to 0$, theory decompactifies. The $\gamma$-correction lifts the degeneracy into runaway, not stability. Block scope: any mechanism relying on the $\gamma(z_0)$ inheritance alone to stabilize the Karch-Randall radion is dead. | ER-CC-003: Discrete shift symmetry $\rho \to \rho + 2\pi/(c Y_{\mathrm{MM}})$ as protective for the AM periodic structure | explicit symmetry breaking (Point Block, v4.8) | radiative stability of AM potential | Symmetry-based protection (analogous to QCD axion protection by Peccei-Quinn shift symmetry) would be the strongest defense against radiative degradation of the topological vacuum tower. | ER-MM-001: Antisymmetry-based vanishing of the 30×30 primary-primary block of the second-class Dirac matrix | explicit algebraic computation (Point Block, v4.9) | Paper -1 §VI D ultra-locality argument | The original Paper -1 §VI D claim was that antisymmetry of the Poisson bracket combined with index symmetry of $Z^i_{AB} Z^j_{CD}$ forces $\{Z^i_{AB}(x), Z^j_{CD}(y)\}$ to vanish identically, delivering an ultra-local 44×44 Dirac matrix amenable to pointwise Schur-complement factorization. Killed by Gemini Deep Research report on Paper -1 §VI rewrite (April 2026, Q2) and DeepSeek cross-examination (April 2026, Q1) through two independent explicit algebraic computations of the bracket. Both reproduce the same nonvanishing leading term $\{Z^i_{ab}(x), Z^j_{cd}(y)\} \supset -2\alpha v\,\epsilon_{cdab4}\,[\cdots]\,\partial_k \delta^3(x-y)$, driven by $v$ and spatial curvature through the BF-type pre-symplectic structure. The cancellation argument conflates antisymmetry of the full bracket (under simultaneous coordinate-plus-index swap, automatic) with a symmetric-index cancellation (not forced). Block scope: Point Block. The specific cancellation argument is dead; block structure of the 44×44 matrix must be treated as pseudo-differential rather than ultra-local. Structural origin: the argument was imported from pure BF theory, where $B$ is an independent configuration and the analogous bracket vanishes because $\{\Pi, B\} = 0$. In MM, $B$ is replaced by $F(A)$, which depends on the gauge connection through $\partial A + AA$, so the analogous bracket activates through connection dependence. The BF-to-MM distinction is the structural reason the import fails. Reactivation conditions: discovery of a different symmetry of the MM action (not present in pure BF) that forces the bracket to vanish through a mechanism not identified in the two-source audit. Unlikely on current evidence. Date killed: April 2026. | Gemini DR §VI Rewrite Route (April 2026); DeepSeek Cross-Examination Report (April 2026) |
| ER-MM-002: Local algebraic constraint redefinition $\widetilde{Z} = m(x) Z$ absorbing the 30×30 primary-primary derivative block | principal symbol order preservation (Class Block, v4.9) | Paper -1 §VI ultra-locality rescue via canonical transformation | The hypothesis was that an invertible local algebraic redefinition $\widetilde{Z}^i_{AB}(x) = Z^i_{AB}(x) + k^{ij}_{AB}{}^{CD}(x) Z^j_{CD}(x)$, with $k$ a pointwise polynomial function of $A$, $\phi$, and $F$, could absorb the derivative block and restore the Dirac matrix to ultra-local form. Killed by the No-Go Lemma (ChatGPT Track A Construction, April 2026; formalized in paper_minus1_section_VI_obstruction_lemma.md). For local algebraic $K$, the four-term expansion of $\{\widetilde{Z}, \widetilde{Z}\}$ reduces on the constraint surface to $m(x) \{Z, Z\} m(y)^T$ with $m = I + k$. At the principal symbol level, $\sigma(\widetilde{\Delta}_{ZZ}) = m \sigma(\Delta_{ZZ}) m^T$: local conjugation preserves operator order. Cancellation of the derivative block would require $m \mathcal{C}^k m^T = 0$, which for invertible $m$ forces $\mathcal{C}^k = 0$, contradicting the established nonvanishing result (ER-MM-001). The only escape routes are singular $m$ (not an admissible redefinition) or non-local $K$ (relocates the non-locality into the transformation rather than eliminating it). Block scope: Class Block. Any mechanism relying on local algebraic canonical transformations to achieve ultra-locality in the MM Dirac matrix is structurally obstructed. Structural origin (DeepSeek identification, April 2026): the derivative index pattern $\epsilon^{0ikl}\partial_k$ in $\mathcal{C}^k$ is a spatial curl operator whose inverse on $\mathbb{R}^3$ is the Biot-Savart kernel, non-local by construction. Any $K$ solving the cancellation condition at the operator level inherits $\Delta^{-1}$. The obstruction is specifically tied to the BF-type topological kinetic structure $\epsilon_{ABCDE} F^{AB} \wedge F^{CD} \phi^E$. Reactivation conditions: discovery of a non-algebraic canonical transformation framework that preserves locality through a mechanism not anticipated in the No-Go Lemma, or reformulation of the MM action replacing the BF-type kinetic structure with something that avoids the curl-operator obstruction. Both speculative and unlikely. Date killed: April 2026. | ChatGPT Track A Construction (No-Go Lemma, April 2026); DeepSeek Track A Construction (April 2026) |
| ER-MM-003: Pointwise Schur-complement recovery of the clean determinant factorization $\det \Delta \propto (\det e)^k (v+\rho)^m \lambda^n$ in coordinate space | non-local Schur complement (Point Block, v4.9) | Paper -1 §VI determinant analysis route | The hypothesis was that the clean factorization could be recovered in coordinate space via pointwise Schur-complement inversion of the full 44×44 Dirac matrix, even with the 30×30 derivative block treated honestly. Killed by Schur-complement obstruction: when the upper-left 30×30 block $A$ is a first-order differential operator with $A^{-1}$ a non-local Green's function (specifically, the Biot-Savart kernel per ER-MM-002 structural origin), the Schur complement $D - C A^{-1} B$ is an integro-differential operator in coordinate space. Its determinant is not a pointwise algebraic function of the fields. The clean factorization $(\det e)^k (v+\rho)^m \lambda^n$ cannot be computed in coordinate space; it can only be recovered at the principal symbol level in Fourier space (a finite algebraic computation at each $\xi$). Block scope: Point Block. The pointwise determinant route specifically is obstructed; the operator-theoretic reformulation via principal symbol survives as S-MM-002. Reactivation conditions: discovery of a coordinate-space regularization scheme that renders $A^{-1}$ local in some effective sense while preserving the physics.
