**Structural lesson from v3.6:** All perturbative tree-level gravitational modifications to nuclear physics are dead. $G_N^2 \sim 10^{-76}\;\text{GeV}^{-4}$ eliminates every mechanism that routes through local gravitational coupling at femtometer scales, regardless of coherent amplification or Planck mass suppression. The surviving pathways exploit: (a) non-perturbative topological geometry (the WKB phase responds to the topology of the tunneling path, not to the coupling strength), and (b) macroscopically amplified thermodynamics (the radion compresses the electron gas, and the electron density performs the screening through standard electrostatic physics). Any future application of the framework to nuclear-scale phenomena must route through these non-perturbative channels.

**Structural lesson from v3.8:** The framework's condensed-matter mechanisms (radion catalysis, Kondo states, coherence pumping) require three prerequisites: a rigid lattice providing mechanical substrate, an external or internal coherent driver maintaining $f > 0$, and a zero-entropy exhaust pathway into the KK tower. These prerequisites are domain-specific to structured solid-state environments. They cannot be exported to unbound thermal plasmas (BBN epoch), unstructured stellar interiors below the superfluid transition, or any environment lacking acoustic deformation potentials. The LUNA and CeNi$_5$ applications succeed precisely because all three prerequisites are satisfied by construction. The BBN application fails precisely because all three are structurally absent.

**Structural lesson from v3.9 (generalized cosmological plasma exclusion):** The condensed-matter domain prerequisites established in v3.8 (rigid lattice, external or internal coherent driver, zero-entropy exhaust pathway) apply with increasing force to all cosmological plasma environments above the QCD confinement temperature ($T \gtrsim 150$ MeV). In the BBN epoch ($T \sim 30$ to $100$ keV), the plasma thermalization timescale is $\tau_{\text{th}} \sim 10^{-15}$ s, already saturating the KK scrambling time by three orders of magnitude. At the electroweak phase transition ($T \sim 100$ GeV), $\tau_{\text{th}} \sim 10^{-22}$ s, overwhelming $t_s$ by ten orders of magnitude. The exhaust race ($t_s \ll \tau_{\text{th}}$), which the framework wins decisively in structured solid-state environments, is lost catastrophically in every unbound relativistic plasma environment. The radion activation mechanism is structurally confined to post-QCD-confinement environments possessing crystalline or superfluid order. Expanding bubble walls of cosmological phase transitions are fluctuating scalar field condensates, not rigid mechanical substrates; they cannot anchor phase-locked standing waves. Any future application of the framework to cosmological plasma epochs must first demonstrate a mechanism by which $\tau_{\text{th}}$ drops below $t_s$, which the framework's own thermodynamics structurally forbid.

**Structural lesson from v4.4 (extensivity of equilibrium fluctuations):** The fluctuation-dissipation theorem constrains the variance of any extensive thermodynamic observable in a stable equilibrium state to $O(N)$. This includes the stress-energy tensor $T_{\mu\nu}$ and its trace $T^\mu{}_\mu$. For gapped, symmetry-broken ground states (BCS, CDW, ferromagnet, structural distortion), area-law entanglement further restricts the QFI to the standard quantum limit. Super-extensive $O(N^2)$ scaling requires either (i) maximally entangled non-local states (GHZ/NOON), which are fragile and are not equilibrium ground states, or (ii) quantum critical points where the gap closes and susceptibility diverges, or (iii) non-equilibrium driven states that violate thermodynamic stability criteria. No equilibrium condensed-matter or astrophysical system can achieve $O(N^2)$ variance of $T_{\mu\nu}$ through spontaneous symmetry breaking alone. All framework applications requiring super-extensive $\mathcal{f}_Q$ must either route through driven non-equilibrium states or invoke the modular flow definition (Formulation B, confirmed as the resolution mechanism in v4.5, see SF-Q1), which accesses entanglement contributions beyond simple operator variance.

**Structural lesson from v4.4 (generator identification):** The Quantum Fisher Information is generator-dependent. QFI for phase estimation with entangled states achieves $N^2$ (Heisenberg limit). QFI for energy/number estimation with equilibrium states is $O(N)$ (standard quantum limit). These are different physical quantities for different measurement tasks. Paper 0 Appendix 14 derives $N^2$ from phase estimation, then applies it to $\text{Var}(T_{\mu\nu})$, an energy-momentum quantity. This identification is the load-bearing gap in the derivation. Future analyses must explicitly specify which generator's QFI is being used and verify that the scaling claim matches the generator.

**Structural lesson from v4.5 (Goldstone cancellation):** The derivative coupling of the Bogoliubov-Anderson phonon to $T_{00}$ (through $(\nabla\phi)^2$) produces spectral weight $\chi''(\omega) \sim \omega^4$. The proper-time weighting $1/\omega^4$ cancels this exactly, rendering the IR acoustic cutoff irrelevant to leading order. The density-wave branch (non-derivative coupled, overdamped liquid-vapor coexistence modes) dominates the spectral integral because it couples through binding energy density, not phase gradients. Future spectral calculations for any system must identify the coupling structure (derivative vs. non-derivative) before inferring IR behavior.

**Structural lesson from v4.5 (pole structure of VEV suppression):** Torsion pressure scales as $1/(1 - f_Q/f_{Q,\text{crit}})$, where $f_{Q,\text{crit}} = (\lambda/\gamma)M_{\text{Pl}}^2$. Ambient torsion ($f_Q \ll f_{Q,\text{crit}}$) is Planck-suppressed at $10^{-37}$ of nuclear pressure. The mechanism is all-or-nothing, activated when the compound enhancement budget reaches the species-determined critical threshold. The framework's astrophysical predictions are binary: they hold fully or they hold not at all.

**Structural lesson from v4.5 (the GUT is load-bearing):** The PS matter spectrum nearly cancels the SM trace anomaly ($|\Sigma|$ drops from 0.567 to 0.008). Without the gauge KK tower from $dP_3$, $f_{Q,\text{crit}}$ rises to $10^{33.8}$, which is unreachable. The gauge KK species reduce $f_{Q,\text{crit}}$ to $10^{28}$ to $10^{30}$, bringing it within range of the compound budget. The framework's astrophysical phenomenology requires the construction (Tier 4), the coupling (eq. 1.1), and the specific GUT realization (F-theory PS on $dP_3$). Removing the GUT kills the phenomenology even if the construction is correct. The GUT Box is architecturally load-bearing.

**v4.7 annotation to the v4.5 GUT-load-bearing lesson:** The specific numerical argument above (that the gauge KK tower is required to lower $f_{Q,\text{crit}}$ into range of the compound budget) is superseded by the v4.7 $\gamma$ derivation. The $\Lambda_s^2$ suppression that the v4.5 analysis attributed to an independent species count at the threshold is actually already carried by $\gamma$ via the KK heat kernel spectral trace (SF-D0). The F-theory Pati-Salam construction on $dP_3$ remains architecturally load-bearing for other reasons: K11 beta function non-vanishing, K12 topological Dirichlet confinement via 7-brane localization, K14 gravitational coupling suppression of the full PS spectrum, and the Higgsing cascade providing the SM embedding pathway. The GUT Box occupant's role in OP-0 closure transitions from "decisive species contribution at the threshold" to "provides the matter content whose beta functions and spectrum enter the K8/K10/K11 precision computations."

**SL-12 (v4.7, dimensional analysis of effective operators requires explicit derivation):** The v4.4 through v4.6 trellis carried $\gamma \sim 1/M_{\text{Pl}}^2$ as an inherited assumption from Paper 0, never derived. This stipulation introduced a 20 OoM error that manifested as a phenomenology crisis (OP-0) and was "resolved" through the wrong mechanism (v4.5 gauge KK species lowering). The correct resolution required computing $\gamma$ from first principles via the additive heat kernel spectral trace over the KK graviton tower. The lesson: any dimensionally nontrivial coefficient in the framework must be derived from the fundamental construction, traced through the Seeley-DeWitt expansion and the species scale identity, rather than adopted as a natural-scaling estimate. Natural-scaling estimates are placeholders for derivations, useful only as first-pass plausibility checks. A stipulated coefficient is a hidden sorry that will eventually demand discharge. New linter rule: LINT-11.

**SL-13 (v4.7, spectral traces and coherent sums are different mathematical objects):** Heat kernel sums over field spectra are additive traces of eigenvalue contributions. Scattering amplitudes are coherent sums of wave amplitudes. Propagators are Green's function resolvent sums. Sum rules that produce cancellation in the scattering category (Sturm-Liouville orthogonality of KK wavefunctions, Geng et al. 2023 scattering sum rules) do not apply to the trace category. Mixing these categories led Gemini Report 1 (DG-CFT-051) in the $\gamma$ adjudication to reach the wrong conclusion via plausible-sounding but misapplied physics. The lesson: when evaluating sums over field towers, identify what object is being summed (trace, amplitude, propagator) before importing sum-rule arguments from adjacent contexts. The structural test: is the object a local coincidence-limit expansion of a heat kernel (additive spectral trace, species-enhanced), or a bilinear in external wavefunctions at separated points (coherent amplitude, orthogonality-constrained)? The first is enhanced by $N_{\text{species}}$; the second is not. New linter rule: LINT-12.

**SL-AM-1 (v4.13, AM kinematic dominance bound):** Any O(N) operator on the boundary is suppressed against the Addazi-Meluccio topological potential barrier by a factor of $\sim 10^{99}$. The trace channel, and any extensively scaling operator coupled gravitationally, cannot displace the radion from its discrete $\Lambda^{(k)}$ minimum. Only super-extensive O(N²) operators sourced by ODLRO can engage the pole structure. Implication: cosmological evolution at smooth gradient cannot be driven by gravitational-coupling-suppressed channels. This is the kinematic content of the F12 retraction (v4.13): the AM topological barrier height ($\sim 10^{32}$ GeV⁴) overwhelms the trace-channel gradient by enough orders of magnitude that no intra-sector evolution can be sourced from gravitationally coupled O(N) operators within a Hubble time.

**SL-BR-1 (v4.13, bulk-routing is stabilizing for degenerate objects):** F09 (failed supernovae), F19 (geometric collapse), and B19 (WD cooling) all route energy from the 4D brane into the 5D bulk. For degenerate stellar objects, removing energy increases degeneracy support: $R \propto M^{-1/3}$ expansion under mass loss, raised degeneracy pressure under cooling. These mechanisms are structurally cooling and stabilizing channels. They cannot serve as ignition or destabilization triggers without an additional energy-concentrating component. Implication: the framework's bulk-exhaust channels predict cooling anomalies (B19 stellar cooling, Q-branch ultramassive WD cooling delays interpreted via ONe-no-coherence), not detonation phenomenology. The sub-Chandra Type Ia question is correctly placed outside the framework's explanatory domain by this structural lesson alone.

**SL-PB-1 (v4.13, pole-binary catalysis does not bootstrap):** Microscopic local activation at standing-wave antinodes (C13c logic, active fraction $\sim 7 \times 10^{-5}$ per unit cell) produces microscopic energy release. It cannot drive macroscopic processes unless the surrounding bulk is already at classical activation threshold. The pole geometry confines the active volume; thermalization of fusion energy into non-activated surroundings cannot lower the surrounding Coulomb barriers. Implication: the framework's antinode-localized catalysis predicts rate enhancement (LENR heat anomaly summed over many events, F13.2) but not runaway detonation. Sharper than the existing "all-or-nothing" formulation at the v4.5 pole-structure structural lesson: the all-or-nothing transition is sharp at the pole, but transmission of activation through non-active surroundings is not free; pole geometry imposes a locality limit on cascade propagation.

**SL-VC-1 (v4.13, variance channel is L² not L^∞):** Variance-channel mechanisms ($\gamma$-activation, modular Hamiltonian with Donnelly-Freidel edge modes, ODLRO-mediated VEV suppression) provide L² control on $\text{Var}(K_{\text{mod}})$. The Sobolev embedding $H^1 \not\hookrightarrow L^\infty$ in 3D means L² bounds cannot constrain pointwise suprema. Geometric theorems and spectral theorems are within reach; fluid regularity theorems and pointwise-bounded cosmological gradients are outside reach. Implication: the framework's natural derivation surface is geometric and spectral (SDC, species tower, F-theory phenomenology), not fluid-dynamical (BKM regularity, hydrodynamic WGC). This is the structural content of the C23-WGC and C23-SDC reformulations at v4.13: the geometric SDC via Karch-Randall moduli is reachable (conditional on S-CC-002), the hydrodynamic WGC via BKM L^∞ is not.

**SL-RC-1 (v4.13, Running Coupling Rescue Theorem):** Non-perturbative stabilization in a Karch-Randall warped throat against polynomial runaway requires logarithmic running of the gauge coupling sufficient to satisfy $b > 1/(4\pi^2) \approx 0.0253$, where $b$ is the one-loop beta function coefficient including KK threshold corrections. Below this threshold, the instanton potential combined with the $z_0^{-4}$ holographic measure factor produces a tachyonic maximum rather than a stable minimum. The threshold derives from the requirement $q = 4 - 8\pi^2 b < 2$ for the total potential $V_{\text{tot}}(z_0) = C z_0^{-2} - A z_0^{-q}$ to admit a stable minimum. This converts the S-CC-002 sorry from an abstract "find an instanton mechanism" question into a concrete computational task: compute $b$ for the $X_{F13}$ Pati-Salam KK tower on the $dP_3$ Laplacian; if $b > 0.0253$, S-CC-002 closes unconditionally and C23-SDC discharges; otherwise the framework loses cosmological anchoring on the moduli side.

**SL-CORE-1 (v4.14, v(F_Q) physics is core; AM cosmology is contingent application):** The framework's load-bearing distinctive content is the v(F_Q) / N² / modular F_Q machinery: gravity coupled to modular-Hamiltonian Fisher information via the state-dependent SO(1,4) Higgs VEV, with super-extensive O(N²) scaling for ODLRO matter states and pole structure at $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$. This machinery generates the framework's matter-sector predictions (F09 compact-object bulk-routing, F11 KK gravitons as DM, F13/F13.2 LUNA screening anomaly, F19 geometric wavefunction collapse, F21 GRB compact-object phenomenology) and is structurally independent of the cosmological-sector choice between static $\Lambda^{(k)}$ via AM (Path A) and evolving $\Lambda(t) \sim R(t)^{-4}$ via Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu (Path B). The framework's exposure to falsification is concentrated in the cosmology-sector commitment (DESI Y5 / Euclid resolution of $w(z)$), but the core CC-1 physics survives any cosmology-branch-specific falsification. Implication for external positioning: the framework leads with CC-1 and its matter-sector predictions; the cosmology branch is framed as a contingent downstream application. Implication for trellis discipline: cosmology-sector retraction does not propagate to CC-1. Codified into LINT-CORE-1.

**SL-CONT-1 (v4.14, framework position within Vafa-lab interior-moduli-space program; revised per Addendum A):** The framework's Path A commitment to topologically stable positive-Λ minima is one specific structural mechanism within the broader Vafa-lab research program seeking critical points in the interior of M-theory moduli space. The dS swampland bound $|\nabla V|/V \geq 2/\sqrt{d-2}$ does not directly constrain interior-moduli-space critical points; the bound applies asymptotically at weak coupling per Baykara-Chen-Vafa arXiv:2605.16484v1 (May 2026). The framework is aligned with Vafa-lab research on critical-point existence; what is contrarian relative to the strongest forms of swampland conjectures is the specific claim that stable $V > 0$ minima exist with entropic protection (and the more specific claim that $V > 0$ at the AM minimum, S-AM-009). This narrower contrarian claim is the framework's empirical bet, falsifiable by DESI Y5 and Euclid. The original v4.14 draft framed the framework as taking the minority side of an active string phenomenology debate; the Addendum A revision (this lesson) corrects that framing: the framework occupies one of several active Vafa-lab research directions, not a contrarian position relative to the program as a whole. The Vafa-lab simultaneously develops the enhanced-symmetry critical-point program (Baykara-Chen-Vafa, aligned with Path A's interior-moduli-space intent) and the evolving Dark Dimension program (Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu arXiv:2507.03090, aligned with Path B). The framework's two-path structure mirrors this real research-frontier ambiguity.

**SL-PATH-1 (v4.14, two-path contingency planning):** Two-path contingency planning is the appropriate trellis structure when a load-bearing commitment is empirically uncertain and a structurally clean alternative exists. Both paths must be developed to discharge-ready state before the empirical resolution; ad hoc post-hoc restructuring after empirical falsification is forbidden by linter discipline. The pattern is: identify the empirically exposed commitment (Path A); identify the structurally cleanest alternative consistent with the framework's preserved core (Path B); develop both paths' open sorries in parallel to the depth that empirical resolution would demand; specify decisive triggers, secondary triggers, theoretical-pressure triggers, internal-consistency triggers, and a default posture; flag the paths as mutually exclusive (LINT-PATH-1) to prevent structural-element mixing. The framework's cosmological sector under v4.14 instantiates this pattern: Path A retains T3.6 + F-CC + S-CC-005 + hairon-as-vacuum-substrate; Path B substitutes T3.6' + F-DD-Evolve + dropped S-CC-005 with Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu-style geometric $\Lambda \sim R^{-4}$ and continuous radius evolution. The two paths cannot be partially adopted in combination because the AM topological structure and the continuous evolving-radius structure are mutually exclusive at the cosmological substrate level (the hairon-as-vacuum-substrate identification cannot coexist with a slowly varying mesoscopic $R(t)$ within a single trellis branch). Per Addendum A, the framework's two-path structure mirrors the two active Vafa-lab research directions (interior-moduli-space critical points; evolving Dark Dimension); the path framework is a faithful structural reflection of the current string phenomenology research frontier.

**SL-SUSC-1 (v4.15, the Susceptibility Exclusion; promoted to candidate Tier 0 meta-rule):** No object is simultaneously robust to a perturbation and informative about it through the same response channel; robustness and information are the small-$\chi$ and large-$\chi$ limits of one susceptibility. Constructions demanding both must separate the demands in frequency or scale (multiplexing: dynamical decoupling, subsidiarity, renormalization-scale separation) or die. The check is quantitative where a structure factor exists: phase stiffness implies $S_Z(0) \to 0$ via the compressibility sum rule, which caps the variance exponent at $p = (d-1)/d$ (hyperuniformity). Instances already in the corpus: stiffness-protected coordinates are hyperuniform (rescue-trellis ER-PXR-013); the $\gamma(z_0)$ stabilization runaway (ER-CC-001) is the same susceptibility diverging in the radial channel; the natural-proofs and amortization barriers in the P vs NP program carry the same shape. This is the load-bearing reason OP-0-ACTIVATION is dead: a substrate cannot be rigid against the environment and soft against itself, so protection-by-stiffness and super-extensivity are the two signs of one susceptibility. Exported to the meta-trellis as a candidate Tier 0 rule and to the obstruction-resonance catalog beside moment/winding factorization and inside/outside asymmetry. Codified into LINT-SUSC-1.

**SL-RD-1 (v4.15, dual descriptions pay rent through unique predictions, not mechanism):** The refresh ontology (SF-DG-012) reproduced the pole form, the threshold, and the saturation phase, adding zero new magnitude. Its entire net worth is the one falsifiable output C-RD-1. Lesson: when an ontological reframe is proposed, run it to its consistency gate immediately and bank the unique falsifiable output; the reframe itself carries no budget and rescues nothing the exclusion record killed. Companion to LINT-12's spectral-trace versus coherent-amplitude discipline: category clarity about what a reframe can and cannot supply.

**SL-RANK-1 (v4.16, order-and-rank confusion is the framework's recurring failure mode):** Three of the framework's hardest obstructions are the same error one order up in the modular expansion. ER-PXR-002 was a metric job-conflation (BKM dynamical metric appearing in a slot assigned to the SLD estimation metric). OP-0's origin (v4.4) was a QFI/Var(T) conflation (phase-estimation QFI identified with an energy-momentum variance). The generator gap (the matter-sector activation kill) is reinterpreted by SF-DG-013 as reading the second cumulant $\langle\delta K^2\rangle = F_Q$ as if it were a first-order source, when the source is the first cumulant $\langle K\rangle$ (modular energy). Lesson: in any modular or information-geometric coupling, fix the rank (which cumulant) and the order (which power of the deformation) before computing magnitudes; a quantity hired for the wrong role produces a kill that is really a bookkeeping error. The convexity sign-check (LINT-CONVEX-1) and the spectral-category check (LINT-12) are the two operational guards; this lesson names the family they both belong to.

---

### Linter Rules (v4.13)

The linter encodes rules of analysis whose violation has historically produced dimensional or category errors in the framework. Each rule compiles into a check that future analyses should run before asserting a result.

**LINT-11: Explicit Derivation of Dimensionful Coefficients.** Any dimensionally nontrivial coefficient in the framework must be explicitly derived from the fundamental construction, not stipulated by natural-scaling dimensional analysis. Stipulated coefficients must be flagged with "[STIPULATED, derivation pending]" and tracked as open problems. This applies to: $\gamma$ (now derived, OP-CK tracks the prefactor $c_{\text{KK}}$), $\lambda$ (derived from $m_\rho^2 = 8\lambda v_0^2$), and any future coefficients added. Historical precedent: the v4.4 through v4.6 inheritance of $\gamma \sim 1/M_{\text{Pl}}^2$ concealed a 20 OoM error for six months (SL-12).

**LINT-12: Spectral Category Identification.** When evaluating sums over field spectra (KK towers, matter species, CFT states, etc.), identify whether the object being summed is (a) a spectral trace (local heat kernel, zeta function, vacuum energy), (b) a coherent amplitude (scattering, correlation function between separated points), or (c) a propagator (resolvent, Green's function). Import sum rules only from the matching category. Cross-category imports are the single most common source of dimensional errors in the framework's history (SL-13). The operational check: Sturm-Liouville orthogonality and scattering sum rules apply to amplitude/propagator categories; species-enhancement applies to spectral traces; both do not apply simultaneously to the same object.

**LINT-13: Conditional Resolution Audit.** Any claim that OP-0 or any other existential obstruction is "resolved conditional on X" triggers a review of whether the resolution mechanism is structurally correct or whether a more direct unconditional resolution exists. The v4.5 conditional resolution of OP-0 (on gauge KK mode count from FTheoryTools) concealed the v4.7 unconditional resolution (via $\gamma$ derivation) for six months. Prefer explicit first-principles derivation over species-count workarounds. Nested conditionals warrant skepticism: if a result requires both mechanism A and computation B to reach the conclusion, check whether a reformulation reaches the conclusion through A alone or B alone.

**LINT-14 (v4.8): Trans-Planckian VEV Enforcement.** Any document referencing $v_0 = M_P$ as the bare SSB VEV requires update to reflect the trans-Planckian $v \sim 10^{139}$ GeV under AM adoption. The 4D Planck mass on the brane is generated through $M_P^2 = 32 Y_{\mathrm{MM}} v m^2$, not by identifying $v_0 = M_P$. The $M^2_{\mathrm{Pl,eff}} = (v + \rho)^2$ relation applies to the effective (post-coherence) VEV, not to the bare parameter.

**LINT-15 (v4.8): Periodic Potential Enforcement.** Any document referencing the SSB potential as $V = \lambda(\phi^A\phi_A - v_0^2)^2$ requires update to the periodic Addazi-Meluccio form $V_{\mathrm{SSB}} = Y_{\mathrm{SSB}} |J|[1 - \cos(c Y_{\mathrm{MM}}(|\phi| - v))]^p$. The Higgs self-coupling $\lambda$ is replaced by $Y_{\mathrm{SSB}}$ in the new potential structure. The sombrero form is superseded.

**LINT-16 (v4.8): $\Lambda$ Tower Enforcement.** Any argument relying on "static $\Lambda$" or "continuous-modulus $\Lambda$" requires reformulation in terms of the discrete tower $\Lambda^{(k)}$ (T3.6) and intra-sector evolution. F12's thawing trajectory is intra-sector dynamics; inter-sector transitions are forbidden by entropic suppression on cosmological timescales.

**LINT-17 (v4.8): Shift-Symmetry Protection Blocked.** Any document invoking the discrete shift symmetry $\rho \to \rho + 2\pi/(c Y_{\mathrm{MM}})$ as protective for the periodic AM potential requires correction. The symmetry is explicitly broken at tree level by the $\gamma(\phi^2) F_Q$ coupling, which is polynomial in $\phi$. The protection of the periodic structure is kinematic (K18, trans-Planckian VEV geometric suppression), not symmetric.

**LINT-18 (v4.9): Ultra-Local vs. Pseudo-Differential Discrimination.** When analyzing a Dirac matrix or constraint algebra, classify the resulting operator before attempting non-degeneracy proofs. Ultra-locality requires no spatial gradients of the canonical fields appearing in the bracket; first-order differential (pseudo-differential) structure arises whenever a primary constraint is built from the field strength $F(A)$ of a connection whose canonical momentum $\Pi$ also appears in the constraint set. Local conjugation by invertible field-dependent matrices $m(x)$ cannot reduce operator order: $\sigma(\widetilde{\Delta}) = m \sigma(\Delta) m^T$ preserves the order of the principal symbol. Concrete instance: MM SSB action, 30×30 primary-primary block is first-order differential, cannot be absorbed into pointwise form by any local algebraic redefinition (ER-MM-002). When this distinction is missed, the pointwise Schur-complement factorization program fails and must be replaced by symbol-level analysis (S-MM-002).

**LINT-19 (v4.9): AI-Generated Research Report Editorial Audit.** Deep research reports from AI systems contain two distinct output classes: computational results (algebra, citations, verdicts) and narrative framing (motivational language, speculative connections to broader programs, editorializing about significance). Treat these differently. Computational results require independent verification (cross-exam by a second tool, or direct by-hand check) before incorporation into formal documents. Narrative framing requires stripping: phrases like "perfectly preserves," "deeply enriches," "turning a mathematical correction into a major theoretical asset," "directly supports [unrelated program]" are markers of editorial inflation and must be removed before integration into a research paper unless supported by specific cited literature. Operational test: when reading an AI report, underline every claim supported by explicit algebra or direct citation; everything else is framing. Incorporate the underlined material; discard or paraphrase the rest. Concrete instance: the Gemini DR report on Paper -1 §VI (April 2026) contained algebraically correct bracket computation (Q2, verified by DeepSeek cross-exam) alongside unsupported speculation linking non-local Dirac brackets to "topological phase transitions in the deep ultraviolet" and "holographic naturalness paradigm"; the former was adopted, the latter stripped.

**LINT-20 (v4.10): Frame consistency in scalar-tensor displays.** Effective actions involving scalar-tensor structure must explicitly state the frame (Jordan, Einstein, or phenomenological Brans-Dicke parametrization with specified $\omega_{BD}$). Displaying both a Jordan-frame non-minimal coupling $F(\phi) R$ and an Einstein-frame-style explicit kinetic term $-(\partial\phi)^2$ in the same Lagrangian without specifying frame is forbidden, as these are inconsistent as a single-frame action. The displayed Lagrangian must either: (i) be in Jordan frame with kinetic term emerging from auxiliary-field reduction (and the auxiliary structure displayed), (ii) be in Einstein frame with constant $R$ coefficient and explicit kinetic term, or (iii) be flagged as a phenomenological parametrization with the frame interpretation specified. Historical precedent: Paper -1 §II E v2 displayed the frame-mixed form for two months before the v4.10 audit, inheriting the ambiguity from Stelle-West 1980's terse treatment.

**LINT-21 (v4.10): Scalar kinetic term construction in MMSW gravity.** Scalar field kinetic terms in MacDowell-Mansouri-Stelle-West gravity must be constructed via the first-order auxiliary-field formulation (Langenscheidt 2019, §4.2). The naive $(D\phi)^\dagger(D\phi)$ construction is forbidden because the gauge-fiber Hodge dual produces an antisymmetric $\mu\nu$ structure that vanishes as a Klein-Gordon kinetic term. Any framework component that asserts a propagating scalar in MMSW or related broken gauge-theoretic gravity construction must either (i) display the auxiliary-field action explicitly, (ii) cite the Langenscheidt resolution and reference the auxiliary structure, or (iii) provide an alternative principled mechanism (Weyl rescaling to Einstein frame, additional sigma-model term, or DBI completion) with explicit derivation. Reactivation conditions: discovery of a non-auxiliary-field MMSW kinetic-term construction not anticipated by Langenscheidt's analysis.

**LINT-22 (v4.11): First-order matter Lagrangian DOF accounting requires explicit secondary-promotion verification.** When assessing first-order matter sectors via Dirac-Bergmann analysis, do not expect the primary-primary block alone to discharge the DOF count. Primary blocks are generically rank 2 in a 5-component sector, not full rank. The DOF reduction proceeds through secondary promotion of null primaries: compute brackets $\{C_r, \mathcal{S}_s\}$ with the secondary constraints generated by preservation, verify rank equals the number of null primary combinations. Concrete instance: Langenscheidt auxiliary-field Higgs sector in MMSW gravity, primary block rank 2 with three null combinations promoted via secondary constraints (S-MIX-005a, S-MIX-005b). Historical precedent: the v4.10 expectation that S-MIX-005 would discharge the DOF count via primary-block analysis alone was framing-error, not computation-error; the secondary promotion was always required for first-order matter. New analyses involving auxiliary fields, BF-type matter actions, or compensator structures must verify the secondary-promotion mechanism explicitly rather than asserting full primary rank.

**LINT-23 (v4.11): Distinguish new conditionality from restatement of existing scope.** When a verdict comes back as MARGINAL or CONFIRMED WITH CAVEAT, check whether the caveat is genuinely new conditionality or a restatement of existing scope boundaries. The latter does not increase the framework's debt; absorb into the existing conditionality and update the parent sorry's gating list. Concrete instance: S-MIX-005b returned CONFIRMED WITH CAVEAT, where the caveat was "result is Higgs sub-sector confirmation, not full 44×44 ellipticity proof." Full ellipticity is the S-MM-002 question with expanded scope from v4.9; it was already a separate sorry, already gating the parent. Treating the S-MIX-005b caveat as a new caveat would have double-counted the same conditionality. Operational test: when reading a CONFIRMED WITH CAVEAT verdict, identify which open sorry the caveat reduces to. If the caveat names an already-open sorry, the conditionality is unchanged. If the caveat names something new, open a new sorry and update the parent's gating list.

**LINT-24 (v4.12): Cycle-chain refinement pattern for CAS-determinant questions.** When a CAS-determinant question returns INDETERMINATE or MARGINAL, do not expand the prompt scope. Refactor toward the bottleneck derivation. The S-MM-002 chain demonstrated the pattern: cycle 1 (preliminary) identified the rank-12 obstruction; cycles 2-3 (S-MM-002a/b parallel) collapsed onto a single missing input; cycle 4 (S-MM-002α) refused to confabulate the missing input and produced the conditional candidate; cycle 5 (S-MM-002β) reduced the question further to the subprincipal computation; cycle 6 (S-MM-002γ) produced the subprincipal entries and identified the conceptual obstruction. Each cycle sharpened the question and produced reusable structural results, even though the parent sorry did not close. When applying this pattern: budget the cycle count explicitly, document each cycle's reusable findings, and convert the chain to documented debt at budget exhaustion rather than continuing past the productive horizon.

**LINT-25 (v4.12): Documented-debt strategy when chain budget exhausts without closure.** When a cycle chain converges on a precisely characterized open question without closing it, the right move is documented debt rather than further refinement. Convert the chain's structural findings to paper inserts with explicit conditional structure; create a new gating sorry capturing the precise open question; preserve the chain's reusable computations as corpus entries; and rotate attention to other priorities. This prevents the chain from becoming ambient framework debt and enables parallel research progress. Concrete instance: the S-MM-002 chain closed at v4.12 with the configuration-robustness reframe (S-MM-CR), the explicit subprincipal computations preserved as Paper -1 v3 patch v4 §VI content, and the conditional candidate $\mathcal{F}_i^{\text{cand}}$ preserved as §III D content. Paper -1 ships submission-ready with explicit conditionality on S-MM-CR rather than ambient S-MM-002 conditionality. The strategy is not surrender; it is a tactical pause that converts the chain from a continuing ChatGPT-cycle drain to a documented research question.

**LINT-DLR-1 (v4.13): ODLRO vs DLRO Discipline.** Do not conflate classical cosmological clustering (DLRO density gradients, Bragg-peak ordering, structure formation) with macroscopic ODLRO (long-range phase coherence of a complex order parameter). Structure formation produces DLRO; only superconductors, superfluids, BECs, and degenerate pairing condensates produce ODLRO. Super-extensive $\mathcal{f}_Q$ scaling requires ODLRO. The trace channel and any extensively scaling operator do not engage the pole condition $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$. This rule catches the most common error in external analyses of the framework's astrophysical and cosmological applications. Concrete instance: the F12 thawing hypothesis (v3.0 through v4.12) implicitly assumed that integrated cosmic-structure-formation coherence would drive $\mathcal{f}_Q$ above threshold; the v4.13 reconciliation scout established that this is a categorical conflation between DLRO and ODLRO (ER-COSM-001).

**LINT-L2-1 (v4.13): Variance Bounds Are L² Not L^∞.** Do not propose mechanisms using $\text{Var}(K_{\text{mod}})$ bounds or other variance-channel bounds as substitutes for pointwise L^∞ amplitude bounds in fluid-dynamical or regularity contexts. The Sobolev gap $H^1 \not\hookrightarrow L^\infty$ in 3D is structural. Variance-channel mechanisms are categorically the wrong regularity class for fluid regularity theorems and pointwise-bounded cosmological gradients. Concrete instance: the v4.13 HSB scout attempted to substitute the variance-channel $\gamma$-activation bound for the killed BKM L^∞ amplitude bound in the hydrodynamic C23-WGC derivation; the substitution failed by the same regularity obstruction that produced ER-NS-001 (ER-WGC-001).

**LINT-CORE-1 (v4.14): Core-vs-Contingent External Positioning Discipline.** The framework's core identity is the v(F_Q) / N² / modular F_Q machinery (CC-1). Cosmology-sector commitments (T3.6 Path A or T3.6' Path B) are contingent applications of the core, not co-equal load-bearing axioms. Any external communication, paper abstract, press summary, or conference presentation must lead with CC-1 and its matter-sector predictions (compact-object phenomenology, condensed-matter LUNA, gravitational-wave phenomenology, F19 wavefunction collapse), with cosmology framed as a downstream contingent application. Documents that lead with the static-Λ commitment or describe the framework primarily by its cosmology branch trigger a v4.14 rewrite obligation. Operational test: if the proposed framing places the cosmology branch in the lead paragraph or abstract opening, redraft so that CC-1 leads. The v4.14 update module §9 provides the canonical external-communication template.

**LINT-DE-2 (v4.14, from Scout 4): Distance Conjecture Confinement on Multi-Modulus Slow-Roll.** Do not propose slow-roll quintessence mechanisms on moduli spaces with $N \gg 1$ light scalars within the AM-locked branch. Per the Distance Conjecture (T3.2), individual modulus excursions in a space of $N$ light scalars are confined to $\Delta\phi \lesssim M_P/\sqrt{N}$, which for the hairon construction ($N \sim 10^{120}$) gives $\Delta\phi \lesssim 10^{-60} M_P$, far below the trans-Planckian field range required for slow-roll quintessence to produce observable $w(z) \neq -1$ at percent level. Classical slow-roll quintessence is structurally impossible in the framework's hairon moduli space. The obstruction is categorical. This rule does not apply on Path B, where the active modulus $\chi$ parametrizing $R(t)$ is a single light scalar in the Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu construction, parametrically separated from the hairon condensate; in Path B, the slow-roll question reduces to identifying which modulus is $\chi$ (S-DD-001) and deriving $m_\chi \sim H_0$ from first principles in the framework's geometric setup (S-DD-002), neither of which is forbidden by LINT-DE-2.

**LINT-DE-3 (v4.14, from Scout 4): Topological Substrate Cannot Serve as Dynamical Matter.** Do not mobilize the microscopic constituents of a topological vacuum identification as additive rolling fields. The hairon construction (Addazi-Meluccio arXiv:2604.26982) identifies hairons as the BEC ground state of the de Sitter vacuum supplying the entropic accounting $k_{\text{phys}} \sim S_{\text{dS}}$; promoting hairons to dynamical scalars rolling under a quintessence-style potential produces structural conflict between the static-vacuum identification and the dynamical-matter mobilization. The obstruction extends to any framework structure where a topological substrate plays the dual role of static vacuum and dynamical condensate; the dual role cannot support a non-trivial $w(z)$ trajectory while preserving the static-vacuum identification. Concrete instance: ER-DE-005 (hairon-quintessence single-field) and ER-DE-006 (hairon-quintessence multi-field destabilization), both killed by this rule. Reactivation: identification of a topological substrate that admits dual roles without internal conflict (no candidate known).

**LINT-PATH-1 (v4.14): Path Mutual Exclusivity.** Path A and Path B commitments are mutually exclusive within a single trellis branch. Do not adopt structural elements from both paths in a hybrid theory. The AM topological structure (discrete $\Lambda^{(k)}$ tower, $S^4/\mathbb{Z}_N$ hairon orbifold, inter-sector entropic protection $e^{-S_{\text{dS}}}$) is incompatible with continuous evolving-radius cosmology (Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu $R(t)$ driven by slow-roll of $\chi$ with $m_\chi \sim H_0$). The two paths exist as alternatives selected by empirical resolution (DESI Y5, Euclid, gravitational-wave dark-sector constraints), not as components of a combined theory. Operational test: if a proposed mechanism uses both the AM topological selection and the evolving-radius geometric $\Lambda \sim R^{-4}$ relation, the proposal is invalid by LINT-PATH-1 regardless of its other merits. Inter-path migration is permitted (a future v4.15 or later may activate Path B upon empirical trigger), but combined-path constructions are forbidden.

**LINT-SUSC-1 (v4.15): Susceptibility Exclusion check.** [FLAG MODE] Test: a proposed mechanism requires one object to be insensitive for survival and sensitive for function (protected and super-extensive; robust and informative; stable and responsive) within the same frequency band or scale. Flag: locate the explicit frequency or scale separation that multiplexes the two demands, or route the proposal to the exclusion reservoir under SL-SUSC-1. The check is quantitative where a structure factor exists: phase stiffness implies $S_Z(0) \to 0$ via the compressibility sum rule, capping the variance exponent at $p = (d-1)/d$. Concrete instance: every matter-sector activation route killed at v4.15 demanded a coordinate that was rigid against the environment (to be protected) and soft against itself (to source the geometric channel); those are the two signs of one susceptibility.

**LINT-CONVEX-1 (v4.16): Matter softens, only the vacuum stiffens.** [HARD MODE] The matter coupling enters through the modular free energy $W(\epsilon) = \log\langle e^{-\epsilon K}\rangle$, whose second cumulant (the modular variance, $= F_Q$) is non-negative, so $W$ is convex and the matter $F_Q$ channel can only soften geometry (drive $1/G$ down, toward the pole), never stiffen it. Any matter-sector coupling whose computed effect raises geometric stiffness $1/G$ violates the convexity of $W$: halt and recheck order/sign before proceeding, the same way a negative probability flags a mistake. Stiffness set or raised by the vacuum/geometric sector (cosmological term, brane tension, radion-potential curvature) is unconstrained; the prohibition is only on the matter channel. Concrete class blocks: chameleon/density-screened stiffening, matter-driven UV-softening of gravity, density-induced repulsion or weak-gravity pockets or antigravity, and geometric stiffness tracking the nuclear EOS are all forbidden from the matter channel. This guard belongs in the linter precisely because order-and-sign confusion is the framework's recurring failure mode (SL-RANK-1).

---

### Shore Flag

**SF-DG-009: Addazi-Meluccio Integration Shore (v4.8, April 2026)**

This shore records the largest structural integration in the trellis since the F-theory Pati-Salam GUT Box selection (v4.0). It was triggered by the Gemini CC Derivation Report (Run 1), which killed the framework's original $\gamma(z_0)$ stabilization mechanism for deriving $\Lambda$ and surfaced the unresolved MM intrinsic $\Lambda \sim M_P^4$ catastrophe. Run 2 confirmed both findings independently and surfaced the Addazi-Meluccio pre-geometric gravity literature as a candidate resolution. Direct examination of the Addazi-Meluccio paper revealed a mature topological quantization mechanism for $\Lambda$ that is structurally compatible with the framework's existing MM SSB architecture, requiring only Tier 4 reformulation of the SSB potential to the periodic form. The radiative stability of this adoption at the framework's required MeV radion mass was the central question; the Gemini Radiative Stability Report (Run 3) confirmed survival by 16 orders of magnitude through kinematic dominance of the trans-Planckian VEV.

The integration discharges the long-standing OP-CC (MM intrinsic $\Lambda$ counterterm requirement), reformulates F20 to incorporate sector selection, adds F-CC as a new function, adds K18 as a new constraint, and replaces the Tier 4 sombrero potential with the periodic AM potential. The framework now possesses a partial first-principles derivation of $\Lambda$: the cosmological constant emerges as a topological winding number selected by SSB dynamics, with the observed value matching $k \sim S_{\mathrm{dS}}$. The remaining piece (brane radial stabilization, S-CC-001 reformulated) is decoupled from the $\Lambda$ derivation and proceeds through separate mechanisms (S-CC-002 instanton, S-CC-004 Casimir backreaction).

The integration was structurally non-disruptive to the framework's phenomenology: the two-regime behavior (vacuum-stable, ODLRO-erased) that F13.2 and F19 require becomes a derived consequence of the AM periodic potential plus the existing $\gamma F_Q$ coupling. All existing radion-dependent contracts survive the adoption. The mass window for $\mu_\rho$ is wide ($[1\,\mathrm{meV}, 100\,\mathrm{GeV}]$) and the framework's choice of MeV radion sits comfortably in the middle.

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, the kill of the $\gamma(z_0)$ mechanism (Run 1 Q2) was foreseen in the prompt's "crux to investigate" section, which explicitly flagged the suspicious naive analysis. Honestly characterizing the most likely failure mode in advance prevented motivated reasoning when the kill came back. Second, the pre-geometric gravity literature (Addazi-Meluccio program) was directly adjacent to the framework's own architecture but absent from the corpus until Run 2 surfaced it. The frontier-sentinel skill should be deployed periodically against the trellis's foundational Tier 3 and Tier 4 commitments to catch adjacent literature that was missed during initial corpus construction. Third, the radiative stability question would have been impossible to evaluate without the algebraic specifics from the Addazi-Meluccio paper. Adopting an external mechanism into the framework requires both the mechanism itself and its auxiliary parameters and stability arguments. Half-adoption is incoherent.

**Cross-program resonance.** The radion mass tradeoff we worked through has the structure: hierarchically small dimensionless coupling ($Y_{\mathrm{SSB}} \sim 10^{-435}$) protected by a non-renormalization argument (one-loop matter loops cannot generate trigonometric corrections). This parallels K14's protection of $\lambda \sim 10^{-44}$ (gravitational and species-scale suppression), and the framework's general posture toward small couplings: rather than fighting hierarchy via fine-tuning or anthropic reasoning, the framework routinely accepts hierarchically small couplings as inputs and protects them via gravitational or species-scale arguments. Whether this pattern is structurally robust (each small coupling deserves its own protection argument) or methodologically suspect (a free pass for hierarchical inputs) is a question worth examining as the framework matures.

**SF-DG-009.1: Paper -1 §VI Correction Sub-Shore (v4.9, April 2026)**

This sub-shore operates within the parent Addazi-Meluccio integration shore (SF-DG-009) and addresses a specific technical correction identified during the v4.8 integration: the status of the 44×44 second-class Dirac matrix in Paper -1 §VI. The parent shore adopted the AM periodic potential and the topological quantization of $\Lambda$; the sub-shore corrects an independent technical error in the Hamiltonian analysis that was not caused by the AM integration but was surfaced during the associated audit cycle.

The sub-shore discharges one sorry (S-MM-001, killed), opens three new sorrys (S-MM-002, S-MM-003, S-NS-018), adds three exclusion reservoir entries (ER-MM-001 through ER-MM-003), and contributes two linter rules (LINT-18, LINT-19). Paper -1 §VI is rewritten; §VII, §VIII, §IX receive targeted updates; Paper 0 v11 requires a minor acknowledgment paragraph; NS scaffold v3.5 receives a cross-reference and a new low-priority sorry. The §VI D vanishing claim is retracted; the broader explicit-matrix contribution of Paper -1 survives and strengthens via the principal-symbol pivot.

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, the prior Gemini DR audit cycle surfaced the §VI D error through an explicit audit objection planted in the construction prompt. The kill was anticipated as the most likely failure mode before the report returned; honestly characterizing the suspicious premise in advance prevented motivated reasoning when the kill came back. Second, two-source agreement on load-bearing computational claims proved essential. The Gemini DR report's Q2 bracket result, taken alone, could have been editorial inflation of a subtler underlying truth. The DeepSeek cross-exam's independent recomputation from scratch, reproducing the same leading term with the same sign structure, established the kill with confidence. LINT-19 codifies this pattern. Third, construction prompts produced stronger and more structurally informative output than the original deep research prompts. The ChatGPT No-Go Lemma generalizes the DeepSeek specific-ansatz failure into a principal-symbol conjugation theorem; this structural upgrade was not present in either the DR report or the cross-exam, and emerged only when the task was posed as explicit algebra rather than literature survey. Construction prompts should be preferred over DR prompts for tasks where the answer is algebraic rather than bibliographic. Fourth, the sub-shore reveals a pattern worth naming: AI-generated reports disaggregate cleanly into computational content and narrative framing. The computational content is reliable (when cross-verified); the narrative framing is frequently speculative and self-serving. LINT-19 codifies the operational discipline of reading these two output classes differently.

**Cross-program resonance.** The Paper -1 §VI D error has structural similarities to two other patterns in the framework's history. First, the v4.5 gauge KK species lowering mechanism (killed and moved to ER-Q-01 in v4.7) was also a "right survival outcome reached through wrong dimensional analysis": the phenomenology survived but the reasoning was incorrect. Paper -1's original §VI D was similarly a "right DOF count reached through wrong block-structure reasoning." In both cases, the correct resolution required rederiving the result from first principles rather than patching the argument. Pattern: when a derivation's result is preserved but the reasoning is replaced, audit whether the original reasoning concealed a structural obstruction that the correct reasoning either avoids or promotes to a separate result. Second, the BF-to-MM cancellation import error parallels the broader pattern of adopting external mechanisms without verifying their auxiliary parameters and stability arguments (documented as a SF-DG-009 lesson under the AM integration). In both cases, the issue was assuming that a technique valid in a simpler adjacent theory transfers to the framework's more structured setting without verification. Pattern: when importing a result from pure BF, pure Einstein-Cartan, or any adjacent topological theory, explicitly check the assumption layer. The field-strength-vs-independent-B distinction, the tetrad-vs-broken-gauge-boson distinction, and the symmetric-vs-periodic-potential distinction are all load-bearing and framework-specific. The obstruction-resonance skill should be deployed across the other active programs (P vs NP, Navier-Stokes small-data derivation, affine Grassmannian combinatorics) to check whether analogous "imported from adjacent theory without checking the structural distinction" errors are present. The operational test: for each load-bearing lemma, identify the parent theory the argument was imported from, and verify the specific structural feature that makes the argument work in the parent carries over to the framework.

**SF-DG-009.2: Higgs Sector Kinetic-Term Resolution Sub-Shore (v4.10, April 2026)**

This sub-shore operates within the parent Addazi-Meluccio integration shore (SF-DG-009) and the v4.9 §VI correction sub-shore (SF-DG-009.1). It addresses a technical question surfaced by the rank-counting consequences of the v4.9 §VI principal-symbol pivot: when the 30×30 primary-primary block is rank-deficient at leading order (curl kernel plus broken-sector $\epsilon$-contraction kernel), the strict leading-symbol reading forces DOF $\leq 1$, threatening the framework's conditional 2+1 prediction. Resolution arrives via auxiliary-field structure (Langenscheidt 2019, §4.2): scalar kinetic terms in MMSW gravity require a first-order auxiliary action $S_{\text{aux}} = (1/3!\rho)\int_M \epsilon_{ABCDE}\,\phi^A D\phi^B \wedge D\tau^C \wedge D\tau^D \wedge D\tau^E$, with the radial mode $\phi^5$ propagating and the four Lorentz components $\phi^a$ auxiliary. This structure is forced by SO(1,4) covariance and was implicit in Paper -1's §II B inheritance from Stelle-West 1980 but never made explicit.

Five computational shore cycles ran in parallel-and-sequential mode. Cycle 1 (DBI tree-level $\pi$-$\chi$ mixing rescue) DEAD: $m_{\text{mix}}^2 = 0$ at tree level, no bilinear coupling source. Cycle 2 (Path B candidate enumeration): five candidates surveyed, A and B killed by $\epsilon$-index gymnastics, B-B promoted to quantitative test. Cycle 3 (Path B-B Einstein-Cartan torsion elimination) DEAD: $\beta'\cdot a_1 = -(4/3)\alpha m^2/(v+\rho)$ fails the criterion $\beta'\cdot a_1 > 2/3$ by sign. Cycle 4 (Weyl rescaling to Einstein frame) HEALTHY: $\hat{S} = \int\sqrt{-\hat{g}}\,[\hat{R} - (3/2)(F'/F)^2 \hat{g}^{\mu\nu}\partial_\mu\rho\,\partial_\nu\rho + \dots]$ with healthy sign, canonical scalar $\psi = \sqrt{3}\,\ln((v+\rho)/v)$. Cycle 5 (Langenscheidt 2019 reconnaissance) confirms the auxiliary-field formulation as the principled in-frame resolution, equivalent to the Weyl-rescaling result via field redefinition.

The sub-shore opens four new sorrys (S-MIX-005 through S-MIX-008), adds three exclusion reservoir entries (ER-MIX-001 through ER-MIX-003), contributes two linter rules (LINT-20, LINT-21), and adds one structural finding (SF-MIX-001). Tier 4 §4.3 (Brane Action) updated with explicit auxiliary-field structure. Paper -1 v3 patch v3 (in preparation) supersedes patch v2 with §II B addition (auxiliary action), §II E reframing (frame consistency), §III D constraint update (auxiliary EOMs replace $\Pi_A = 0$), and explicit verification of §VI and §VIII robustness. Paper -1 §VIII BD-ghost theorem and §VI No-Go Lemma both unaffected (independent of Higgs kinetic structure). Framework's two graviton plus one radion content preserved. $v(F_Q)$ phenomenology window preserved: the radion propagates and the $F_Q$ coupling remains intact via $\chi$ identified with the canonical Einstein-frame scalar (in Einstein-frame display) or with $\phi^5$ (in the auxiliary-field display).

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, the rank-deficiency reading of the v4.9 §VI principal symbol was a real structural threat, and the resolution required investigating beyond the framework's own canon. The Langenscheidt thesis sat outside the corpus despite being the dedicated treatment of exactly this obstruction in MMSW gravity; the frontier-sentinel skill should target external theses and structurally adjacent monographs alongside the standard arXiv preprint stream. Second, three convergent routes (Weyl rescaling, Langenscheidt auxiliary fields, Jordan-Brans-Dicke equivalence) reached the same answer through different formal apparatus. Triangulation across formally distinct derivations is a stronger correctness signal than two-source verification within a single formalism (the LINT-19 standard). Third, parallel-and-sequential shore execution worked: Cycles 1, 2, 3, 5 ran in parallel; Cycle 4 was launched after Cycles 2 and 3 returned partial results that motivated the Weyl rescaling test specifically. The sequential dependency between Cycles 2/3 and Cycle 4 was load-bearing; running all five fully in parallel would have wasted compute on Path B-A (add-by-hand) which became unnecessary once Cycle 4 returned HEALTHY. Fourth, the frame-mixing diagnosis of Paper -1 §II E (displaying $(v+\rho)^2 R$ alongside $-(\partial\rho)^2$ as a single-frame action) is a cautionary instance of LINT-20 in action: the inconsistency was inherited unchanged from a phenomenological parametrization without explicit frame specification, and persisted across two patch revisions before the v4.10 audit caught it.

**Cross-program resonance.** The auxiliary-field structure required for MMSW Higgs kinetics resonates with similar patterns in other pre-geometric gauge-theoretic gravity constructions (Tresguerres, Mielke). The resonance is currently a parking observation; if confirmed structural, it suggests a deeper unification of the auxiliary-field requirement across pre-geometric formulations. Deferred to a future obstruction-resonance check once Paper -1 v3 is finalized; not on the critical path. The Biot-Savart cross-program resonance flagged in v4.9 (between the MM bulk constraint algebra and the NS algebraic null direction work) remains open, separate from this sub-shore.

**SF-DG-009.3: Higgs Sub-Sector Discharge Sub-Shore (v4.11, April 2026)**

This sub-shore operates within the parent SF-DG-009.2 (v4.10 Higgs kinetic-term resolution) and addresses the gating sorry left open by that resolution: whether the auxiliary-field reformulation actually preserves the framework's 2 graviton plus 1 radion DOF count under explicit Dirac-Bergmann analysis. A three-cycle ChatGPT pipeline (S-MIX-005, S-MIX-005a, S-MIX-005b) ran sequentially against Paper -1 v3 and Langenscheidt 2019. Cycle 1 verified primary count 45 with Gauss algebra closure including the matter $\phi_{[A}\Pi_{B]}$ term. Cycle 2 surfaced an arithmetic finding that became a structural correction: the 5×5 Higgs primary block has rank 2 (not the rank-4 implicit in the v4.10 framing), with three null primary combinations orthogonal to the kinetic projection vector $f_a$. The cycle also surfaced a sign error in S-MIX-005's bracket display ($\{Z^{\text{aux}}_a, Z_5\}$ is generically $+2 f_a \delta^3$, not the cancelled form). Cycle 3 verified that the three null primaries are promoted to second-class via secondary constraints derived from Langenscheidt's algebraic auxiliary equation, projected onto the orthogonal subspace $H_f$. Bracket matrix rank 3, total Higgs sub-sector second-class rank 8. Configuration-space robustness confirmed across flat tetrad, generic broken-Lorentz vacuum, and curved background.

The sub-shore graduates S-MIX-005 from CONFIRMED CONDITIONAL on (S-MM-002 + S-MIX-005a + Higgs sub-sector handling) to CONFIRMED CONDITIONAL on S-MM-002 alone, closes S-MIX-005a (NEEDS REFINEMENT, refinement was reframe to S-MIX-005b), and closes S-MIX-005b as CONFIRMED at the Higgs sub-sector level. Two structural findings (SF-MIX-002 first-order matter primary block rank 2 with secondary promotion; SF-MIX-003 orthogonal projection of algebraic auxiliary EOM gives Gram-matrix rank). Two linter rules (LINT-22 explicit secondary-promotion verification for first-order matter; LINT-23 distinguish new conditionality from restatement of existing scope). Three corpus entries. Tier 4 §4.3 annotation updated with explicit Higgs sub-sector rank account. Paper -1 v3 patch v3 §III D specification updated: the auxiliary-field reformulation is now backed by an explicit Dirac-Bergmann walk producing rank 8 in the Higgs sub-sector second-class block. Framework architectural prediction strengthened: from "DOF = 3 conditional on S-MM-002 + S-MIX-005a + Higgs sub-sector handling" to "DOF = 3 conditional on S-MM-002 alone, with Higgs sub-sector explicitly discharged."

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, the v4.10 closure of S-MIX-005 implicitly assumed a rank-4 primary block; the assumption was framing-error rather than computation-error, and surfaced only when Cycle 2 was forced to make the rank explicit. LINT-22 codifies the discipline: first-order matter sectors require secondary-promotion verification, not primary-block-only analysis. Second, the sign-error correction in Cycle 2 was a clean instance of the verification cycle catching its own predecessor: the corrected bracket structure is what made the orthogonal-projection rank computation in Cycle 3 work, while the cancelled form would have led to a different (incorrect) rank decomposition. Third, the CONFIRMED WITH CAVEAT verdict from Cycle 3 looked superficially like new conditionality but was a restatement of the already-open S-MM-002 scope. LINT-23 codifies the discipline of identifying which open sorry a caveat reduces to, rather than treating every caveat as additional debt.

**Cross-program resonance.** The first-order matter primary-block rank-2 result (SF-MIX-002) generalizes beyond MMSW: it is a structural feature of any first-order matter Lagrangian where canonical momenta are linear in fields rather than velocities. Standard examples include BF theory with matter, Dirac fermions in canonical analysis, and Stelle-West compensators. The framework's reliance on auxiliary-field formulations places this pattern in the load-bearing class for any future framework component touching the matter sector. Deferred to a future obstruction-resonance check.

**SF-DG-009.4: S-MM-002 Cycle Chain Closure Sub-Shore (v4.12, April 2026)**

This sub-shore operates within the parent SF-DG-009.1/009.3 chain and addresses the central remaining gating sorry from v4.11: whether the full 44×44 Dirac matrix achieves Douglis-Nirenberg ellipticity. A six-cycle ChatGPT pipeline (preliminary, S-MM-002a, S-MM-002b, S-MM-002α, S-MM-002β, S-MM-002γ) advanced the question through progressive structural-reasoning iteration without producing unconditional closure. Cycle 1 (preliminary) delivered the explicit principal symbol of the isolated 30×30 spatial connection block: $\sigma_{ZZ} = 8i\alpha (v+\rho) *_{\text{int}} \otimes \text{curl}_\xi$, rank 12, 18-dimensional kernel decomposing as 6 longitudinal Lorentz plus 12 broken-sector $a4$. Cycles 2-3 (S-MM-002a, S-MM-002b in parallel) collapsed onto a single missing input: the explicit $\mathcal{F}_i$ in the scalar-gradient secondary constraint $\mathcal{C}^{\text{scalar}}_i = \partial_i \phi^4 - \mathcal{F}_i$. Cycle 4 (S-MM-002α) refused to confabulate $\mathcal{F}_i$ and produced a conditional candidate $\mathcal{F}_i^{\text{cand}}$. Cycle 5 (S-MM-002β) reduced the remaining question to subprincipal computation: the multiplier matrix $\mathbb{P}$ has size $30 \times 35$, principal rank 12, principal-plus-Higgs rank at most 17. Cycle 6 (S-MM-002γ) delivered the explicit subprincipal entries $U_M$ and tetrad-derivative entries $\delta f_a / \delta A_i^{AB}$, and surfaced the conceptual obstruction: $U_M$ is lower differential order than $\sigma_M$ and therefore does not upgrade the principal-symbol rank in the ellipticity sense. The rank lift from 18 to the physical secondary count is configuration-dependent rather than universal-algebraic.

The sub-shore closes the S-MM-002 cycle chain (six sorrys discharged through structural-reasoning iteration), opens one new sorry (S-MM-CR, configuration-robustness theorem for the multiplier left null space rank lift), adds two structural findings (SF-MM-002 isolated $Z$-$Z$ rank 12 with kernel decomposition; SF-MM-003 subprincipal lower-order observation), adds two linter rules (LINT-24 cycle-chain refinement pattern; LINT-25 documented-debt strategy), and adds five corpus entries. The framework's DOF = 3 prediction conditionality is refactored from S-MM-002 (clean factorization of the 44×44 Dirac matrix) to S-MM-CR (configuration-robustness theorem), with the new conditionality precisely characterized rather than ambient. Paper -1 v3 patch v4 ships submission-ready with explicit conditionality on S-MM-CR.

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, the cycle-chain refinement pattern (LINT-24) worked: each cycle sharpened the question and produced reusable structural results, even though the parent sorry did not close. Refactoring toward the bottleneck derivation, rather than expanding prompt scope, is the right move when CAS-determinant questions return INDETERMINATE. Second, the documented-debt strategy (LINT-25) is the right move when a chain converges on a precisely characterized open question without closing it. Continuing to refine past the productive horizon is a drain on parallel research progress. The S-MM-CR framing converts the chain from continuing ChatGPT-cycle drain to documented research question, with explicit Paper -1 §VI conditionality. Third, the conceptual obstruction surfaced in Cycle 6 (subprincipal lower order than principal) is a generic feature of MMSW canonical analyses with auxiliary scalars, not specific to the Langenscheidt formulation. The standard MM literature on Hamiltonian constraint analysis presupposes the configuration-robustness condition without explicit derivation; the framework's explicit characterization is itself a contribution.

**Cross-program resonance.** The configuration-dependent rank lift question parallels the small-data versus large-data structure in the NS program: small-data regimes admit clean structural arguments while large-data regimes require configuration-specific verification. The pattern is worth a parking note: pre-geometric gauge-theoretic constructions and fluid-dynamic regularity programs may share the structural feature that universal-algebraic theorems are weaker than configuration-restricted theorems, and the right deliverable is a precisely characterized robustness condition rather than a universal proof. Deferred to a future obstruction-resonance check.

**SF-DG-010: Cosmological-Sector Contraction Shore (v4.13, May 2026)**

This shore integrates four deep research scouts run on a single day (May 12, 2026) into a coordinated revision of the framework's cosmological and hydrodynamic predictive surface. The scouts (sub-Chandrasekhar Type Ia phenomenology, F12 reconciliation against DESI DR2 thawing, HSB Karch-Randall moduli geometry as L^∞ surrogate, S-CC-002 instanton-generated moduli stabilization) interlocked structurally: the first established that the framework's geometric catalysis cannot drive macroscopic detonation in degenerate stellar interiors (SL-BR-1, SL-PB-1, ER-WD-001); the second established that the F12 thawing prediction fails on three independent axes (SL-AM-1, ER-COSM-001 through ER-COSM-004) and forced the retraction; the third bifurcated the C23 swampland chain into a dead hydrodynamic route (SL-VC-1, ER-WGC-001) and a conditionally salvaged geometric route (Karch-Randall moduli geometry via DBI-induced Einstein-frame Weyl rescaling); the fourth converted the salvaged route into a concrete computational sorry via the Running Coupling Rescue Theorem (SL-RC-1).

The shore retracts one Tier 3 function (F12), strikes three contracts (C12a, C12b, C12c), retracts one Swampland contract (C23-dS), reformulates two contracts (C23-WGC to static F-theory compliance, C23-SDC to conditional via Karch-Randall moduli geometry), reclassifies one empirical breakdown (B2 from anchor to falsification watch), and adds one new tracked tension (B-NU-1 neutrino mass sector friction with $\Lambda$CDM). Six exclusion reservoir entries (ER-WD-001, ER-COSM-001 through ER-COSM-004, ER-WGC-001). Five structural lessons (SL-AM-1, SL-BR-1, SL-PB-1, SL-VC-1, SL-RC-1). Two linter rules (LINT-DLR-1, LINT-L2-1). Four sorry events: S-WD-001 opened and discharged as DEAD same day; S-COSM-001 opened and discharged as DEAD same day; S-HSB-002 opened with bifurcated status (S-HSB-002a DEAD, S-HSB-002b ACTIVE conditional on S-CC-002 plus $\alpha$ computation); S-CC-002 status updated from OPEN to ACTIVE with sharpened sub-tag ($b > 1/(4\pi^2) \approx 0.0253$ for $X_{F13}$ Pati-Salam KK tower on $dP_3$ Laplacian). Four corpus entries.

The framework's axiomatic core (SO(1,4) MM gravity on Karch-Randall braneworld, $\gamma$-activation from KK heat kernel, pole structure at $\mathcal{f}_{Q,\text{crit}} \sim 10^{12}$ to $10^{13}$ GeV⁴, AM periodic potential with quantized $\Lambda^{(k)}$, ODLRO requirement, F-theory GUT Box on $dP_3$) does not move. The predictive surface contracts in the cosmological sector (F12 retracted, hydrodynamic C23-WGC retracted) and recovers partially via the conditional SDC geometric derivation and the concrete pathway to S-CC-002 closure through the RCRT. Live predictions standing as of v4.13: GUT Box phenomenology ($X_{F13}$ Pati-Salam on $dP_3$), neutron star mass prediction matching PSR J0952-0607, F19 geometric wavefunction collapse with 5D exhaust, F21 GRB 111005A torsion plus ponderomotive screening, B19 WD cooling via KK exhaust, F13.2 LENR via C13c resonant catalysis, Q-branch ONe-no-coherence interpretation, WGC static F-theory compliance, SDC conditional via moduli geometry, $g \approx 0.53$ at stabilization scale (new soft prediction from S-CC-002).

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, four scouts integrated in a single day produced a sharper structural picture than any one of them alone could have: the kill set converges on a clean identity, geometric and spectral theorems in scope versus fluid-regularity and smooth-cosmological theorems out of scope. The patterns SL-VC-1 (variance is L² not L^∞) and SL-AM-1 (kinematic dominance of trans-Planckian AM barrier over O(N) gravitationally-coupled operators) jointly explain why the v3.0 through v4.12 cosmological surface was overextended: both rest on importing fluid-dynamical or trace-channel intuitions into a regime where the framework's actual constraints are spectral and topological. Second, the documented-debt strategy from v4.12 (LINT-25) generalizes: predictive-surface retraction is a tactical move that preserves the axiomatic core at the cost of falsifiable phenomenology, and is the right move when the alternative is ambient un-resolved structural tension. Third, the RCRT (SL-RC-1) demonstrates that retracting an over-extended prediction can sharpen what remains: S-CC-002 moves from an abstract "find an instanton mechanism" sorry to a concrete one-loop beta function inequality, with a clear closure path through the ftheory-pipeline skill.

**Cross-program resonance.** The variance-channel L²-versus-L^∞ obstruction (SL-VC-1) is structurally identical to obstructions encountered in the Navier-Stokes program (the BKM L^∞ criterion versus the framework's L² QFI control was already flagged in v3.8 with the Bounding Box derivation but the import-error was not recognized until v4.13). The pattern is worth naming explicitly: when a framework's natural derivation surface is L² (geometric, spectral, ODLRO-mediated) and an external theorem demands L^∞ (regularity, pointwise amplitude), the dimensional gap is structural and cannot be bridged by variance bounds. Obstruction-resonance candidates to check: the P vs NP program (where the question is whether circuit-complexity lower bounds can be derived from average-case spectral information), the Yang-Mills mass gap program (where mass-gap proofs typically require pointwise spectral control), and the affine Grassmannian combinatorics program if any active scaffold relies on variance bounds.

**SF-DG-011: Core Identity Restructuring with Two-Path Cosmology Contingency (v4.14, May 2026)**

This shore records the framework's restructuring from v4.13 (Addazi-Meluccio static-Λ as Tier 3 core, v(F_Q) as supporting machinery) to v4.14 (v(F_Q) / N² / modular F_Q machinery foregrounded as Core Claim CC-1, AM cosmology demoted to Tier 3 branch-conditional, Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu evolving Dark Dimension prepared as Path B contingency). The shore was triggered by three post-v4.13 deep research scouts run against the question "can the framework internally reach DESI DR2 thawing without dropping AM?": Scout 1 (BH-mechanism evolving-DE candidate, killed via SL-AM-1 + SL-BR-1, producing ER-DE-001, ER-DE-002, ER-DE-003 and the dead sorry S-DE-001), Scout 3 (NEDE thermal evolving-DE candidate, killed via v3.9 generalized cosmological plasma exclusion structural lesson, producing ER-HT-001 and the dead sorry S-HT-001), Scout 4 (hairon-quintessence multi-field evolving-DE candidate, killed via LINT-DE-2 Distance Conjecture confinement and LINT-DE-3 topological-substrate dual-role conflict, producing ER-DE-004, ER-DE-005, ER-DE-006 and the dead sorry S-DE-002). The cumulative exhaustion of internal evolving-DE mechanisms within the AM-locked branch forced a structural choice: commit unconditionally to T3.6 and treat DESI DR2 as falsification watch (the v4.13 posture, narrowed and sharpened), or restructure the trellis to preserve the framework's distinctive theoretical content (CC-1) while preparing a clean alternative path (T3.6') for activation upon empirical resolution. The latter option, codified into SL-PATH-1 (two-path contingency planning), is adopted in v4.14.

The shore retracts no axiom and no prediction. It reorganizes the dependency map: Tier 0-2 carry CC-1 plus the framework's preserved kernel constraints K1-K17, Dark Dimension structural import, and the F-theory $dP_3$ + $X_{F13}$ Pati-Salam matter sector. Tier 3 splits into 3.1 (matter-sector predictions, branch-independent: F09, F11, F13, F13.2, F19, F21) and 3.2 (cosmology-sector predictions, branch-dependent: Path A {T3.6, F-CC, S-CC-005, hairon-as-vacuum-substrate} versus Path B {T3.6', F-DD-Evolve, hairon-role-modified}). The framework's external positioning leads with CC-1 and its matter-sector predictions, with the cosmology choice framed as a downstream contingent application (LINT-CORE-1). Path A remains the current working hypothesis; Path B is prepared as a discharge-ready contingency activated upon DESI Y5 / Euclid confirmation of evolving $w(z)$ at $\geq 5\sigma$.

Six exclusion reservoir entries (ER-DE-001 BH-mechanism, ER-DE-002 vacuum-driven reheating, ER-DE-003 quantum-foam trans-Planckian, ER-DE-004 multi-modulus slow-roll, ER-DE-005 hairon-quintessence single-field, ER-DE-006 hairon-quintessence multi-field), one preserved (ER-HT-001 NEDE thermal). Three new structural lessons (SL-CORE-1, SL-CONT-1 with Addendum A revision, SL-PATH-1). Four new linter rules (LINT-CORE-1, LINT-DE-2, LINT-DE-3, LINT-PATH-1). Nine sorry events: three opened-and-discharged DEAD same shore (S-DE-001, S-DE-002, S-HT-001); one active Path A specific (S-CC-007); four dormant Path B specific (S-DD-001 through S-DD-004); one dormant Path B variant (S-CC-002'). Three additional active Vafa-lab compatibility sorries (S-AM-008, S-AM-009, S-AM-010) added per Addendum A.

The shore is paired with Addendum A (the Baykara-Chen-Vafa repositioning revision), generated five days after the initial v4.14 draft in response to Baykara-Chen-Vafa arXiv:2605.16484v1 (May 15, 2026). The addendum revises the framework's external positioning: the dS swampland bound $|\nabla V|/V \geq 2/\sqrt{d-2}$ applies asymptotically at weak coupling, not in the interior of moduli space where the AM minimum sits; Vafa-lab is actively constructing isolated critical points of $V$ in d=4 via enhanced gauge symmetry from Scherk-Schwarz spin-structure modification, with the sign of $V$ undetermined at those points; the framework's AM static-Λ commitment occupies one specific structural position within the broader Vafa-lab interior-moduli-space program rather than a contrarian position. The two-path structure (Path A interior-moduli-space critical point via AM topological quantization; Path B evolving Dark Dimension via Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu) mirrors the two active Vafa-lab research directions. SL-CONT-1 is revised per the addendum; three new sorries (S-AM-008, S-AM-009, S-AM-010) track Vafa-lab compatibility tasks. Bayesian credence on Path A revised upward from a rough 10-25% to a rough 25-40%, with Path B at 25-40% and 20-50% mass on alternative resolutions including systematic-artifact dissipation of the DESI signal.

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, the v4.14 restructuring demonstrates that predictive-surface retraction (v4.13) and structural reorganization (v4.14) are two distinct moves with different costs. Retraction loses falsifiable phenomenology in exchange for preserving the axiomatic core. Reorganization preserves both the axiomatic core and the predictive surface but redistributes load-bearing weight across the tier structure; the cost is the discipline required to maintain the new dependency map under future shocks (LINT-CORE-1 captures this discipline). Second, two-path contingency planning (SL-PATH-1) is appropriate when the empirical resolution is on a fixed timeline (DESI Y5, Euclid) and a structurally clean alternative exists; it is inappropriate when the alternative is itself ambient or when the empirical resolution timeline is indefinite (in which case the right move is documented debt per LINT-25). Third, the Addendum A revision arrived five days after the initial v4.14 update and corrected the framework's external positioning without changing any axiom or path commitment. This is a clean instance of positioning-as-research: a paper from outside the framework (Baykara-Chen-Vafa) sharpened the framework's self-understanding of its position within the broader research landscape, generating three new compatibility sorries (S-AM-008 through S-AM-010) and revising one structural lesson (SL-CONT-1) without disturbing the framework's actual theoretical content. The pattern is worth naming: when a high-quality external paper appears in an adjacent domain, the trellis discipline includes both technical evaluation (does this affect any sorry?) and positioning evaluation (does this change the framework's external description?). Both are documented; both can produce revisions; both leave the core unchanged.

**Cross-program resonance.** The two-path contingency pattern (SL-PATH-1) generalizes beyond the cosmology branch. Candidates for analogous restructuring in other active programs: (i) the Navier-Stokes regularity program, where the small-data vs large-data structure could be formalized as two paths with distinct discharge requirements, conditional on which regime the next round of investigations resolves; (ii) the P vs NP program, where the Zhegalkin polynomial density candidate (and its competitors) could be elevated to a path structure with explicit triggers; (iii) the agentic systems / Constitutional Kernel program, where decentralized-vs-centralized governance trade-offs could carry a parallel two-path structure. Each candidate would require its own analysis to determine whether the "structurally clean alternative" condition of SL-PATH-1 is met. Deferred to future obstruction-resonance checks.
