**SF-DG-011 (Refresh Duality): Refresh Duality and Matter-Sector Closure (v4.15, June 12, 2026)**

*Numbering note: this shore self-labels SF-DG-011, the same designation the v4.14 core-identity restructuring carries. The two are distinguished by version and date (v4.14 restructuring, May 2026; v4.15 refresh duality, June 2026). The cross-references inside the three June shores are internally consistent under their own numbering and are preserved as written; renumbering the June shores to SF-DG-012/013/014 is a clean future bookkeeping move but was not imposed here.*

This shore is the verified contraction half of the Refresh Duality session. It closes the matter-sector activation question that has gated the framework since OP-0 opened at v4.4. The instrument is the matter-sector exclusion record v1, which supersedes the v4.7 unconditional OP-0 resolution by splitting OP-0 into two components with opposite fates. OP-0-COUPLING (the $\gamma$ derivation, the pole form, the threshold $F_{Q,\text{crit}} = 16\pi^2 m_\rho^2 \Lambda_s^2/c_{\text{KK}}$) stands as derived machinery and gains independent corroboration this shore. OP-0-ACTIVATION (the claim that some matter substrate reaches the threshold) closes DEAD: the compound budget of $10^{27}$ to $10^{29}$ GeV⁴ rested on super-extensive Var(T), which the exclusion record kills on five independent arguments (volume-law FDT scaling, decoherence of GHZ-class states, dimensional pinning of the conversion, and two failed vehicle searches). The threshold sits 12 to 25 orders above what any audited equilibrium or driven laboratory substrate supplies. The pole is real in the Lagrangian and dormant in every known matter environment; its one confirmed activation domain is horizon-scale physics, where saturation coincides with the holographic bound. CC-1 is demoted from foregrounded core to conditional structure. The matter-sector activation chain (F13, F13.2, F19, F21, F05 and the C13/C21 contracts) moves to the exclusion reservoir, governed by the exclusion record's three-gate reactivation test: a coupling other than species-summed $G_N$, a real-observable vehicle, and substrate survival of the required coherence.

The generative result of the session's first half is the refresh duality (the structural finding SF-DG-012, banked here). The state-dependent VEV mechanism admits an exact dual description as registration latency. The dictionary: the $\phi$-norm is geometry's registration capacity; $\gamma F_Q$ consumption of the VEV is queue utilization $u = F_Q/F_{Q,\text{crit}}$; $G_{\text{eff}} = G/(1-u)$ is the latency factor of a saturating channel; radion softening $m_{\text{eff}}^2 = m_\rho^2(1-u)$ is bandwidth exhaustion; $v_{\text{eff}} \to 0$ is queue overflow, which is local symmetry restoration to the pre-geometric SO(1,4) phase. The registration bandwidth is set by the softest geometric mode (the radion frequency), with the species scale supplying per-channel stiffness. The duality pays exactly two rents. First, the parameter-free queue-capacity formula $\Lambda_s^4/N_{\text{eff}} = \Lambda_s^6/M_{\text{Pl}}^2 = 2.1\times10^{12}$ GeV⁴ reproduces $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$ at $c_{\text{KK}}\sim5$ with zero fitted parameters, a soft prediction registered against OP-CK. Second, equating the two threshold expressions yields the radion mass equality $m_\rho = \sqrt{c_{\text{KK}}}\,\Lambda_s^2/(4\pi M_{\text{Pl}}) = 0.44$ to $1.4$ MeV across $c_{\text{KK}} \in [1,10]$, which is C-RD-1: a two-sided prediction landing at the bottom edge of the v4.8 adiabaticity window where the framework independently sits. Everything else the duality produces is interpretive; it adds no magnitude to any matter-sector budget and rescues nothing the exclusion record killed. The frame question (Einstein versus Jordan assignment of matter and gravity under the Weyl factor) is open (S-FRAME).

One erratum was corrected (E-1): the 4D geometric-mean species-scale display $\Lambda_s^{\text{ambient}} \sim \sqrt{M_{\text{Pl}} m_{\text{KK}}}$ with $N \sim 10^{32}$ is stale by five orders in $\Lambda_s$ and ten in $N$; the correct 5D values $\Lambda_s = M_5 = (M_{\text{Pl}}^2 m_{\text{KK}})^{1/3} \sim 2.6\times10^8$ GeV and $N_{\text{eff}} \sim 2\times10^{21}$ were already used in all v4.7+ quantitative work, so the erratum is confined to the §4.6 display line and the Appendix C notation entry, with an audit obligation logged as S-E1-AUDIT. Two new structural lessons (SL-SUSC-1 the susceptibility exclusion, SL-RD-1 dual descriptions pay rent through unique predictions), one new linter rule (LINT-SUSC-1), one new conditional contract (C-RD-1).

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, a kill and a generation can arrive in the same session and must be kept on separate tiers: the exclusion record is verified, the refresh ontology is a dual description whose only verified output is C-RD-1, and conflating "we found a beautiful reframe" with "we found new physics" is exactly the error SL-RD-1 names. Second, the susceptibility exclusion (SL-SUSC-1) is the structural reason the matter sector closed, and it is domain-neutral: it shows up as protected-versus-adaptive in the ethics trellis, as variety-versus-persistence resolved by subsidiarity in the Constitutional Kernel, and as natural-versus-useful and robustness-versus-amortization in the P vs NP program. The shore exports it to the meta-trellis as a candidate Tier 0 rule. Third, the matter-sector closure is honest rather than evasive: it reduces the sector to two named live items (the rescue-trellis torsion-Lagrangian calculation and the quantum-reference-frame loophole), both with likely-negative priors, so either verdict closes the sector cleanly rather than leaving ambient debt.

**Cross-program resonance.** The protection/variance exclusion is filed in the obstruction catalog beside moment/winding factorization (Navier-Stokes) and inside/outside asymmetry, with a single trigger question for any program: is the required-robust band disjoint from the required-sensitive band? The statics/dynamics two-metric split surfaced here (SLD for resolution, BKM for dissipation) mirrors the Constitutional Kernel's accounting/flow split and the Carlen-Maas gradient-flow structure: circulation plus dissipative descent on different state spaces. The quantum Damköhler number $Da_Z$ that orders the candidate substrates is the physics instance of the $(\text{Péclet}, \text{Damköhler})$ regime discipline the ethics trellis uses (S-14): einselection is the high-$Da$ copying regime of the environment-as-ledger.

**SF-DG-012 (Ontology Companion): Ontology Exploration and the Laminar Timescale Correction (Speculation Quarantine, June 13, 2026)**

This is the generation/quarantine companion to the refresh-duality shore. It records the speculative arc that followed the verified contraction and isolates it so it cannot contaminate the verified ledger. The document is a Speculation Ledger: every entry is flagged Unverified and carries two explicit unpaid bills, the GENERATOR bill (does the coordinate couple to the operator gravity reads, translational stress-energy, rather than to spin or electronic structure) and the MAGNITUDE bill (is the amplitude within orders of any bound). Nothing in it is load-bearing or citable. The single exception, promotable to the verified ledger, is a structural correction to a prior kill rather than a new claim.

That one real result is the laminar clock-quarantine of the torsion timescale. The hypothesis that propagating torsion supplies the held-open interval in which a decision models its alternatives had been killed on timescale: the torsion clock $\hbar/\Lambda_T \sim 6.6\times10^{-24}$ s against deliberation at $\sim10^{-1}$ s, a gap of 22 orders, declared dead because a slow process cannot run inside fast dynamics. The kill assumed a single shared control loop. The laminar split, validated independently in the grid-operating-system domain (a fast autonomous edge controller at 5 to 20 ms and a slow governance controller at hours to days, coupled only by parameter-setting and an algedonic interrupt), shows that two processes separated by many orders in clock rate are not in conflict, they are quarantined: each runs at its native clock, the slow layer configures the fast layer and reads exceptions from it without participating in the fast loop, and large separation is cleaner quarantine, not worse. The timescale sub-objection is therefore answered without being paid, superseded by two interface obligations (S-LAM-IF-UP, S-LAM-IF-DOWN) and left downstream of the generator gate. This changes the status of one sub-objection only; it does not revive the torsion matter-sector claim (still governed by S-TORSION-LAGRANGIAN) and is restated as verified at v4.16 (SF-DG-013 Part A.4).

A near-coincidence was also dissolved before it could become a load-bearing intuition: the species count $N_{\text{eff}} \sim 10^{21.3}$, the species/Planck clock ratio $M_{\text{Pl}}/\Lambda_s \sim 10^{10.7}$ (= $\sqrt{N_{\text{eff}}}$), and the torsion/cognition clock ratio $\sim 10^{22.2}$ are three different numbers that merely collide near $10^{22}$. The torsion/cognition ratio is built from a nuclear scale and a biological deliberation time and slides with the deliberation time; it is not $N_{\text{eff}}$. The recurring structure in the corpus is the seesaw $\Lambda_s^2 = M_{\text{Pl}}\times(\text{low scale})$, which yields the MeV radion (C-RD-1) and a keV-ish companion, not a universal $10^{22}$.

The speculative arc itself (SL-EXP-01 through SL-EXP-10) is recorded with bills and is uniformly negative on the matter-to-geometry question. The F_Q-pixel carve and Born-sphere ontology turn four reservoir entries into corollaries but reproduce the existing radion machinery exactly rather than founding a successor (deflated by the refresh-duality computation). Born enforcement / gravitization of QM is an axiom attack on standard QM supported by elegance only. The susceptibility exclusion as empirical-face funnel is the strongest pattern: five routes converge on the gravitational-noise observable (stochastic G), which uses the correct generator and is the most defensible branch, with its magnitude unknown until S-NOISE is computed. Life as pixel-wall maintainer is dead on generator and magnitude (biological gradients are classical, anti-coherent in exactly the channel a pixel wall needs). Qualia as coherent F_Q carries a recorded retraction of an in-session overclaim and a surviving separability statement (hard-problem solution and gravity coupling are distinct bills). The N_eff-coherence/error-correction route is the cleanest statement of the matter sector's last conceivable life and stalls on a likely-unpayable power bill. DNA as error correction confirms classical QEC and gates the quantum reading on an orthogonality requirement that pulls against the coupling requirement through the same parameter. Laminar cognition survives as a gravity-agnostic deliberation architecture independent of whether the fast layer is quantum.

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, accumulated speculative surface area is a hazard to the verified ledger and deserves explicit quarantine: flagging every entry Unverified with named bills is what keeps a generative session from silently promoting elegance into the corpus. Second, the falsify-cheap-first discipline orders the work correctly: the two cheapest decisive tests (S-QFI-DEATH, a living-versus-freshly-dead collective-QFI measurement; S-DNA-DFS, whether DNA repair maintains a decoherence-free subspace) are gravity-agnostic and should precede any attempt on the generator gate, because a null there closes the biology arc without needing the framework at all. Third, a kill can be a status change rather than a death: the laminar correction reopened a closed timescale objection not by paying its bill but by showing the bill was mis-posed (clock separation is quarantine, not conflict), which is a distinct and legitimate move that the trellis should record as QUARANTINED-PENDING-INTERFACE rather than either DEAD or live.

**Cross-program resonance.** The laminar split is itself an imported isomorphism from the AVF Grid Operating System architecture (a fast physics-layer controller and a slow governance-layer controller coupled only by parameter-passing and algedonic interrupt). The same two-layer, clock-quarantined, algedonic-coupled shape appears in the Constitutional Kernel's VSM architecture and in the ethics trellis's establishment/maintenance split. The structural claim worth tracking across programs: when two subsystems must run at incommensurable rates, do not seek a shared loop; quarantine them and couple only through parameters and exception channels.

**SF-DG-013 (Cumulant Reorganization): The Cumulant Reorganization (v4.16, June 13, 2026)**

This is the third shore of the Refresh Duality session and the one that promotes verified-tier structure to the parent core. It mixes tiers deliberately and labels each: Part A is verified (computed, promoted to v4.16), Part B is live-sorry-tier (calculations that survived their first kill and are gated on one named computation each, not results), Part C is open-questions speculation. The most common error of the session was mis-ranking a consistency check as a derivation; this shore exists partly to prevent that error from entering the corpus.

The headline result is the cumulant reorganization. The matter-state functional that couples to geometry is not quantum Fisher information acting as the source; it is the modular free energy $W(\epsilon) = \log\langle e^{-\epsilon K}\rangle$, the cumulant generating functional of the modular Hamiltonian $K$, whose cumulants fill the three coupling roles with fixed unit weights. The first cumulant $\langle K\rangle$ (modular energy) is the source, manifestly stress-energy coupled because the modular Hamiltonian of a region is an integral of $T_{\mu\nu}$ (Bisognano-Wichmann for wedges); this dissolves the generator gap, because geometry reading modular energy is automatically stress-energy coupling, no bridge required. The second cumulant $\langle\delta K^2\rangle$ (modular variance) is the stiffness, and it is the quantum Fisher information (canonical energy = QFI, Lashkari-Van Raamsdonk); $F_Q$ lives here, at second order, controlling the pole, not at first order as the source. The third cumulant (non-Gaussianity) is the predicted, uncomputed leading correction. $F_Q$ is not wrong, it is mis-ranked: hired as the source, it is in fact the stiffness. What makes this verified rather than speculative is that three independent anchors each force their weight to unity, and the forced weights are exactly the cumulant coefficients: the entanglement first law forces source = first cumulant, canonical-energy = QFI forces stiffness = second cumulant, and horizon entropy $S_{dS} = \langle K\rangle_{\text{horizon}}$ forces capacity = first cumulant at saturation. Anchors A and C use the same functional with the same weight in two regimes, which is a consistency check the reorganization passes. The assembly into $W(\epsilon)$ from DG's own coupling is what remains to be derived (S-CUMULANT-DERIVE).

Two further verified items promote with it. The convexity selection rule: the modular variance is non-negative, so $W$ is convex, so the matter $F_Q$ channel can only soften geometry, never stiffen it. Matter softens, only the vacuum stiffens. This is a sign-sanity check for every future matter-sector calculation and is codified as LINT-CONVEX-1 [HARD MODE]; the class blocks it forbids (chameleon stiffening, matter-driven UV-softening, density-induced repulsion or antigravity, geometric stiffness tracking the nuclear EOS) are all stiffening from the matter channel. The catastrophe count: the registration sector is a codimension-two cusp catastrophe with controls $(g F_Q - \lambda v_0^2, -h_0\cos\theta)$, proven stable against the entire KK tower because heavy modes are Gaussian-and-bilinear and integrate out to renormalize the $\phi^2$ coefficient only, never generating an independent $\phi^3$ or new $\phi^1$. The trans-sector fold (a single pleated surface multiplexing one cognitive control axis and one geometric control axis) is closed through the tower route. The only surviving route is a codimension-three umbilic requiring a second light scalar degenerate with the radion (S-SECOND-LIGHT-SCALAR, decidable by a spectrum calculation in the existing dP_3 F-theory model). The cusp point sits exactly at the CC-1 pole / symmetry-restoration value, coinciding with the refresh-duality threshold of SF-DG-012, which pairs verified catastrophe geometry with C-RD-1.

The deepest structural shift is the reclassification of S-GEN. The generator gate is no longer an independent frontier sorry; it is the output of S-CUMULANT-DERIVE. The wall that closed the matter sector and gated the entire biology arc is reinterpreted as a rank-confusion in the modular expansion, the same error family as ER-PXR-002 (metric job-conflation) and the OP-0 origin (SL-RANK-1). S-NOISE (the parameter-free radion-mediated decoherence spectrum that decides whether DG has a live laboratory empirical face or a purely cosmological one) moves downstream of S-CUMULANT-DERIVE, since the generator identity it relies on is what the cumulant derivation establishes. Part B logs two live-but-gated calculations that are explicitly not results: the cumulant derivation itself (consistency-checked, not derived) and the LENR transient-exhaust route. The exhaust route is the live one for the priority target: the matter sector stays dead as a rate mechanism but is potentially open as a transient single-event coherent emission, where conventional screening does the in-channel and the bulk does the radiationless out-channel. It survives the wall that closed everything else because the bill is instantaneous coherence rather than standing power, because $N_{\text{coh}} = (\Lambda_s/E)^2 \sim 6.8\times10^{22}$ matches the available $N_{\text{eff}} \sim 2.2\times10^{21}$ to within $\sim31\times$ (the match is structural, holding because nuclear transition energies sit at the seesaw scale $E\sim\Lambda_s^2/M_{\text{Pl}}$), and because the fusion event is faster than decoherence in the de-excitation window. It is gated entirely on S-EXHAUST-COHERENCE (does a fusion product couple superradiantly to the degenerate KK/species tower within $\sim10^{-15}$ s) with a second gate behind it (S-EXHAUST-COLOCATION, do the screening and high-F_Q conditions co-locate or does the susceptibility exclusion separate them). Part C logs five open questions as characterized speculation, none load-bearing, the most interesting being whether DG's natural holography is a de Sitter correspondence probed via the double-scaled SYK chord algebra.

**Lessons for the trellis methodology.** First, the session's recurring error (mis-ranking a consistency check as a derivation) is exactly why the tiering is explicit and labeled: a three-anchor weight-forcing that passes a consistency check is verified-tier as a reorganization but does not promote the underlying derivation, which stays a live sorry (S-CUMULANT-DERIVE). Second, a result can dissolve a long-standing obstruction by reclassifying it rather than solving it: the generator gap, which gated the matter and biology sectors for the whole session, turns out to be an order error in the modular expansion, and naming the error family (SL-RANK-1) is more valuable than any single fix. Third, a sign rule earns its place in the linter when the framework's recurring failure mode is sign-and-order confusion: LINT-CONVEX-1 lets a future calculation that comes out stiffening geometry be rejected immediately, before anything else is checked.

**Cross-program resonance.** The order-and-rank confusion family (SL-RANK-1) is a candidate obstruction-resonance entry for every program that uses information-geometric or modular objects: the question to ask is whether a quantity has been hired for a role one order away from where it belongs. The convexity-as-sign-sanity discipline generalizes to any program with a one-signed potential and a recurring sign-error history (the thermodynamic-solvency accounting and the ethics trellis's dissipative-descent structure are candidates). The de Sitter / DSSYK probe (OQ-1) connects DG's horizon registration-cell Fisher structure to the double-scaled SYK chord algebra; if they are the same boundary object from two sides, dS/CFT gains a controlled example with a bulk interpretation, which is a cross-program bridge to the solvable-dual literature rather than a DG-internal claim.

# 6. v4.14 UPDATE MODULE: CORE IDENTITY RESTRUCTURING WITH BRANCHING COSMOLOGY PATHS

This section integrates the full v4.14 update module (Section 19 per the integration procedure of the source update document) into the trellis as a self-contained reference for the core-vs-contingent restructuring. The content covers the rationale for the restructuring, the Core Identity Statement, Path A (static-Λ AM-locked) and Path B (variable-Λ Bedroya-Vafa-aligned) specifications, selection criteria, trellis element updates, the SF-DG-011 shore record reference, and external communication implications. Sections that already appear elsewhere in the trellis (the axiom reorganization in §1, the exclusion reservoir entries in §5, the structural lessons and linter rules in §5) are summarized here with cross-references rather than duplicated in full.

## 6.1 Restructuring Rationale

The v4.13 trellis treated the Addazi-Meluccio topological quantization mechanism (T3.6, F-CC, S-CC-005) and the static-Λ commitment derived from it as a load-bearing Tier-3 axiom alongside the v(F_Q) / N² / modular F_Q machinery. Empirically this elevated the framework's most exposed bet (static Λ contra Vafa's dS swampland conjecture, per the strong-form reading later refined in Addendum A) to the same structural prominence as its most distinctive theoretical contribution (gravity coupled to coherent matter via super-extensive Fisher information). The conflation carried two costs.

First, it concentrated the framework's identity in a place where it was most likely to be falsified. If DESI Y5 confirms thawing at 5σ, the headline result reads "framework wrong about cosmology," which obscures that the v(F_Q) / N² physics survives the falsification intact and continues to generate predictions in compact-object astrophysics, condensed matter (LUNA), gravitational-wave phenomenology, and possibly cold-atom experiments.

Second, it forced the framework into unnecessary external tension. The AM mechanism is one specific way of using the radion's potential structure; the v(F_Q) coupling does not require it. By treating AM as core, the framework adopted a contrarian position against mainline Swampland phenomenology that was incidental to its actual novel content. (Addendum A subsequently refines the "contrarian" framing: per Baykara-Chen-Vafa arXiv:2605.16484v1, the dS swampland bound applies asymptotically at weak coupling, and Vafa-lab is actively constructing interior-moduli-space critical points; the framework is one structural position within the broader Vafa-lab program rather than contrarian to it.)

The v4.14 restructuring reorganizes the trellis to foreground the v(F_Q) / N² / modular F_Q machinery as the framework's core identity and demotes the AM cosmology-sector commitments to a Tier-3 contingent hypothesis with an explicit alternative path (Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu evolving Dark Dimension) prepared as fallback. The restructuring does not invalidate any axiom. It reorganizes the dependency map and modifies the framework's external positioning.

## 6.2 Core Identity Restatement

The framework's central theoretical claim, foregrounded in Tier 0-2 per §1.0:

**Core claim (CC-1):** Gravity couples to the modular-Hamiltonian Fisher information of the matter sector via the state-dependent VEV $v(F_Q)$ of the SO(1,4) gravitational Higgs, with super-extensive O(N²) scaling for ODLRO matter states. The coupling exhibits a pole structure at $F_{Q,\text{crit}}$ that produces qualitatively distinct gravitational responses below and above threshold.

Constituent commitments preserved across both branches: K1-K6 (5D Karch-Randall braneworld plus MM gravity plus mandatory topological bulk), K7-K17 (kernel constraints on Newton's constant, KK adiabatic stability, BBN structural immunity), Formulation B ($F_Q = \text{Var}(K_{\text{mod}})$ with Donnelly-Freidel edge modes on finite causal diamonds), the $v(F_Q)$ coupling generating F19 (geometric wavefunction collapse at the pole), F09 (KK exhaust from compact objects), F13 (LUNA screening anomaly resolution), F21 (GRB compact-object phenomenology), F11 (KK gravitons as dark matter, partially via this coupling), Dark Dimension structural import (Montero-Vafa-Valenzuela arXiv:2205.12293; static-vs-evolving status of $R$ moved to the contingent cosmology layer), and F-theory $dP_3$ + $X_{F13}$ Pati-Salam matter sector.

The framework is a theory of gravity-matter coupling in which gravity responds to the coherent structure of the matter state through a state-dependent Higgs VEV with super-extensive Fisher-information scaling, embedded in a 5D Karch-Randall braneworld with Dark Dimension content. The framework's most distinctive empirical predictions live in compact-object astrophysics, condensed-matter screening, and gravitational-wave phenomenology. The cosmology-sector application is a downstream commitment with two prepared paths depending on DESI Y5 + Euclid resolution.

## 6.3 Path A: Static-Λ (AM-Locked) Cosmology Branch

**Status as of v4.14:** Current working hypothesis. Selected as long as DESI thawing remains below 5σ and the Addazi-Meluccio program continues to develop.

**Commitments.** T3.6 (AM topological quantization): $\Lambda$ is quantized into a discrete tower $\Lambda^{(k)}$ via the periodic Addazi-Meluccio potential $V_{AM}(\rho) = -\frac{1}{2}\mu_\rho^2 v^2 \cos(c Y_{MM} (\rho/v - v))$ with barrier height $\sim 10^{32}$ GeV⁴ (Addazi-Meluccio arXiv:2602.16840). F-CC (entropic SSB selection): The physical sector $k_{\text{phys}} \sim S_{\text{dS}} \sim 10^{122}$ is selected via SSB with entropic weighting matching the de Sitter horizon entropy. S-CC-005 (inter-sector tunneling protection): Inter-sector transitions suppressed by $e^{-S_{\text{dS}}} = e^{-10^{122}}$, eternally stable within the current cosmic epoch. Hairon-as-vacuum-substrate: The de Sitter vacuum is identified with a Bose-Einstein condensate of $N \sim 10^{120}$ hairon moduli from the $S^4/\mathbb{Z}_N$ orbifold instanton construction (Addazi-Meluccio arXiv:2604.26982). Hairons mediate BCS-like neutrino superfluid condensation at $T_c \sim$ meV, providing a CDM candidate channel.

**Cosmological prediction.** Static $\Lambda^{(k_{\text{phys}})}$ within the current cosmic epoch. Equation of state $w = -1$ to within experimental precision. The DESI DR2 thawing signature ($w_0 \approx -0.67$, $w_a \approx -1.0$) is treated as an external observational anomaly subject to falsification watch.

**Solution to the cosmological constant problem.** The bare $\Lambda$ is not fine-tuned; it is selected from a discrete tower by entropic SSB. The matching $k_{\text{phys}} \sim S_{\text{dS}}$ is structurally forced by the AM construction. This is the framework's solution to the CC hierarchy problem on this branch.

**Dark matter content.** Two complementary channels. F11 (KK gravitons as DM with $m_{KK} \sim 1$ meV, standard Dark Dimension picture); hairon-mediated bulk neutrino superfluidity (BCS Cooper pairs of bulk right-handed neutrinos at $T_c \sim$ meV, Scout 3 verified per arXiv:2604.26982).

**Strategic position (revised per Addendum A).** Path A's commitment to topologically stable positive-Λ minima protected by entropic suppression is one specific realization of the broader research program (including Vafa-lab work on Scherk-Schwarz critical points per Baykara-Chen-Vafa arXiv:2605.16484 and related publications) seeking critical points in the interior of M-theory moduli space. The dS swampland bound $|\nabla V|/V \geq 2/\sqrt{d-2}$ applies asymptotically at weak coupling and does not directly constrain Path A's interior-moduli-space commitments. The framework's specific contribution is the AM topological quantization mechanism plus the hairon-as-vacuum-substrate identification plus the entropic stability argument; this is a particular structural addition to the landscape, alongside Vafa-lab enhanced-gauge-symmetry constructions. The framework's most exposed empirical bet remains the static cosmic equation of state $w(z) = -1$ within the current epoch, falsifiable by DESI Y5 and Euclid.

**Falsification criteria.** DESI Y5 confirms evolving $w(z)$ at $\geq 5\sigma$ with CPL parameters inconsistent with $w \approx -1$; Euclid confirms time-evolving $w(z)$ at independent significance; independent gravitational-wave or large-scale-structure analyses confirm a dynamical dark sector at high significance. Any trigger transitions to Path B.

**Open sorries specific to Path A.** S-CC-002 (instanton-generated $z_0$ stabilization, active per RCRT, requires $b > 1/(4\pi^2)$ for $X_{F13}$ Pati-Salam on $dP_3$); S-CC-007 (hairon-vacuum entropic consistency, open). S-DE-001, S-DE-002, S-HT-001 all DEAD per Scouts 1, 4, 3 respectively (logged in exclusion reservoir).

## 6.4 Path B: Variable-Λ (Bedroya-Vafa-Aligned) Cosmology Branch

**Status as of v4.14:** Prepared contingency. Activated if Path A falsification criteria trigger.

**Commitments.** T3.6' (replacement for T3.6): $\Lambda$ is set geometrically by the Dark Dimension radius: $\Lambda \sim R^{-4}$ with $R \sim$ μm. The smallness of $\Lambda$ derives from $R$ being mesoscopic. F-DD-Evolve (replacement for F-CC): $R$ evolves cosmologically driven by slow-roll of a separate light modulus $\chi$ with $m_\chi \sim H_0 \sim 10^{-33}$ eV. $R(t)$ trajectory follows from $\chi(t)$ via $R(\chi)$ functional dependence (following Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu arXiv:2507.03090). Drop S-CC-005: No inter-sector tunneling protection needed because there is no discrete sector tower. $R$ is continuous. Hairon role redefined: Hairons remain as moduli of the $S^4/\mathbb{Z}_N$ instanton construction, but the static-vacuum identification is dropped. The BCS neutrino superfluid mechanism (Scout 3) may survive in modified form if the hairon condensation dynamics are compatible with the evolving background; requires explicit verification (S-DD-004).

**Cosmological prediction.** Evolving $\Lambda(t) \sim R(t)^{-4}$. Equation of state $w(z) \neq -1$ with thawing or freezing behavior depending on $V(\chi)$. Specific $w_0, w_a$ values match DESI DR2 thawing within the Bedroya-Vafa class.

**Solution to the cosmological constant problem.** $\Lambda$ smallness derives from $R$ being mesoscopic. The Dark Dimension's μm-scale radius gives the right order of magnitude without fine-tuning. The CC problem is solved geometrically rather than topologically.

**Dark matter content.** F11' (KK gravitons as DM with $m_{KK}(t) \sim 1/R(t)$, evolving cosmologically; DM mass evolution is a falsifiable prediction). Hairon BCS neutrino DM: status uncertain; requires verification that the hairon construction survives the dropping of the static-vacuum identification (S-DD-004).

**Strategic position (revised per Addendum A).** Aligned with the Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu evolving Dark Dimension construction (arXiv:2507.03090), one of two active research directions in current Vafa-lab cosmology phenomenology (the other being the enhanced-symmetry critical-point program of Baykara-Chen-Vafa arXiv:2605.16484). Path B's adoption would replace the AM topological quantization mechanism with continuous radius evolution while preserving the rest of the framework's bulk-brane structure.

**Open tasks specific to Path B.** S-DD-001 (light modulus identification): identify which modulus parameterizes $R(t)$ in the framework's specific F-theory geometry. Candidates: Kähler moduli of $dP_3$ base, axion-like fields from complex structure, or a new modulus added phenomenologically. S-DD-002 (modulus mass derivation): derive $m_\chi \sim H_0$ from first principles in the framework's geometric setup. Without a structural reason for $m_\chi \sim H_0$, the mechanism is phenomenologically tuned. S-DD-003 (DM mass evolution constraints): verify that the evolving $m_{KK}(t)$ is consistent with BBN, CMB, and structure-formation constraints. S-DD-004 (hairon role compatibility): verify whether the hairon BCS neutrino DM mechanism survives in the evolving-background context. If yes, retain F-hairon-DM. If no, fall back to F11' only. S-CC-002': $z_0$ stabilization mechanism in the absence of AM instanton potential. Need alternative stabilization (possibly KKLT-like flux stabilization, or a brane-localized superpotential).

**Falsification criteria.** DESI Y5 confirms static $\Lambda$ within experimental precision (reverts to Path A); specific Bedroya-Vafa predictions (DM mass evolution at percent level, $R$-evolution rate) inconsistent with structure-formation observations; failure to identify a structurally natural $m_\chi \sim H_0$ modulus.

## 6.5 Selection Criteria

**Primary empirical triggers (decisive).** DESI Y5 final $w(z)$ analysis at $\geq 5\sigma$ for evolving DE selects Path B; DESI Y5 final $w(z)$ consistent with $w = -1$ at $\geq 5\sigma$ retains Path A; Euclid DE constraints provide independent confirmation as secondary trigger.

**Secondary empirical triggers (informative).** Direct gravitational-wave constraints on dark energy equation of state from binary mergers and stochastic backgrounds; large-scale-structure constraints from LSST, Roman on $S_8$ tension and compatibility with each path; BBN and CMB constraints on $m_{KK}$ evolution (Path B's DM mass variation prediction).

**Theoretical pressure triggers (modifying).** Continued development of the Addazi-Meluccio program with new structural arguments or successful experimental tests strengthens Path A; new Swampland-program developments (refined dS conjecture, new no-go theorems, model-building constraints) strengthen Path B; resolution of contested string-theoretic stable de Sitter constructions (KKLT and variants) shifts the prior.

**Internal consistency triggers.** Path A internal failure (e.g., S-CC-002 cannot be discharged without violating S-CC-005, or AM mechanism turns out mathematically inconsistent); Path B internal failure (e.g., S-DD-001 cannot be discharged within the framework's existing F-theory geometry without contrived phenomenological additions).

**Default posture.** In the absence of decisive triggers, Path A is the current working hypothesis (consistent with v4.13 and prior versions). Path B remains a prepared contingency to be activated upon explicit empirical or theoretical trigger.

**Bayesian credence (per Addendum A).** Updated credence on Path A: roughly 25-40% (revised upward from rough 10-25% in light of Baykara-Chen-Vafa's demonstration that Vafa-lab is actively constructing interior-moduli-space critical points and the dS swampland bound does not directly constrain interior-moduli-space commitments). Path B: roughly 25-40%. Remaining mass (20-50%) on alternative resolutions of the cosmological tensions including possibility that DESI thawing is artifact of systematics that fade with deeper data.

## 6.6 Trellis Element Updates (Cross-Reference)

The full element-by-element updates from the v4.14 update module are integrated throughout the trellis as follows.

**Axiom reorganization.** §1.0 (Core Identity Statement, CC-1) added; §1.1-1.3 (Tiers 0-2) preserved unchanged; §1.5 T3.6 annotated branch-conditional, T3.6' added as Path B contingency; Tier 3 predictive functions split conceptually into 3.1 (matter-sector, branch-independent: F09, F11, F13, F19, F21) and 3.2 (cosmology-sector, branch-dependent), tracked in this update module §6.3-6.4 rather than re-numbered in §3 to avoid disruption to existing function tags.

**Cosmological-sector contraction shore (SF-DG-010).** Preserved unchanged at the structural level; the v4.14 reorganization is recorded as SF-DG-011 (this shore's companion), not as a rewrite of SF-DG-010.

**Sorry ledger updates.** S-DE-001, S-DE-002, S-HT-001 (all opened-and-discharged DEAD same shore); S-CC-002 retained branch-conditional active with the v4.13 sharpening preserved on both paths; S-CC-007 new Path A active; S-DD-001 through S-DD-004 and S-CC-002' new Path B dormant; S-AM-008 through S-AM-010 new active per Addendum A. All entries are recorded in Appendix D.

**Exclusion reservoir updates.** ER-DE-001 through ER-DE-006 and ER-HT-001 added per §5 above; ER-COSM-001 through ER-COSM-004 (v4.13 F12 kills) preserved.

**Linter rules (cross-reference).** LINT-CORE-1, LINT-DE-2, LINT-DE-3, LINT-PATH-1 added per §5 above. Existing rules preserved.

**Structural lessons (cross-reference).** SL-CORE-1, SL-CONT-1 (with Addendum A revision), SL-PATH-1 added per §5 above.

**Shore record.** SF-DG-011 added per §5 above (preceding this update module section).

**Corpus index.** New entries DG-CFT-055 through DG-CFT-060 added in Appendix E.

## 6.7 External Communication Implications

The framework's public positioning changes with this restructuring. Before v4.14, the framework was positioned as "static topologically-quantized cosmological constant via AM mechanism, with gravity-matter coupling via v(F_Q) as supporting machinery." After v4.14, the framework is positioned as "gravity coupled to coherent matter via state-dependent Higgs VEV with super-extensive Fisher-information scaling, with one of two cosmology-sector applications pending empirical resolution."

The new positioning leads with novel theoretical content rather than contrarian empirical bet. It is easier to engage with academically, harder to dismiss as a Swampland disagreement, and more accurate about what the framework's actual structural commitments are. The cosmology prediction remains sharp and falsifiable but is no longer the headline.

When publishing or presenting: the core paper foregrounds v(F_Q) physics and its compact-object / condensed-matter / LUNA predictions; cosmology appears as a downstream application section with explicit acknowledgment of the two-path contingency; the AM commitment is flagged as the framework's most exposed bet, with the Bedroya-Vafa fallback acknowledged as the prepared alternative.

**Per Addendum A.** The framework should be described publicly as a specific structural mechanism within the broader landscape of Vafa-lab research on M-theory moduli space critical points and Dark Dimension cosmology. The framework's two cosmology paths (Path A AM-locked; Path B Bedroya-Vafa evolving) mirror the two active directions in current Vafa-lab research (enhanced-symmetry critical points; evolving Dark Dimension). The framework's specific contributions are the AM topological quantization mechanism, the hairon-as-vacuum-substrate identification, the entropic stability argument, and the v(F_Q) / N² / modular F_Q matter-gravity coupling machinery. The framework is not contrarian relative to current Vafa-lab research; it is one structurally specific position within the program.

This restructuring is not a retreat from the static-Λ prediction. The prediction stands as the framework's current working hypothesis on Path A. The restructuring is a clarification of where the prediction's load-bearing weight lives in the framework's overall structure, and a preparation for the empirical resolution without panic-restructuring.

## 6.8 Open Questions and Next Moves

**Branch-independent open tasks.** Discharge S-CC-002 via $X_{F13}$ RG running computation (priority 1, applies to both paths); strengthen F13.2 LUNA empirical anchor via additional experimental contact; develop F19 wavefunction collapse predictions for testable mesoscopic systems; complete the v(F_Q) compact-object thermodynamics for F09 predictions.

**Path A maintenance tasks.** S-CC-007 hairon-vacuum entropic consistency; falsification watch on DESI DR3 and beyond; track Addazi-Meluccio program developments; investigate S-AM-008 (anomaly cancellation compatibility against Baykara-Chen-Vafa Appendix A.3 conditions); document S-AM-009 (sign of V at AM minimum); pursue S-AM-010 (d=4 critical point comparison).

**Path B preparation tasks.** S-DD-001 through S-DD-004 to discharge-ready state; identify candidate light modulus in F-theory $dP_3$ + $X_{F13}$ geometry; build the Bedroya-Vafa-Wu compatibility map for the framework's existing structure.

**Strategic watch list.** DESI DR3 (~2027); DESI Y5 final (~2028-2029); Euclid DE cosmology results (~2027 onward); continued Addazi-Meluccio program publications; continued Swampland conjecture refinements and counter-arguments; continued Vafa-lab interior-moduli-space and evolving-Dark-Dimension publications.

# 6.A ADDENDUM A: REPOSITIONING VS VAFA-LAB RESEARCH

**Target:** v4.14 update module (§6 above)
**Update type:** Strategic positioning revision; no axiom changes, no path commitment changes
**Date:** May 19, 2026
**Triggered by:** Baykara-Chen-Vafa arXiv:2605.16484v1 (May 15, 2026), "Isolated Critical Points for Scherk-Schwarz Compactifications of M-theory"

## 6.A.1 Motivation

The v4.14 update module as drafted positions the framework's static-Λ commitment as taking the minority side of an active string phenomenology debate, in tension with Vafa's de Sitter swampland conjecture. This framing was constructed against the strong form of the dS swampland conjecture (Obied-Ooguri-Spodyneiko-Vafa 2018, arXiv:1806.08362), which forbids critical points of $V > 0$ generically.

The Baykara-Chen-Vafa paper (arXiv:2605.16484, May 15, 2026) makes explicit that the dS swampland bound $|\nabla V|/V \geq 2/\sqrt{d-2}$ applies "asymptotically at weak coupling" only. The Vafa-lab itself is now actively constructing isolated critical points of $V$ in the interior of moduli space using enhanced gauge symmetry from duality groups. The paper finds explicit critical points in d = 8, 6, 5, 4 (with a no-go result in d = 7). The sign of $V$ at these critical points cannot be determined by the symmetry argument, so V > 0 (dS-like) is not ruled out.

This is the same kind of "critical points exist in the interior of moduli space" research that the framework's AM mechanism realizes through a different specific structural mechanism (topological quantization rather than enhanced gauge symmetry). The framework and Vafa-lab operate in the same research program, not in opposition.

The addendum revises the v4.14 update module's strategic positioning language without changing any axiom, sorry, linter rule, path commitment, or selection criterion. The two-path structure remains valid. The dependency map remains valid. What changes is how the framework's external positioning is described.

## 6.A.2 Key Findings of arXiv:2605.16484 Relevant to Framework

**Refined dS swampland bound domain.** The paper's Eq. (1.1) gives the swampland bound $|\nabla V|/V \geq 2/\sqrt{d-2}$ as applying "asymptotically at weak coupling." The interior of moduli space, where Planck-scale couplings dominate, is explicitly outside the bound's domain. The framework's static-Λ commitment lives in the interior (the AM minimum is a Planck-scale topological selection), not at asymptotic weak coupling. The swampland bound therefore does not directly constrain the framework's Path A.

**Active critical-point construction.** The paper uses unbroken U-duality subgroups (after Scherk-Schwarz spin-structure modification) to find points in moduli space where enhanced gauge symmetry forces $\nabla V = 0$. These are isolated critical points of $V$ in the interior of moduli space. Found in d = 4, 5, 6, 8; ruled out in d = 7. The framework's d = 4 effective theory lives in a regime where such critical points exist by the paper's own analysis. The Vafa-lab is therefore not arguing against critical points; it is constructing them. The framework's contribution is a specific mechanism (AM topological quantization with hairon-as-vacuum-substrate) for producing critical points, alongside the Vafa-lab's enhanced-gauge-symmetry mechanism. Multiple mechanisms can coexist in the same theoretical landscape.

**Sign of V undetermined.** The paper explicitly states (Section 1): "We cannot determine the sign of V at these critical points." This is structurally important. The Vafa-lab is finding critical points without determining whether they are local minima, saddle points, or maxima, and without determining whether V > 0 (dS-like) or V < 0 (AdS-like) or V = 0 (Minkowski-like). The framework's commitment to stable V > 0 minima protected by entropic suppression is a specific additional commitment that the Vafa-lab analysis does not contradict, but also does not establish; the question of $V > 0$ at the AM minimum is formalized as S-AM-009.

**Duality-covariant anomaly cancellation condition.** The paper introduces (Sections 2-5, Appendix A) a duality-covariant anomaly cancellation condition for M-theory orbifolded by discrete $\mathbb{Z}_N$ symmetries acting as phases on the charge lattice. This generalizes the perturbative string level-matching requirement. Explicit quadratic equations are given for each dimension (paper's Table 3 and Appendix A.3). This is technically relevant to the framework's commitments. The hairon construction (Addazi-Meluccio arXiv:2604.26982) involves $S^4/\mathbb{Z}_N$ orbifolding with $N \sim 10^{120}$. While the framework's gravitational instanton orbifold is structurally different from M-theory toroidal compactification, the underlying anomaly-cancellation logic for $\mathbb{Z}_N$ phase shifts on charge lattices may be portable. This generates the new open task S-AM-008.

**Reference [7] is Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu 2507.03090.** The paper explicitly cites the evolving Dark Dimension scenario as reference [7], demonstrating that the Vafa-lab is simultaneously developing critical-point construction (this paper) and evolving-DE constructions (the cited paper). The Vafa-lab research is exploring both directions, validating the framework's two-path structure as mirroring real research-frontier ambiguity rather than picking sides.

## 6.A.3 Revisions Applied to v4.14 Update Module

The Path A strategic position (§6.3 above), the Path B strategic position (§6.4 above), the structural lesson SL-CONT-1 (§5), and the external communication implications (§6.7) have been revised in place per the Addendum A textual replacements. The Bayesian credence note has been added to §6.5. No axiom is changed; no path commitment is changed; no selection criterion is changed.

## 6.A.4 New Open Tasks Generated by Addendum

**S-AM-008 (Anomaly Cancellation Compatibility, active, Path A specific).** Verify whether the hairon construction's $S^4/\mathbb{Z}_N$ orbifold (Addazi-Meluccio arXiv:2604.26982) satisfies the duality-covariant anomaly cancellation condition introduced in Baykara-Chen-Vafa arXiv:2605.16484. The Baykara-Chen-Vafa condition is formulated for M-theory toroidal compactifications; portability to gravitational instanton backgrounds requires evaluation. If satisfied, Path A gains structural credibility from passing a current Vafa-lab consistency condition. If not satisfied, the hairon construction has a technical concern that needs addressing (either modification, non-portability of the condition, or a deeper structural problem). Method: apply the quadratic equations from arXiv:2605.16484 Appendix A.3 to the hairon $\mathbb{Z}_N$ phase shift acting on the M-theory charge lattice. Determine whether the hairon configuration satisfies the conditions. Technical computation that could be done analytically or numerically. Priority: moderate. Not blocking but informative for Path A credibility.

**S-AM-009 (Sign of V at AM Minimum, active, formalized by addendum).** The framework's Path A assumes that the AM minimum has $V > 0$ (positive cosmological constant). Baykara-Chen-Vafa note explicitly that their critical-point construction cannot determine the sign of V. The framework's argument for V > 0 at the AM minimum should be explicitly documented and verified, not assumed. Method: trace through the AM construction (Addazi-Meluccio arXiv:2602.16840) and establish whether the topologically selected sector has V > 0 by structural argument or by additional assumption. If by structural argument, document. If by assumption, flag as a Path-A-specific commitment. Priority: moderate. The current Path A relies on V > 0 at the AM minimum to match observation; this needs to be established structurally rather than assumed.

**S-AM-010 (d=4 Critical Point Comparison, active, comparative analysis task).** Baykara-Chen-Vafa find a specific isolated critical point in d=4 at the $A^7_1$ lattice point with $T^7$ orthogonal at self-dual radii and $C_{ijk} = 1$ on basic 3-cycles, with anti-periodic boundary conditions on the diagonal direction. Determine the structural relationship between this Vafa-lab critical point and the framework's d=4 effective theory critical point selected by the AM mechanism. Possibilities: (a) they are the same critical point in different language (framework and Vafa-lab converge on the same physics through different theoretical pathways); (b) they are different critical points (framework's AM mechanism produces a structurally distinct critical point from the Vafa-lab construction); (c) the framework's Karch-Randall setup is structurally incompatible with the Vafa-lab Scherk-Schwarz construction (they live in different regions of moduli space). Method: identify the moduli of the Karch-Randall + AM construction in M-theory-on-$T^7$ language. Compare to the $(A^7_1, v_1)$ critical point of Baykara-Chen-Vafa. Priority: moderate. Could illuminate whether framework's Path A is technically aligned with or distinct from Vafa-lab d=4 critical-point analysis.

## 6.A.5 Summary

The framework's static-Λ commitment via the AM mechanism is one specific position within the active Vafa-lab research program on M-theory moduli space critical points. The framework is not in opposition to Vafa's program; it is one realization of one branch within it. The other branch (Bedroya-Obied-Vafa-Wu evolving Dark Dimension) is the framework's Path B contingency. Both branches are real research directions in current string phenomenology.

The framework's exposure to falsification is unchanged: DESI Y5 + Euclid will determine whether $w(z) = -1$ holds within current observational precision. If yes, Path A is empirically vindicated; if no, Path B activates. The framework remains a sharp falsifiable structural commitment. What is updated is the surrounding narrative: the framework is no longer described as contrarian relative to Vafa's program, only as a specific position within it.

This is a more accurate description of the framework's actual structural position and a more credible external presentation. No theoretical content is revised. The framework's claims and predictions remain as they were in v4.14. The strategic positioning becomes honest about the framework's relationship to current string phenomenology research.
